### [231] [DiffSlack: Learning under Nonlinear Inequality Constraints via Learnable Slack Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05247)
*Ziqian Wang,Chenxi Fang,Zhen Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DiffSlack 是一种新型可微投影层，通过将不等式约束转化为含松弛变量的等式约束，实现了神经网络输出对复杂非线性约束的硬性满足，在路径规划等工程任务中表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在神经网络中强制执行复杂的非线性不等式约束（如路径规划中的避障、曲率限制等）存在困难，现有方法要么限制约束集合结构，要么在大规模问题上计算开销过大，难以满足工程需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为 DiffSlack 的可微投影层。该方法通过引入可学习的松弛变量将不等式约束转化为等式约束，利用阻尼高斯-牛顿法进行投影，并将松弛变量的预测值作为投影的预热起点；此外，引入了两阶段课程学习策略以增强训练稳定性。

Result: 在包含200个非线性约束的车辆路径规划任务中，DiffSlack 相比现有基线方法在规划成功率和几何约束满足度上表现更优；通过 CARLA 仿真和真实车辆实验，证明了该方法在生成可执行轨迹方面的有效性。

Conclusion: DiffSlack 为在神经网络中嵌入复杂非线性不等式约束提供了一种实用、可扩展的解决方案，能够确保预测结果严格满足工程应用中的几何约束要求，并提升了训练的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Enforcing nonlinear inequality constraints in neural networks remains challenging, especially when the output is subject to many coupled constraints. Existing hard constraint methods often impose structural restrictions on the constraint set or introduce substantial computational overhead for large-scale nonlinear problems. Here, we propose DiffSlack, a differentiable projection layer for nonlinear inequality-constrained neural prediction. DiffSlack reformulates inequalities as equalities with learnable slack variables, which are predicted as part of the augmented network output and provide a data-driven warm start for damped Gauss-Newton projection. The projection layer maps raw predictions onto the augmented feasible manifold while preserving end-to-end differentiability. A two-stage curriculum further stabilizes training and improves constraint satisfaction. We evaluate DiffSlack on vehicle path planning with 200 nonlinear inequality constraints from collision avoidance, curvature limits, and waypoint spacing. Compared with existing learning-based baselines, DiffSlack achieves a higher planning success rate and stronger geometric constraint satisfaction under a comparable inference budget. Ablation studies further show that the hard projection layer reduces sensitivity to supervision quality. Closed-loop tracking in CARLA and real-world vehicle experiments confirms the executability of the generated trajectories. These results demonstrate that DiffSlack provides a practical and scalable approach to embedding hard inequality constraints into neural networks for engineering applications.

### [232] [Alpha-RTL: Test-Time Training for RTL Hardware Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05253)
*Peilong Zhou,Zhirong Chen,Cangyuan Li,Haoyu Gao,Kaiyan Chang,Ziming Qu,Ying Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TTT-RTL 是一种针对 RTL 设计的新型测试时强化学习框架，它通过闭环 EDA 反馈实时更新 LLM 策略，成功将硬件生成从功能实现推向了高性能的物理优化阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大多数 LLM 硬件生成方法（如 RTLLM）主要依赖预训练模型或冻结策略进行搜索，难以针对具体的硬件设计需求进行深度优化。为了弥补 LLM 从“功能正确”到“物理优化”的鸿沟，研究者旨在通过测试时训练（TTT）将 LLM 策略与 EDA 工具链形成闭环，实现对特定硬件任务的实时调优。

Method: 提出 TTT-RTL 框架，在测试阶段对 LLM 进行强化学习。核心组件包括：1. 采样候选实现并进行语法/仿真验证；2. 利用综合后的 PPA（功耗、性能、面积）作为奖励；3. 使用 PUCT 索引的设计状态池复用高分变体；4. 引入自适应 KL 预算控制器，根据参考 KL、有效样本量和奖励饱和信号调整熵约束，以稳定策略更新。

Result: TTT-RTL 在 RTLLM v2.0 基准测试中将 PPA 乘积降低了 65.1%，比现有的冻结策略智能体高出 26.1%。在工业级 XuanTie C910 FPU 设计中，实现了 59.4% 的面积-延迟-功耗（ADP）降低。实验证明，策略自适应、状态复用和 KL 预算控制对提升性能均有显著贡献。

Conclusion: 测试时训练（Test-Time Training）是超越单纯功能正确性、实现硬件物理优化的有效路径。通过闭环反馈机制，LLM 能够根据特定硬件设计任务动态调整自身策略，从而显著提升生成代码的质量（PPA 指标）。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown increasing promise in generating
  functionally correct register-transfer-level (RTL) hardware designs.
  Recent systems improve further through EDA-integrated reinforcement
  learning with syntax, simulation, and PPA rewards, but train a general
  RTL generator before deployment while test-time approaches search with
  a frozen policy. We instead perform reinforcement learning at test time,
  allowing the LLM policy to adapt to executable EDA feedback for the
  specific RTL problem at hand. We propose TTT-RTL, to our knowledge the
  first per-design test-time training framework that closes the loop
  between an LLM policy and an EDA pipeline for RTL optimization. TTT-RTL
  samples candidate implementations, verifies them through syntax checking
  and simulation, scores valid designs using synthesis-derived PPA product,
  reuses high-reward variants through a PUCT-indexed design-state pool,
  and updates the policy with an entropic policy-gradient objective. To
  stabilize policy updates under sparse or plateaued rewards, we introduce
  an adaptive KL-budget controller that adjusts the entropy constraint
  using reference KL, effective sample size, and reward saturation signals.
  On RTLLM v2.0 under Nangate 45nm, TTT-RTL reduces the geometric-mean
  PPA product by 65.1% over the reference, outperforming the strongest
  published frozen-policy agent baseline at 26.1%. On an industrial
  XuanTie C910 FPU leading-zero-anticipation unit under Sky130, TTT-RTL
  achieves a 59.4% ADP reduction, and ablations confirm that policy
  adaptation, state reuse, and KL-budget control each contribute. These
  results suggest that test-time training with executable EDA feedback can
  move LLM-based RTL generation beyond functional correctness toward
  physically optimized hardware.

</details>


### [233] [MolE-RAG: Molecular Structure-Enhanced Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Chemistry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05693)
*Joey Chan,Wonbin Kweon,Ashley Shin,Niharika Bhattacharjee,Pengcheng Jiang,Yue Guo,Jiawei Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MolE-RAG 是一种无需微调的检索增强框架，通过引入化学文献、分子属性描述和相似分子结构等上下文信息，显著增强了大语言模型在分子属性预测任务中的推理能力和预测精度。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MolE-RAG 的训练无关（training-free）的分子中心检索增强生成框架。该方法在推理阶段为每个分子查询补充三种互补的上下文信息：1. 相关的化学文献；2. 分子特异性信息（如同义词、标识符、功能基团注释及物化描述符）；3. 从训练集中检索到的结构相似分子。

Result: 在九项分子属性预测任务中，MolE-RAG 显著提升了表现。与仅使用 SMILES 的基准相比，在通用大模型上，分类任务的 ROC-AUC 最高提升了 28 个百分点，回归任务的 RMSE 最高降低了 67%。实验发现不同模型对三种上下文来源的依赖程度各异。

Conclusion: MolE-RAG 证明了通过无需训练的检索增强生成（RAG）框架，能够有效填补大语言模型在化学结构理解与自然语言推理之间的语义鸿沟，为分子属性预测提供了一种灵活且高效的集成异构化学知识的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown promise for molecular property prediction, but their ability to reason over chemical structures remains limited, as molecular representations such as SMILES differ substantially from the natural language on which LLMs are primarily trained. To bridge this semantic and chemical knowledge gap, we propose MolE-RAG, a training-free, molecule-centric retrieval-augmented generation framework for LLM-based molecular property prediction. MolE-RAG augments each prediction with three complementary sources of inference-time context: retrieved chemistry literature, molecule-specific information including compound synonyms, identifiers, functional group annotations, and physicochemical descriptors, and structurally similar molecules retrieved from the training set. We evaluate MolE-RAG across nine molecular property prediction tasks using proprietary, chemistry-specialized, and open-source LLMs. Across general-purpose LLMs, MolE-RAG improves ROC-AUC by up to 28 percentage points on classification tasks and reduces regression RMSE by up to 67% relative to a SMILES-only baseline. We further find that the utility of each context source varies across models and tasks, with different models benefiting most from textual retrieval, molecular context, or structural retrieval. These results suggest that molecule-centric retrieval can improve LLM-based molecular property prediction without model fine-tuning while providing a flexible framework for integrating heterogeneous chemical knowledge at inference time.

### [234] [Flash-WAM: Modality-Aware Distillation for World Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05254)
*Arman Akbari,Ci Zhang,Arash Akbari,Lin Zhao,Yixiao Chen,Weiwei Chen,Xuan Zhang,Geng Yuan,Yanzhi Wang*

TL;DR: Flash-WAM 是一种模态感知的步进蒸馏框架，旨在解决世界动作模型（WAMs）推理慢的问题，通过为视频和动作设置不同的噪声参数，实现了高质量的单步实时机器人控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 世界动作模型（WAMs）虽在操作基准上表现优异，但因需要多步去噪而无法实现实时控制。现有的蒸馏方法无法处理视频流和动作流之间不同的信噪比偏移和边际噪声分布不对称问题。

Method: 提出 Flash-WAM 框架，采用模态感知步进蒸馏方法。针对动作流采用线性梯度缩放参数化以匹配其低噪声机制，针对视频流采用方差保持参数化以匹配其高噪声机制，从而实现单步生成。

Result: 将推理速度提升了 23 倍，延迟从 8.1 秒降至 348 毫秒，实现了实时控制。同时，在仿真和真实机器人环境（Unitree G1）中保持了极高的任务成功率，显著优于传统的蒸馏方法。

Conclusion: Flash-WAM 证明了通过模态感知的蒸馏策略，可以有效地克服视频-动作联合生成模型在推理速度上的瓶颈，实现高质量的实时机器人控制。

Abstract: World-action models (WAMs) jointly generate future video and robot actions through iterative diffusion, achieving strong performance on manipulation benchmarks but requiring tens of denoising steps, a cost that precludes real-time control. Step distillation has emerged as the natural remedy, but off-the-shelf methods break down in the joint video-action setting because video and action streams use different SNR-shifted noise schedules and reach training with substantially different marginal noise distributions, an asymmetry that single-modality distillation methods cannot accommodate. We introduce \textbf{Flash-WAM}, a modality-aware step-distillation framework inspired by consistency distillation that selects the consistency function for each modality to match its noise regime: a linear-gradient-scaling parametrization for the action stream's low-noise regime, paired with a variance-preserving parametrization for the video stream's high-noise regime, grounded in a structural analysis of the consistency-function family that characterizes the achievable gradient scaling under the consistency boundary condition. Instantiated on LingBot-VA, Flash-WAM compresses inference to a single step in each modality. On RoboTwin 2.0, this reduces per-chunk latency from $8.1$ seconds to $348$ ms on NVIDIA L40S, a $23{\times}$ speedup that enables real-time inference. Flash-WAM preserves task success on simulation benchmarks ($85.5\%$ RoboTwin 2.0, $95.7\%$ LIBERO) and substantially recovers real-world performance ($60\%$ average on a Unitree G1 humanoid robot), while naive consistency distillation drops to $24\%$ at the same step budget.

### [235] [Policy-Conditioned Counterfactual Credit for Verifiable Reinforcement Learning of Long-Horizon Language Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05263)
*Renwei Meng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对长程语言智能体在强化学习中产生的幻觉和捷径行为，本文提出 CVT-RL 算法，通过反事实贡献估计和约束优化，实现了更精准的奖励评估与行为控制，显著提升了任务成功率与推理的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习奖励机制多基于相关性（correlational），难以判断推理步骤是否真正对最终成功有贡献，导致长程任务中的智能体容易产生“捷径行为”（shortcut actions）、幻觉及证据链断裂。

Method: 提出了 CVT-RL 算法，核心包含三个组件：1. 密集可验证奖励机制；2. 干预有效性门控（Intervention-validity gating）；3. 策略条件反事实贡献（PCCC）估计器。利用多种受控干预（如删除、语义替换等）结合增强拉格朗日乘子法，对推理过程中的证据链、工具使用及安全性进行严格约束。

Result: 在长文本问答、ALFWorld、ScienceWorld 等任务中，CVT-RL 的任务成功率提升至 78.9%，证据 F1 值提升至 82.8%，并将“黑客”行为（hacking）比例显著降低，在应对针对性规避攻击时表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入反事实归因和显式约束，有效解决了长程语言智能体在推理和工具使用中的幻觉、信念漂移及捷径行为问题，为构建更可靠、更具鲁棒性的智能体提供了一种可验证的强化学习路径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards improves reasoning and tool use, yet long-horizon language agents still learn unsupported evidence chains, belief drift, and shortcut actions that satisfy terminal checks. Existing process rewards are mostly correlational: they reward retrieval-, reflection-, or verification-like steps without estimating whether the step contributes to final verified success under a specified intervention. We propose CVT-RL, a constrained policy-gradient algorithm with dense verifiable rewards, intervention-validity gating, and a policy-conditioned counterfactual contribution (PCCC) estimator. Deletion, semantic substitution, evidence substitution, and tool-output perturbation define separate controlled interventions; continuations are sampled from a frozen reference policy, and a selection-adjusted doubly robust estimator augments the advantage. Belief control uses only prefix-observable labels, while an augmented Lagrangian constrains unsupported claims, skipped verification, tool tampering, and unsafe calls. On long-context QA, ALFWorld, ScienceWorld, and web/tool tasks, CVT-RL improves average task success from 71.8% for compute-matched non-causal RL and 75.4% for an information-matched counterfactual-process baseline to 78.9%, improves evidence F1 from 78.9 to 82.8 over the information-matched baseline, and reduces measured hacking from 7.2% to 3.9%. Independent human audit estimates 4.6% hacking for CVT-RL versus 8.1% for the information-matched baseline, and adaptive detector-evasion attacks raise hacking only to 7.1%. Stratified bootstrap and mixed-effects tests give p<0.01 after Holm correction for all primary metrics. Carefully scoped counterfactual credit, paired with validity gating, diagnostics, and verifiable constraints, provides a reproducible route toward more reliable long-horizon RL for language agents.

### [236] [REGEN: Reference-Guided Synthetic Multivariate Time Series Generation for Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05264)
*Moulik Gupta,Dhruv Kumar,Murari Mandal,Saurabh Deshpande*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ReGeN 是一种创新的时间序列生成框架，它将参考数据视为“结构脚手架”而非简单的模仿对象，通过显式分解周期性、随机残差和变量关联，实现了在小样本场景下高质量、可控的时间序列数据合成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时间序列生成方法存在局限性：基于先验的方法生成样本缺乏领域针对性，而基于数据驱动的方法（如 TimeGAN）将参考序列视为黑盒，难以显式控制周期结构、局部变异和变量间关系，导致模型在处理低数据量、多变量时间序列时难以保证生成数据的质量与可用性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ReGeN 的参考引导生成流水线。该方法不直接模仿参考序列，而是将其解构为三个可解释组件：1. 用于捕获周期性骨架的相位对齐组件；2. 采用深度核高斯过程建模的变量级随机残差；3. 通过结构因果模型注入的滞后感知跨变量依赖关系。通过在这些组件上进行可控温度采样，实现领域结构与分布扩展的平衡。

Result: 实验表明，ReGeN 生成的数据在替代真实数据时仅产生极小的预测性能损失；在强周期性领域（如交通流量预测）中，其生成数据甚至能比真实源数据达到更好的预测效果。此外，使用 ReGeN 生成语料库预训练的基础模型在表现上显著优于使用先验模型或传统数据驱动模型生成的数据。

Conclusion: 在低数据量场景下，通过结构化方式利用参考数据比单纯追求数据量更为关键。ReGeN 通过将参考序列分解为可控的结构组件，有效缓解了现有生成模型在保持领域结构与扩展性之间的权衡难题。

Abstract: Training robust multivariate time series forecasting models requires large, diverse corpora, yet many real-world domains provide only a handful of observed sequences. Existing generators fail to resolve this mismatch: prior-based approaches (e.g., CauKer, TimePFN) produce domain-agnostic samples, while data-driven methods (e.g., TimeGAN) treat references as black-box supervision, forfeiting explicit control over periodic structure, local variability, and cross-variable dynamics.
  We propose ReGeN, a reference-guided generative pipeline that treats observed sequences not as examples to imitate, but as structural scaffolds for controllable synthesis. ReGeN decomposes each reference into three interpretable components: a phase-aligned periodic backbone capturing dominant domain morphology; per-variable stochastic residuals modeled with a deep-kernel Gaussian process; and lag-aware cross-variable dependencies injected through a structural causal model with fitted coupling coefficients. Sampling these components at controllable temperature broadens distributional coverage while preserving domain-grounded structure.
  We show that ReGeN-generated data consistently substitutes for real sibling data with minimal forecasting degradation, and in strongly periodic domains such as traffic, can outperform the real source itself. We further show that a foundation model pretrained on ReGeN corpora outperforms those pretrained on prior-based and data-driven synthetic alternatives. This suggests that in low-data regimes, how reference data is structurally exploited can matter as much as how much data is available.

The resulting testing threshold coincides, down to the sharp constant, with the known low-degree recovery threshold. In contrast, the task of weak testing, where the goal is to outperform random guessing, does not have a sharp threshold but rather a smooth transition, which we identify. ### [239] [Learning Manifold and Itô Dynamics with Branched Neural Rough Differential Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05272)
*Luke Thompson,Dai Shi,Lequan Lin,Junbin Gao,Andi Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文引入了分支神经粗糙微分方程（B-NRDEs），通过霍普夫代数框架扩展了NRDE，使其能够处理Itô演算及流形约束动力学，显著提升了在复杂随机系统预测中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经粗糙微分方程（NRDEs）基于洗牌代数，仅适用于Stratonovich演算，无法有效处理Itô动力学所需的二次变分项，也无法在带连接的流形上处理有序协变导数，这限制了其在更广泛的随机动力学建模中的应用。

Method: B-NRDEs 利用不同的霍普夫代数结构（如Grossman-Larson树、Munthe-Kaas-Wright平面树）来匹配特定的演算需求（如Itô动力学或流形上的协变导数），将传统的NRDE对数-ODE步骤重构为状态空间流形上的几何数值积分，并引入了分支签名核目标函数以实现Itô一致的分布匹配。

Result: 在粗糙Bergomi波动率建模、SO(3)动力学预测及SPD协方差动力学等任务中，B-NRDEs展现了超越传统欧几里得-Stratonovich设置的建模能力，能够更准确地捕捉随机特征并保持流形约束。

Conclusion: 本文提出的分支神经粗糙微分方程（B-NRDEs）通过霍普夫代数（Hopf-algebraic）框架统一了不同演算下的动力学建模，不仅提升了对Itô动力学和流形约束的处理能力，还通过分支签名核优化目标实现了更稳健的训练，为处理复杂随机和流形值动力学提供了一种通用且高效的方案。

Abstract: Neural rough differential equations (NRDEs) stay accurate under irregular sampling while taking far fewer integration steps than standard neural differential equations, summarising a finely sampled driver by its log-signature and advancing the hidden state over coarse intervals using the log-ODE method. This efficiency rests on the shuffle algebra, the algebraic counterpart of Stratonovich calculus. This reliance means NRDEs cannot expose the quadratic-variation terms Itô dynamics require, nor the ordered covariant derivatives that govern Itô flows on connection-equipped manifolds. Ameliorating this, we introduce Branched Neural Rough Differential Equations (B-NRDEs), a Hopf-algebraic framework that recasts the NRDE log-ODE step as geometric numerical integration on the state-space manifold, matching the driving algebra to the governing calculus: Grossman--Larson rooted trees for Euclidean Itô dynamics, Munthe-Kaas--Wright planar rooted trees for ordered covariant derivatives on manifolds, and the shuffle algebra in the classical Stratonovich case. This yields intrinsic coarse-step dynamics that exactly preserve manifold constraints. Finally, we introduce a branched signature-kernel objective to enable Itô-consistent law matching by making quadratic-variation terms visible during training. On rough Bergomi volatility, sim-to-real $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ dynamics forecasting, and SPD covariance dynamics, B-NRDEs offer a unified, effective approach to stochastic and manifold-valued dynamics beyond the Euclidean--Stratonovich setting.

</details>


### [240] [Anomaly Detection for Electro-Hydrostatic Actuators using LSTM Autoencoder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05274)
*Nehal Afifi,Abdelmonem Elhendawi,Felix Leitenberger,Nadine Piat,Sven Matthiesen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于长短期记忆网络（LSTM）自编码器的重构异常检测框架。通过在受控实验台上采集的温度和压力单变量信号进行训练，利用验证集的重构误差分布设定阈值，并针对多种故障注入场景进行性能评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，该模型平均准确率达到99.0%，最高精度达100%，召回率在90.2%至99.6%之间，F1分数在93.1%至99.8%之间，证明了该方法在不同传感器下具有高灵敏度和极低的误报率。

Abstract: Electro-Hydrostatic Actuators (EHAs) are widely used in aerospace and industrial systems, where timely detection of sensor anomalies is essential to ensure safe and reliable operation. However, the large volume and high sampling frequency of EHA sensor data pose challenges for accurate and efficient anomaly detection. Conventional statistical and classical machine-learning methods such as Z-score, Interquartile Range (IQR), Median Absolute Deviation (MAD), Isolation Forest, Gaussian Mixture, and k-means often fail to capture the temporal dependencies inherent in EHA signals, resulting in limited detection accuracy and elevated false-alarm rates. Furthermore, systematic evaluations of data-driven anomaly detection approaches for EHA systems remain scarce, particularly under varying operational conditions. This study presents an offline anomaly-detection framework for univariate EHA sensor signals, focusing on temperature and pressure data collected from a controlled test bench. The method employs a reconstruction-based Long Short-Term Memory (LSTM) autoencoder, calibrated and evaluated using validation-set reconstruction-error distributions. Performance is assessed across multiple fault-injection scenarios using accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score, complemented by sensitivity analyses under varying operating conditions. The LSTM autoencoder achieved an average accuracy of 99.0\%, precision up to 100\%, recall between 90.2\% and 99.6\%, and F1-scores from 93.1\% to 99.8\%, demonstrating high detection sensitivity and a very low false-alarm rate across all evaluated sensors. These results highlight the feasibility of data-driven offline anomaly detection for EHAs. Future work will focus on adapting the developed framework for an online (real-time) environment.

### [241] [Agentic Monte Carlo: Simulating Reinforcement Learning for Black-Box Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05296)
*Dae Yon Hwang,Raunaq Suri,Valentin Villecroze,Anthony L. Caterini,Jesse C. Cresswell,Noël Vouitsis,Brendan Leigh Ross*

TL;DR: 本文提出“代理蒙特卡洛”（AMC）方法，通过序列蒙特卡洛采样在测试时对黑盒 LLM 代理进行优化，实现了无需模型微调的强化学习效果，显著提升了代理在复杂环境中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习方法通常依赖于模型参数的调整，这在只能通过 API 访问的黑盒大语言模型（LLM）代理上无法实现。因此，作者旨在寻找一种无需修改黑盒模型权重、仅通过测试时推理优化即可提升代理性能的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为“代理蒙特卡洛”（Agentic Monte Carlo, AMC）的方法。该方法基于强化学习与贝叶斯推理的等价性，将最优策略视为轨迹的后验概率。通过序列蒙特卡洛（Sequential Monte Carlo）采样，利用学习到的价值函数在测试时引导黑盒 LLM，从而在不修改模型参数的前提下实现策略优化。

Result: 在 AgentGym 基准测试的三个不同环境中，AMC 显著优于传统的提示词（prompting）基线方法；随着测试时计算资源的增加，其性能甚至超过了基于参数优化的群相对策略优化（GRPO）方法。

Conclusion: AMC 证明了在不改变黑盒模型参数的情况下，通过序列蒙特卡洛方法进行原则性的强化学习式优化是可行且高效的。这种方法为无法进行参数微调的闭源 LLM 代理提供了强有力的性能提升手段。

Abstract: LLM agents operate in two distinct regimes: open-weight agents amenable to reinforcement learning (RL) and black-box agents whose behaviour must be controlled purely at test time. Although black-box agents are often backed by state-of-the-art proprietary LLMs, API-only access precludes parameter-level optimization, rendering most RL methods inapplicable. To address this limitation, we turn to a known equivalence between RL and Bayesian inference. We propose Agentic Monte Carlo (AMC) to directly sample from the optimal policy of a black-box agent rather than training it through RL. The optimal policy is a posterior over trajectories whose prior we define as the fixed black-box LLM agent. We employ Sequential Monte Carlo to sample from this posterior by learning a value function to steer the agent while leaving the underlying black-box model unchanged. We validate AMC on three diverse environments from the AgentGym benchmark, demonstrating significant improvements over prompting baselines and even outperforming Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) as we scale the test-time compute of our method. AMC demonstrates the feasibility of performing principled RL-style optimization of black-box LLM agents. Code is available at https://github.com/layer6ai-labs/Agentic-Monte-Carlo

### [242] [Multimarginal flow matching with optimal transport potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05327)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的流匹配（FM）主要用于学习两个端点分布之间的动态传输，但在处理科学领域常见的、具有多个中间观测边际分布的动态系统时，缺乏有效的约束机制。该研究旨在利用这些中间分布信息来更好地建模系统的时空演化。

Method: 作者提出了一种称为“OT-potential FM (OTP-FM)”的算法。该方法利用流匹配与动态最优传输（OT）之间的联系，通过在动态OT作用量中引入势函数（potentials），将流软约束在中间边际分布上，从而扩展了传统的条件流匹配学习目标，实现了无需模拟的训练过程。

Result: OTP-FM 在单细胞RNA测序、海洋学及气象学等多样化数据集上表现出优于现有算法的性能，且在训练效率上具有显著优势，能够灵活地建模复杂的时空动态。

Conclusion: OTP-FM 提供了一种高效且灵活的框架，通过引入动态最优传输势函数，成功解决了多边际流匹配问题，在处理具有时间演化特征的复杂科学数据任务中表现出优越性。

Abstract: Flow matching (FM) has emerged as a powerful framework for learning dynamic transport maps between two empirical distributions. However, less explored is the setting with intermediate observed marginals that can help constrain the flows between the endpoints. This "multimarginal" regime is central to modeling temporal evolution in dynamical systems in many scientific domains that can sample sequential distributions. We tackle this problem with a novel approach that leverages the connection between FM and dynamic optimal transport (OT), softly steering the flow towards the intermediate marginals through potential terms in the dynamic OT action. By extending the conditional FM learning target to incorporate these potentials, we derive an efficient, simulation-free algorithm for multimarginal FM that offers considerable flexibility in the spatiotemporal dynamics of the learned flows. We demonstrate state-of-the-art performance and training efficiency of OT-potential FM (OTP-FM) on diverse single-cell RNA sequencing, oceanographic, and meteorological datasets. Our code is available at https://github.com/Bexorg-Inc/OTP-FM.

Method: 作者引入了一个形式化的损失扩展层次结构，将模型参数映射到三棱柱的几何表面上。通过分析梯度流在不同极限条件下的行为，推导出了五个基本极限机制（大数据、小数据、平均场、窄隐层、自由机制），并针对其中四个机制推导了训练集和总体损失演化的显式解析表达式。

Conclusion: 研究表明，权重共享线性自动编码器的极限学习机制可以通过一个三棱柱模型进行系统性的分类。这种几何框架揭示了不同参数（输入维度、隐层维度、初始化幅度、数据集大小）如何交互并支配学习动力学，为理解复杂神经网络的训练过程提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Theoretical studies of machine learning models commonly consider different limiting regimes in which the learning dynamics of gradient descent becomes theoretically tractable. It is, however, desirable to have a systematically obtained picture of all qualitatively different extreme learning regimes for a particular type of models. In this paper we propose such a picture for large weight-tied linear autoencoders characterized by input and latent dimensions, initialization magnitude, and training set size. This model is nonlinear in the weights and its gradient flow does not have a general theoretical solution. We show that at the level of the formal loss-expansion hierarchy, its extreme regimes are naturally associated with faces of a triangular prism. In particular, there are five basic extreme regimes associated with the 2-faces of the prism: (1) large-data, (2) small-data, (3) mean-field, (4) narrow-latent, and (5) free. For regimes (1,2,3,4), we derive explicit expressions for both train and population limiting loss evolutions under gradient flow, obtaining very good agreement with experimental results.

### [244] [PJ-RoPE: A Fourier-Jet-Affine Position Space for Relative Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05345)

Method: 本文提出了一种通用的 PJ-RoPE 框架，将傅里叶相位、Jordan 喷流（Jets）和仿射 recency 统一为单一的、可学习的相对位置空间。该方法通过常系数差分算子模块化位置编码，利用 LC/rapidity 坐标稳定高阶项，并引入标量 PJ-偏差核与精确 PJ-旋转特征变换，通过受控探针进行诊断。

Conclusion: PJ-RoPE 框架通过数学上统一 RoPE、Jordan-RoPE 和 ALiBi，展示了相对位置编码在不同任务中对特定“位置空间”的选择偏好。研究表明，线性复杂度和仿射 recency 机制在处理长序列任务（如音乐序列）时具有显著优势，且通过高阶 Jet 修正可提升模型表现。

Abstract: We unify RoPE's Fourier phase, Jordan-RoPE's finite jets, and ALiBi's affine recency into a single learnable relative-position space, and study which regions of this space are selected by different tasks. PJ-RoPE is a Fourier-Jet-Affine formulation for relative attention, with an optional Poincare-type reading as the affine completion of a homogeneous Fourier-jet positional representation. Algebraically, the same primitives form a finite constant-coefficient difference module: simple roots of the lag-shift operator give Fourier/RoPE characters, repeated nonzero roots give Jordan/Fourier jets, and the repeated unit root gives ALiBi-like affine recency.
  The framework separates scalar PJ-bias kernels from exact PJ-rotary feature transforms, introduces adaptive sector diagnostics, and uses LC/rapidity coordinates to stabilize high-order jets. Controlled probes verify sector containment and selection; small language runs expose an affine/recency boundary; music-token streams provide the clearest case where LC/affine variants remain strong while carrying measurable high-order corrections; and LC diagnostics show a scale-stability gain coupled to phase-resolution loss.

### [245] [Mamba-Assisted Non-Markovian Closure for Reduced-Order Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05371)
*Zhi-Feng Wei,Saad Qadeer,Panos Stinis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于Mamba架构的MAC框架，通过建模非马尔可夫闭合项，有效提升了高维动力系统降阶模型在长期预测中的准确性与计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维动力系统的降阶建模（ROM）受限于“非马尔可夫闭合项”（即未解析变量对解析变量的影响），传统方法难以有效处理这些复杂的记忆效应，导致长期预测精度与稳定性不足。

Method: 提出“Mamba辅助闭合”（MAC）框架，将降阶模型中的闭合建模转化为序列建模问题。利用Mamba的双重表示特性：在训练阶段采用卷积形式实现序列到序列的高效并行计算，在部署阶段切换为循环形式实现常数级的步进推理，并将其嵌入到数值积分器中实时更新闭合项。

Result: 在粘性Burgers方程和混沌双尺度Lorenz '96系统中，MAC框架在预测精度和长期滚动稳定性方面均显著优于传统的马尔可夫降阶模型、基于GRU的序列模型以及Wilks方法。

Conclusion: Mamba架构作为一种高效的序列模型，通过模拟Mori-Zwanzig形式主义中的记忆效应，显著提升了高维动力系统降阶模型的预测精度与长期稳定性，证明了其在解决非马尔可夫闭合问题上的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Reduced-order modeling of high-dimensional dynamical systems is often hindered by the non-Markovian closure term that represents the effect of unresolved variables on the resolved dynamics. Inspired by the Mori--Zwanzig formalism, in which the closure takes the form of a memory functional of the resolved trajectory, we recast closure modeling as a sequence modeling problem and propose the Mamba-Assisted Closure (MAC) framework: a Mamba-based sequence model, trained to predict the closure from the resolved trajectory, is coupled with the reduced-order governing equations through a numerical integrator to advance the resolved variables in time. A key feature of the framework is its exploitation of the dual representation of state-space models -- the model is trained in a sequence-to-sequence fashion via the convolutional form, and deployed for step-by-step autoregressive rollout via the recurrent form, yielding both efficient long-trajectory training and constant per-step inference cost. On the viscous Burgers' equation and the chaotic two-scale Lorenz '96 system, the MAC model substantially outperforms the Markovian reduced-order model, the GRU-based sequence model, and the Wilks method in predictive accuracy and long-time rollout stability.

When multiple architectures are competitive, the framework further supports plausibility-weighted ensemble predictions that enhance predictive performance. Compared with a random-search baseline, EVIDENT identified smaller architectures with more consistent forecasting performance on unseen patients. These findings establish EVIDENT as a strategy to neural architecture discovery, enabling reliable model selection for high-consequence forecasting in data-limited and heterogeneous settings.

### [247] [SHALA-LLM: Smartly Handling Ambiguous Labels in Aligning LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05376)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型（LLM）对齐方法通常假设每个输入仅存在单一正确标签，忽略了人类标注中普遍存在的歧义和分歧。为了使模型更准确地反映人类判断的多样性并处理有争议的输入，需要一种能够建模标注歧义的对齐策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为SHALA-LLM的强化学习框架。该方法直接从标注者分布中进行学习，并通过一种动态机制在优化过程中对高度含糊的样本进行优先处理，从而建模完整的人类判断分布。

Result: 在ChaosNLI、GoEmotions和MSP-Podcast等对歧义敏感的基准测试中，SHALA-LLM表现卓越。在ChaosNLI上，其Jensen-Shannon距离降低了高达62.1%，同时F1分数提升了高达16.7%。

Conclusion: 本文提出将标注者间的不一致性视为有价值的信息而非噪声，通过SHALA-LLM框架直接对齐人类标注分布，不仅能显著提升模型在含糊任务上的概率分布拟合能力，还能同时增强其分类准确性。

Abstract: Many human-centered tasks, including natural language inference (NLI) and emotion recognition (ER), have multiple plausible interpretations, leading to label ambiguity and challenging disagreements across human annotators. As LLMs are increasingly deployed in real-world settings, faithfully modeling such ambiguity is essential to identify contested inputs, preserve variability in ambiguous cases, and capture the full distribution of human judgments. Yet, existing LLM alignment approaches have predominantly assumed a single correct label, excluding annotator disagreement during optimization. Instead of treating this ambiguity as noise, we show how to treat it as information that improves model behavior through a new algorithm called SMARTLY HANDLING AMBIGUOUS LABELS IN ALIGNING LLMS (SHALA-LLM). This reinforcement learning framework provides a new way for LLMs to learn directly from annotator distributions while dynamically prioritizing highly ambiguous samples during optimization. Experiments on ambiguity-sensitive NLI and ER benchmarks, including ChaosNLI, GoEmotions, and MSP-Podcast, demonstrate that SHALA-LLM improves agreement with annotator label distributions, e.g. on ChaosNLI, it reduces Jensen-Shannon Distance by up to 62.1%. At the same time, SHALA-LLM improves F1 by up to 16.7%, showing that modeling annotator disagreement can also strengthen classification performance.

</details>


### [248] [Pattern Selectivity is Not Task-Causal Structure: A Cross-Architecture Mechanistic Study of Composed-Task Circuits in 1B-Class Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05378)
*Yongzhong Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过统一的方法对多种大模型进行机械解释性测试，发现相同的任务在不同模型中由迥异的内部机制实现，揭示了模型机制的异质性，并对跨模型的普适性解释提出了质疑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究一套统一的机械解释性分析方法（即“筛选-消融”法）在不同模型家族中是否能产生一致的机制性结论。研究试图回答：不同架构和训练流水线下的模型是否通过相似的内部机制来完成相同的认知任务。

Method: 采用了统一的“筛选-消融”实验范式：首先通过任务模式选择性识别注意力头回路，随后利用匹配随机零假设进行因果消融验证。研究涵盖了四种复合任务（间接对象识别、大小比较、后继序列、变量绑定）及三种不同的1B级别语言模型（Pythia、OLMo、OLMoE），并引入了包含五个类别的结果分类学（主要原因、次要原因、相关性、干扰、空）进行量化评估。

Result: 实验结果显示，在12个测试单元中，没有两个单元共享相同的主要因果回路。相同的任务在不同模型中是由完全不同的注意力模式实现的。研究还发现，OLMoE模型倾向于在基础的“前一令牌”位置基底上构建任务回路，表现出与稠密模型不同的计算策略。

Conclusion: 尽管存在统一的筛选与消融方法论，模型对于相同任务的底层机制实现呈现出高度的特异性。这表明，在大语言模型领域，跨模型家族的“通用机械解释”往往是难以捉摸的，且模型通过不同的注意力模式实现相同的行为能力。作者提出了关于混合专家模型（MoE）依赖前向位置基底的假说，强调了任务特定性与模型架构耦合的重要性。

Abstract: We test whether a single screen-and-ablate recipe -- identify attention-head circuits by task-pattern selectivity, then verify by causal ablation against a matched-random null -- produces consistent mechanistic claims across model families. The recipe ports across pipelines; the specific circuit it identifies does not. Across four composed tasks (indirect-object identification, greater-than, successor sequences, variable binding) and three 1B-class language models from distinct training pipelines (Pythia 1B / Pile / dense; OLMo 1B / DCLM / dense; OLMoE 1B-7B / DCLM / mixture-of-experts), we run a unified protocol with the matched-random null sampled across ten seeds per cell. The resulting 12 (task, model) cells contain no two that share the same primary causal screen at comparable effect size: the same task, with the same behavioral capability, is implemented through different attention-pattern types across models.
  We introduce a five-category screen-outcome taxonomy -- primary cause, secondary cause, correlate, interferer, null -- with quantitative thresholds, and show that all five outcomes appear in the panel. We propose a falsifiable hypothesis: the MoE model in our panel builds composed-task circuits on top of a foundational previous-token positional substrate (the prev-token-circuit ablation is the strongest causal screen on 3 of 4 tasks for OLMoE 1B-7B), with the IOI exception consistent with IOI being a final-position name-copying task whose structure directly probes a different pattern. The hypothesis comes with explicit predictions for other MoE language models.
  We frame the methodology honestly: the spectral participation-ratio signal from the companion methodology paper is a general indicator of specialized computation; what makes a finding task-specific is the task-pattern screen plus a per-model causal verification.

### [249] [Generalized TV--$\ell_p$ Structured Priors for Bayesian $T_1$ Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05381)
*Disi Lin,Martin Berggren,Tommy Löfstedt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合总变差与 $\ell_p$ 范数的新型贝叶斯空间先验，在 $T_1$ 映射中通过增强空间一致性，有效降低了估计偏差与不确定性，实现了更精准的成像效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 $T_1$ 映射任务中，传统的估计方法往往难以同时兼顾参数估计的准确性、空间一致性以及可靠的不确定性量化。研究者旨在通过引入结构化的空间先验，解决估计过程中的偏差与方差问题，从而提升成像质量与可靠性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一类基于总变差（TV）与 $\ell_p$ 范数结合的结构化空间先验，将其融入贝叶斯回归框架中，不仅能够有效地增强 $T_1$ 映射的空间一致性和平滑性，还能提供更精确的参数不确定性量化。实验证明该方法优于传统的极大似然估计及其他贝叶斯先验方法，为 $T_1$ 映射提供了一种更稳健的估计方案。

Abstract: We propose an extended family of structured spatial priors that incorporates the total variation (TV) function with $\ell_p$ norms. The prior is proven to be proper and incorporated into a Bayesian regression framework to enable uncertainty quantification in $T_1$ mapping, with posterior inference performed using the No-U-Turn Sampler (NUTS). This TV--$\ell_p$ construction is proven to constitute a well-defined family of prior distributions, and it naturally enforces spatial consistency and smooth variations in the estimated parameter maps. The method was evaluated in comparison to maximum-likelihood estimation and several Bayesian alternative priors based on the uniform, Gamma, and bounded TV priors. The evaluation includes experiments on synthetic brain and cardiac $T_1$ mapping datasets, as well as a real in-vivo breast $T_1$ mapping dataset. The results show that the TV--$\ell_p$ prior yields more concentrated posterior densities, indicating reduced uncertainty. It also consistently achieves lower variance and smaller (negative) bias, leading to more reliable estimates. Overall, embedding a TV-based structured penalty along with $\ell_p$ norms in a prior in a Bayesian model improves spatial coherence in $T_1$ maps and enhances uncertainty quantification, offering a robust approach for $T_1$ mapping with uncertainties.

### [250] [Trust, but Don't Verify: Epistemic Blind Spots in LLM Source Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05403)
*Rohan N. Pradhan,Steve Goley*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 大语言模型在综合信息时存在严重的“认知对齐”偏差：模型更看重信息来源的专业文风而非内容逻辑，导致其无法识别出看似严谨但数值荒谬的虚假统计信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型常被作为认知代理用于综合多源信息，但人们并不清楚模型是在评估证据质量，还是仅仅基于表面呈现进行信息聚合。研究旨在揭示模型在处理多源统计信息时，是否真正具备识别虚假数据的能力，以及为何在合成过程中会忽略数值逻辑。

Method: 研究人员对Claude、Qwen、OLMo三个模型家族进行了跨领域实验，通过对比单一情境与多源合成情境下的模型表现，揭示了模型处理信息的机制。使用了因果追踪（causal tracing）、线性探针（linear probes）和组件级归因（component-level attribution）等机械可解释性方法，分析了模型内部表征与权重分配机制。

Result: 实验发现模型虽能独立识别虚假统计数据，但在多源合成任务中会失效。模型主要受限于“方法论-语域”门控机制，即倾向于相信看起来专业的论述（即便数值逻辑错误），而完全压制了数值有效性信号。此外，即使进行特定提示，模型也只会表现出无差别的怀疑，而非有效的鉴别。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在多源信息合成中存在“认知对齐”失效的问题。模型倾向于根据文本的风格（“分析性语域”）而非数值内容的真实性来评估信息来源的可靠性。这种对形式的过度依赖导致模型无法在复杂任务中甄别虚假统计数据，且现有的提示工程和后训练流程难以解决这一问题。

Abstract: Language models increasingly act as epistemic proxies, synthesizing evidence from multiple sources to inform decisions. Whether they evaluate the quality of that evidence, or merely aggregate it based on surface presentation, remains poorly understood. We show that models possess the capability to detect fabricated statistics (correct identification rates of 0.76-1.00 for methodology in isolation) but do not recruit this capability during multi-source synthesis, producing similar numeric estimates whether the statistics are fabricated or valid. Specifically, source influence is governed by a methodology-register gate that responds to the distributional register of analytical text but not to numeric validity: for example, statistically impossible confidence intervals receive the same weight as valid ones. The behavioral dissociation replicates across five models from three families (Claude, Qwen, OLMo) and three professional domains. Mechanistic analyses, including causal tracing, linear probes, and component-level attribution, converge on the same account: the model encodes and causally uses a methodology-register representation that transfers across domains (probe AUC 0.83-0.92), while numeric-validity signals, decodable in isolation, are suppressed to chance during multi-source synthesis. Prompting-based mitigations, even an oracle checklist naming the exact statistical checks, produce blanket skepticism rather than selective discernment, and the post-training pipelines we examine reinforce the stylistic shortcut without building numeric verification. Unlike sycophancy, which tracks user preference, this failure tracks whether a source presents as analytically credible, not whether its claims are internally consistent. We term this epistemic alignment: like preference and safety alignment, the question is not capability but deployment.

Abstract: As urban environments continue to evolve rapidly, accurately modeling the dynamic behaviour of Points of Interest is essential for supporting data-driven urban planning and commercial decision-making. While recent advancements in spatio-temporal graph learning have improved POI forecasting, most methods rely on proximity-based graphs and correlation-driven modeling, which overlook the functional dependencies between POIs and fail to capture the causal effects of urban interventions. In this paper, we introduce a novel research problem -- cold-start POI check-in forecasting, which aims to predict the future check-in pattern of a newly introduced POI, by modeling its temporal evolution and functional interactions with nearby POIs in a structured urban spatial context. To address these challenges, we propose CausalPOI, a spatio-temporal graph-based causal representation learning framework. CausalPOI leverages Spatio-Temporal Functional Interaction Graph to model semantic and spatial relationships between POIs, and constructs structurally aligned treatment and control graphs to simulate factual and counterfactual scenarios. Extensive experiments on real-world SafeGraph datasets demonstrate that CausalPOI significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines across the board, validating its effectiveness in spatio-temporal forecasting, semantic interaction modeling, and causal effect estimation, providing a more interpretable and actionable foundation for urban intervention analysis. Source code is available at Github.

### [252] [Selective-Advantage Entropy-Adaptive Horizon GRPO: Asymmetric Token-Level Discounting for Efficient Reinforcement Learning of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05434)
*Chirag Chawla,Rohan Charudatt Salvi,Madhav S. Baidya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SA-AH-GRPO，一种通过非对称折扣机制优化强化学习过程的新方法。该方法根据模型的不确定性加权策略梯度，并专门针对劣质路径进行折扣，在显著提升训练稳定性的同时，有效维持了模型推理任务的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的 GRPO 算法在处理语言模型对齐时，将所有 token 位置和采样回放同等对待，忽视了模型在不同生成阶段的不确定性，且容易在训练过程中产生不稳定性或熵崩溃。因此，需要一种能够感知模型不确定性并区分不同路径质量的优化策略。

Method: 研究提出了两种 GRPO 的扩展方法：(1) 自适应水平 GRPO (AH-GRPO)：利用基于累积熵的折扣来加权每个 token 的策略梯度，从而在模型不确定时减少有效时间跨度；(2) 选择性优势 AH-GRPO (SA-AH-GRPO)：仅将上述折扣应用于优势为负的回放路径，对高优势的成功路径则不进行衰减。

Result: 在 GSM8K 基准测试中，SA-AH-GRPO 表现优异。在 Qwen 2.5-3B 模型上，该方法不仅达到了与 GRPO 相当的峰值准确率（Pass@1 = 0.858），还将训练方差降低了 3.6 倍（0.0246），且在训练后期保持了极高的稳定性。在 1.5B 模型上也显著优于零样本基线。

Conclusion: 通过非对称折扣机制（即仅对低优势回放进行折扣），SA-AH-GRPO 能够有效保留高质量路径的梯度信息，防止熵崩溃，从而在推理任务中实现更稳定、更高效的模型对齐。这种方法为结构化生成任务中的强化学习提供了一种具有原则性的归纳偏置。

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) has emerged as an effective reinforcement-learning algorithm for aligning language models on reasoning tasks, but it treats every token position and every sampled rollout symmetrically. We introduce two complementary extensions: (i) Adaptive-Horizon GRPO (AH-GRPO), which weights each token's policy gradient using a cumulative entropy-based discount that reduces the effective horizon when the model is uncertain, and (ii) Selective-Advantage AH-GRPO (SA-AH-GRPO), which applies this discounting only to negative-advantage rollouts, leaving positive-advantage, successful trajectories unattenuated. We evaluate standard GRPO with alpha = 0, AH-GRPO with alpha = 0.5, and SA-AH-GRPO with alpha = 0.5 on the GSM8K mathematical reasoning benchmark using both Qwen 2.5-1.5B-Instruct and Qwen 2.5-3B-Instruct fine-tuned with LoRA. On the 3B model, SA-AH-GRPO achieves Pass@1 = 0.858 at its peak at step 30 and maintains 0.846 at 180 steps, with training variance reduced to 0.0246, a 3.6 times reduction relative to GRPO while matching its peak accuracy. On the 1.5B model, SA-AH-GRPO achieves a peak Pass@1 of 0.686, improving over the zero-shot baseline of 0.637. Our analysis shows that asymmetric discounting preserves the full gradient signal on correct solutions, prevents entropy collapse, and substantially stabilises training, suggesting a principled inductive bias for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards on structured generation tasks.

### [253] [DP-MacAdam: Differentially Private Mechanism with Adaptive Clipping and Adaptive Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05435)
*Naima Tasnim,Lalitha Sankar,Oliver Kosut*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 DP-MacAdam 算法，通过整合自适应梯度裁剪与自适应动量更新，在差分隐私框架下实现了更优的训练性能和自动化调节，克服了现有算法需要手动调参的缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的差分隐私优化算法中，自适应裁剪（用于限制敏感度）与动量加速（用于提升收敛速度）通常是分开设计的，未能充分利用同一组梯度统计量，且传统的固定阈值裁剪在实际应用中具有局限性，需要手动调参。

Method: 提出 DP-MacAdam 算法，将梯度估计的经验均值和方差同时应用于自适应梯度裁剪（类似于 AdaClip）和动量加速（类似于 DP-Adam），并通过理论分析证明该方法能实现无偏的梯度方差估计。

Result: 实验表明，DP-MacAdam 在模型精度和隐私保护表现上均优于现有的 DP-SGD、AdaClip 和 DP-Adam 基准方法，且消除了手动调整裁剪阈值的需求。

Conclusion: DP-MacAdam 通过统一梯度统计量的使用，实现了自适应裁剪与动量更新的协同优化，在无需手动调整裁剪阈值的情况下，有效提升了差分隐私机器学习的实用性和训练稳定性。

Abstract: Differentially private stochastic gradient descent (DP-SGD) has become the standard framework for privacy-preserving machine learning, yet its reliance on a fixed gradient clipping threshold to limit sensitivity remains a significant practical limitation. Adaptive clipping algorithms such as AdaClip shift and scale the gradient prior to clipping and adding noise so that the clipped gradient yields a more informative descent direction. The shift and scaling parameters are selected adaptively based on the empirical mean and variance. However, in existing adaptive clipping algorithms, these empirical estimates have not been also used for momentum to accelerate training itself. On the other hand, DP-Adam is an algorithm that exploits Adam-like momentum updates based on the gradient mean and variance to accelerate training, but does not exploit these estimates for adaptive clipping. In this work, we propose Differentially Private Mechanism with Adaptive Clipping and Adaptive Momentum (DP-MacAdam), a novel algorithm that combines these two approaches so as to use the same mean and variance estimates for both clipping and momentum. We perform an analysis showing that DP-MacAdam estimates the gradient variances in a bias-free manner. In addition, we empirically evaluate the privacy and accuracy of DP-MacAdam, demonstrating that it achieves improved model utility compared to DP-SGD, AdaClip, and DP-Adam baselines, without requiring manual tuning of the clipping threshold.

### [254] [Sharp First-Order Lower Bounds for Higher-Order Smooth Nonconvex Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05438)
*Dongruo Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文解决了高阶光滑非凸优化中确定性一阶预言机复杂度的理论缺口，通过构造“块链”硬实例，证明了在 Lipschitz Hessian 和三阶导数等条件下，已知的加速复杂度速率即为全局最优的下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管在 Lipschitz 梯度条件下 \(\epsilon^{-2}\) 的复杂度已是经典最优解，但在具备更高阶光滑性假设（如 Lipschitz Hessian 或 Lipschitz 三阶导数）时，已知的加速上限（如 \(\epsilon^{-7/4}\) 和 \(\epsilon^{-5/3}\)）与下界之间长期存在差距，本文旨在解决这一理论缺口，探究高阶光滑性下确定性一阶预言机的最优复杂度。

Method: 提出了一种基于“块链（block-chain）”机制的构造方法。该机制通过强制分块的预言机揭示过程，同时保持标量硬实例所需的光滑性结构，成功构造出了针对高阶光滑函数的维度无关（dimension-free）一阶下界。该方法特别利用了 AI 辅助发现构造方案并经作者验证。

Result: 成功推导出了适用于任意有限光滑阶数的维度无关一阶下界。特别地，该研究为 Hessian-Lipschitz 情况给出了 \(\Omega(\epsilon^{-7/4})\) 的下界，并为三阶光滑情况给出了 \(\Omega(\epsilon^{-5/3})\) 的下界，证明了此前已知的加速上限即为理论最优。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了高阶光滑非凸优化中确定性一阶预言机复杂度的下界，填补了现有理论空白。研究确认了 Lipschitz Hessian 和 Lipschitz 三阶导数情况下的最优速率，证明了这些加速速率不仅在理论上可行，而且在信息论意义上是最优的。

Abstract: We study the deterministic first-order oracle complexity of finding \(ε\)-stationary points in smooth nonconvex optimization when the objective satisfies higher-order smoothness assumptions. While the classical \(ε^{-2}\) rate is optimal under only Lipschitz gradients, higher-order smoothness leads to accelerated first-order upper bounds, most notably the \(ε^{-7/4}\) rate under Lipschitz Hessians and the \(ε^{-5/3}\) rate under Lipschitz third derivatives. The matching lower bounds, however, have remained open. We resolve this gap by proving a new dimension-free first-order lower bound for higher-order smooth nonconvex functions, valid for every finite smoothness order. In particular, our construction gives a matching \(Ω(ε^{-7/4})\) lower bound in the Hessian-Lipschitz case and a matching \(Ω(ε^{-5/3})\) lower bound in the third-order-smooth regime. The hard instance is based on a \emph{block-chain} mechanism that enforces blockwise oracle revelation while preserving the smoothness structure needed for the scalar hard instance. The lower-bound construction was discovered with the assistance of ChatGPT 5.5 Pro and subsequently verified by the authors.

</details>


### [255] [GOTabPFN: From Feature Ordering to Compact Tokenization for Tabular Foundation Models on High-Dimensional Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05441)
*Al Zadid Sultan Bin Habib,Md Younus Ahamed,Prashnna Kumar Gyawali,Gianfranco Doretto,Donald A. Adjeroh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为GOTabPFN的新型模型，通过图引导的特征排序和神经启发式特征压缩，成功解决了表格基础模型在处理高维、小样本数据时的效率与性能瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的表格基础模型在处理高维、低样本量（HDLSS）数据时，往往受限于token预算和计算效率，难以直接应用；需要一种无需大规模重训练即可在受限资源下实现高效预测的方法。

Method: 提出Graph-guided Ordering with Local Refinement (GO-LR)方法，通过权重最小线性排列（Weighted Minimum Linear Arrangement）实现特征排序；引入Neuro-Inspired Subunit Compression (NSC)单元，将邻近特征压缩为元特征，从而适配TabPFN的小型化预测框架。

Result: 在多个表格数据集基准测试中，GOTabPFN在严格的token预算限制下表现出比现有模型更高的稳定性和预测准确度。

Conclusion: GOTabPFN通过结合特征排序与子单元压缩，为HDLSS（高维低样本量）场景下的表格数据预测提供了一种高效且紧凑的解决方案，证明了在不重训练大型基座模型的情况下，通过有效的特征工程与表示学习仍能提升预测表现。

Abstract: We investigate how to make small tabular foundation models effective for High-Dimensional, Low-Sample Size (HDLSS) tabular prediction without retraining large backbones. We introduce Graph-guided Ordering with Local Refinement (GO-LR), show its equivalence to weighted Minimum Linear Arrangement, and interpret the practical solver as a TSP-path-style surrogate. We propose GOTabPFN,which builds on GO-LR, and a Neuro-Inspired Subunit Compression (NSC) unit to pool locally adjacent ordered features into meta-features, yielding a compact representation that makes TabPFN-style prediction practical in HDLSS regimes. Across tabular benchmarks, GOTabPFN improves stability and accuracy under tight token budgets.

*Raffael Theiler,Lev Telyatnikov,Leandro Von Krannichfeldt,Olga Fink*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对工业PHM数据碎片化和标签稀缺的难题，本文提出将时间序列转换为表格数据，并利用表格基础模型进行上下文学习。研究证明该方法在故障预测与诊断任务中优于传统的序列模型和梯度提升树，且具有极高的数据效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种将工业时间序列转化为表格数据行的方法，从而能够应用“表格基础模型”（Tabular Foundation Models）进行上下文学习（In-context Learning）。研究在统一的评估协议下，将其与序列模型、Transformer基准模型以及梯度提升树（GBDT）进行了对比分析，重点考察了其在预测（Prognostics）和诊断（Diagnostics）任务中的性能。

Conclusion: 本文的研究表明，表格基础模型（Tabular Foundation Models）为解决PHM（故障预测与健康管理）领域中的异构数据问题提供了一种通用且高效的接口。通过合理的上下文构建，这些模型能够超越传统的序列模型和梯度提升树，特别是在低数据量场景下表现出极强的竞争力和鲁棒性，是推动工业智能维护系统可重用性的有效途径。

Abstract: Data-driven Prognostics and Health Management (PHM) uses time-varying condition-monitoring data to diagnose system states and estimate remaining useful life in engineered assets. Foundation models offer a route toward reusable predictive systems, yet most time-series foundation models are designed for forecasting and assume long, coherent, regularly sampled sequences. To address this gap, we propose a framework for applying Tabular Foundation Models to industrial time series using in-context learning, and we evaluate them on a variety of PHM tasks. By converting raw unit-level signals into tabular rows, we show that these models perform well across multiple tasks - including prognostics, and diagnostics - and are highly data efficient. We compare them directly with sequence models, transformer baselines, and gradient-boosted trees under a common evaluation protocol. The results indicate that tabular foundation models achieve the best average ranks across prognostic and diagnostic tasks. Our findings further show that PFN-based models are competitive in low-data regimes, that temporal context can be preserved in the tabular representation, and that performance depends on representative context construction under subsampling. These results demonstrate that tabular foundation models provide a practical and general interface for heterogeneous PHM problems.

### [257] [Learned Subspace Compression for Communication-Efficient Pipeline Parallelism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05484)
*Paul Janson,Edouard Oyallon,Eugene Belilovsky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大规模模型流水线并行训练中的通信瓶颈，本文提出了 MAPL 方法，通过在 Stiefel 流形上学习自适应的正交投影，配合锚点嵌入技术，在极低通信开销下实现了高效的模型压缩与训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低带宽网络下，流水线并行训练大型语言模型时，跨阶段激活值的通信成为主要瓶颈。现有的固定正交投影压缩方法会导致显著的性能下降，且难以优化；而简单的低秩投影学习又难以维持训练过程中的正交性。

Method: 1. 提出 MAPL（流形感知投影学习），将压缩投影视为施加了 Stiefel 流形约束的可学习正交矩阵。
2. 利用流形约束最速下降法（Manifold-constrained steepest descent），允许各流水线阶段动态学习任务最优的压缩子空间。
3. 引入分段式锚点嵌入（Factorized anchor embeddings），在通信开销极小的情况下实现激活值的全秩重建。
4. 结合残差向量量化与流式码本同步协议，进一步摊销字典传输成本。

Result: 在 150M 到 1B 参数规模的 LLaMA 模型上，MAPL 实现了高压缩比，且性能衰减几乎可以忽略不计。与现有的子空间网络（Subspace Networks）相比，MAPL 在性能与压缩率之间的权衡上具有显著优势。

Conclusion: MAPL 证明了在流水线并行训练中，通过在流形上施加正交约束来学习低秩投影是可行的。该方法通过动态适应压缩子空间并结合锚点嵌入，在显著降低通信开销的同时，保持了与全精度训练相当的性能，为大规模模型在低带宽网络下的高效训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: Pipeline parallelism enables training of large language models that exceed single-device memory, yet inter-stage activation communication becomes the dominant bottleneck when trained on low-bandwidth networks. Recent work in this area has proposed using fixed orthogonal projections to compress activations. However, this still results in a significant performance degradation and requires a number of non-standard adaptations to constrain the optimization. A natural alternative is to learn a low rank projection for each pipeline stage, however maintaining the necessary orthogonality of these projectors during training remains a challenge. We present Manifold Aware Projection Learning (MAPL), a method that treats inter-stage compression as a learnable orthogonal projection under explicit Stiefel manifold (orthogonal matrices) constraints. Rather than prescribing a fixed global subspace, MAPL lets each pipeline stage discover and continuously adapt its own task-optimal compression subspace via manifold-constrained steepest descent. To recover token-specific signals at stage boundaries, we introduce per-stage factorized anchor embeddings that allow for full-rank activation reconstruction with negligible communication overhead. We further show that we can incorporate residual vector quantization after projection with a streaming codebook synchronization protocol that amortizes dictionary communication. Across LLaMA models from 150M to 1B parameters we show that MAPL can be easily applied to the existing pipeline and can achieve high compression with neglibile performance degradation with a drastically improved tradeoffs in performance vs. compression compared to Subspace Networks.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现：1. 更强的模型在任务和项目层面与人类对齐更好；2. 在捕捉人类的试次级错误分布方面，模型表现不一，有时较小的模型反而与年幼儿童的错误分布更相似；3. 即使是表现最好的模型在矩阵推理和心理旋转任务上也表现吃力。

Conclusion: 当前的视觉语言模型（VLM）仅能部分模拟儿童的认知能力。尽管模型规模增大能提升任务和项目层面的对齐度，但在捕捉人类的错误模式方面表现各异，且在矩阵推理和心理旋转等特定任务上仍存在显著瓶颈。

Abstract: Given the inherently multimodal nature of human experience, vision-language models (VLMs) hold substantial promise for modeling human cognition as it grows and develops with experience. Realizing their potential requires tools for comparing VLMs with human cognitive development across tasks, ages, and populations. We present LEVANTE-bench, a benchmark based on tasks and data from the Learning Variability Network (LEVANTE), which distributes open-source tasks and data measuring children's cognition across languages and cultures. In LEVANTE-bench, we systematically assess VLMs on six tasks, comparing their alignment with children aged 5-12 ($N$ = 1547) across three countries. We compare models at multiple scales, assessing their overall accuracy, their task- and item-level alignment with children, and how well they match children's trial-level error distributions. Alignment was heterogeneous across scales: at the level of tasks and items, more capable models aligned better with humans. However, match to human error distributions varied widely across tasks, and for several tasks, smaller models matched younger children's errors better. In addition, even the best-performing VLMs struggled on matrix reasoning and mental rotation tasks. Thus, current VLM architectures align only partially with the cognitive abilities of children.

### [259] [Dominant-Layer ZO: A Single Layer Dominates Zeroth-Order Fine-Tuning of LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05516)
*Wanhao Yu,Ziyan Wang,Zheng Wang,Abeer Matar Almalky,Yihang Zuo,Shuteng Niu,Sen Lin,Adnan Siraj Rakin,Deliang Fan,Li Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现大模型零阶优化（ZO）微调过程中存在“单层支配”现象，通过预先定位并仅微调关键的单一解码层，即可在显著提升训练速度（最高4.52倍）的同时，实现媲美甚至优于全模型微调的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管零阶优化（ZO）能够通过仅利用前向传播实现内存高效的微调，但目前尚不清楚不同层在适应任务过程中的贡献分布情况，以及如何通过优化微调策略来提升ZO的训练效率。

Method: 1. 观察并揭示了ZO微调中性能主要由单个解码层决定的现象。2. 提出了一种基于激活异常值（activation outliers）的启发式方法，在训练前即可定位该主导层。3. 通过分析扰动效应在残差流中的传播机制，解释了为什么高扰动敏感度且位置靠前的层能产生更强的优化信号。4. 在LLaMA2-7B和Qwen3-8B模型上进行了广泛的基准测试验证。

Result: 研究发现ZO微调受单一解码层支配，该层在模型结构中位置靠前且对扰动极其敏感。通过仅微调这一层，在九个基准测试中平均性能优于全模型ZO微调和基于LoRA的ZO微调，同时训练速度提升高达4.52倍。

Conclusion: 零阶优化（ZO）微调大模型时存在“单层支配”现象，即仅对特定的主导层进行微调即可达到甚至超过全参数微调的效果。该主导层可以通过预训练模型中的激活异常值分布预先识别，这种方法极大地提升了训练效率并降低了资源需求。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (ZO) optimization enables memory-efficient fine-tuning of large language models (LLMs) using only forward passes, but it remains unclear how useful adaptation is distributed across layers. In this work, we reveal a surprising phenomenon: ZO fine-tuning is sharply dominated by a single decoding layer. Across multiple LLM families and downstream tasks, fine-tuning this dominant layer alone consistently matches or even exceeds full-model ZO fine-tuning. We further show that the dominant layer is task-agnostic but model-specific, and can be identified before training through a simple inference-only analysis of activation outliers. Specifically, the dominant layer consistently aligns with the first activation-outlier layer in the pre-trained model. To explain this phenomenon, we analyze how perturbation effects propagate under ZO optimization. We find that the dominant layer combines two key properties: high perturbation sensitivity and early placement in the residual stream, allowing perturbation-induced effects to propagate and accumulate through remaining subsequent decoding layers. As a result, this layer produces disproportionately strong and stable optimization signals under forward-only updates. Extensive experiments on LLaMA2-7B and Qwen3-8B across nine benchmarks show that dominant-layer ZO fine-tuning improves average performance over full-model MeZO and LoRA-based ZO fine-tuning while achieving up to 4.52$\times$ training speedup.

### [260] [What Objects Enable, Not What They Are: Functional Latent Spaces for Affordance Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05533)
*Rohan Siva,Neel P. Bhatt,Yunhao Yang,Seoyoung Lee,Nishant Gadde,Christian Ellis,Alvaro Velasquez,Zhangyang Wang,Ufuk Topcu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: A4D 提出了一种基于“功能性（Affordance）”而非“外观”的机器人规划框架，通过将视觉观测映射到功能潜在空间，显著提升了机器人在新颖场景下的交互泛化能力与推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器人规划系统过于依赖基于外观的视觉推理，难以捕捉对象在任务中的功能性（如“是否可移动”），导致模型在处理新颖的机器人-对象交互时泛化能力不足。

Method: 1. 构建了以功能（Affordance）为中心的共享潜在空间，将视觉观测映射到该空间中；2. 通过测量观测值与功能点的距离来推理对象的任务相关属性；3. 设计了一种功能发现机制，利用潜在空间内的邻近度量来量化推理不确定性，并根据不确定性自主触发新功能的学习与扩展。

Result: 1. 在已知功能的推理准确率上达到了94%，领先现有最先进方法超过15个百分点；2. 在处理未知功能时，推理准确率从70%提升至90%以上，且仅需不到原始训练数据10%的样本；3. 推理速度提升了100倍。

Conclusion: A4D 通过引入以功能性为基础的潜在空间，成功解决了机器人规划中因过度依赖外观而导致的泛化能力差的问题。该方法不仅在已知功能推理上表现优异，还具备高效的未知功能发现能力，为机器人处理复杂、新颖的交互任务提供了鲁棒的框架。

Abstract: Existing robot planning systems rely on appearance-based reasoning, where visual observations are encoded into latent spaces organized around object appearances (e.g., recognizing a "cart" based on how it looks). However, planning requires reasoning about task-relevant functionalities of objects (e.g., whether an object is "movable"), which appearance-based latent spaces do not capture. As a result, existing approaches struggle to generalize to novel robot-object interactions. We address this limited generalizability through affordance reasoning, enabling planning based on task-relevant object functionalities instead of appearance alone. We introduce A4D, which maps visual observations into a shared latent space structured around affordances (e.g., "movable"). By projecting visual observations into this functional latent space and measuring their proximity to affordances, A4D infers functionalities relevant to the observed object. Furthermore, we introduce an affordance discovery mechanism that expands the latent space to handle unseen scenarios where existing affordances are insufficient. A4D uses proximity in the functional latent space to quantify uncertainty in affordance inference and selectively triggers affordance discovery. We evaluate A4D across several planning tasks involving diverse and unseen affordances. A4D achieves 94% inference accuracy on existing affordances outperforming state-of-the-art approaches by over 15% points, improves new-affordance inference accuracy from 70% to over 90% with fewer than 10% of the original training data, and enables 100x faster inference. Code, videos, and data available at: https://A4Dance-reasoning.github.io.

### [261] [Less is MoE: Trimming Experts in Domain-Specialist Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05538)
*Haoze He,Xinkai Zou,Xuan Jiang,Xingyuan Ding,Ao Qu,Juncheng Billy Li,Heather Miller*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对MoE模型压缩效果不佳的问题，提出了一种基于Fisher重要性评估的FFN中间维度剪枝方法（Fisher-MoE），在显著减少参数量和提升推理速度的同时，能够比传统压缩手段更好地保持模型的通用能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的MoE压缩方法在处理除常识推理以外的通用任务时表现不佳，且模型巨大的参数量限制了其在实际场景中的部署。研究旨在通过分析模型能力在MoE架构中的分布规律，寻找更有效的压缩粒度和策略，以实现性能与效率的平衡。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为“Fisher-MoE”的压缩方法。核心思路是利用Fisher信息度量来识别FFN层中对任务至关重要的中间维度，并据此进行剪枝。研究对比了激活值、路由分数及权重幅度等多种排序指标，最终确定Fisher重要性是识别关键维度最有效的方法。

Result: 在保持50%压缩比的前提下，Fisher-MoE不仅有效地保留了模型的核心能力，还将权重内存占有量降低了约45%，并将推理吞吐量提升了21%。此外，实验表明通过移除极少量的关键中间维度，模型在特定任务上的性能会发生剧变，证明了该粒度对性能评估的关键性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了MoE模型中的能力高度集中在FFN层的中间维度，通过Fisher重要性评估对这些维度进行剪枝（即Fisher-MoE），能够以更细的粒度实现高效压缩。该方法在大幅降低模型参数量和提升推理速度的同时，显著优于现有的MoE压缩技术，能够有效平衡通用能力与模型性能。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models achieve strong performance through conditional computation, but their large parameter footprint poses deployment challenges. Prior MoE compression approaches catastrophically fail when evaluated on general-purpose benchmarks beyond commonsense reasoning. We trace this failure to the granularity of compression: important capabilities are distributed across experts but concentrated in FFN sparse intermediate dimensions. To identify these dimensions, we use Fisher importance which outperforms activation-, router-score-, and magnitude-based alternatives, and identifies tiny sets of task-critical dimensions: in Qwen1.5-MoE, removing as few as 12 of 1.35M routed-FFN intermediate dimensions collapses GSM8K accuracy while largely preserving factual-knowledge performance. Building on this, we propose Fisher-MoE, which operates within FFN to remove intermediate dimensions ranked by Fisher importance. At the same 50% MoE compression ratio, Fisher-MoE preserves model capability, while reducing weight memory by ~45% and improving inference throughput by 21%. These findings suggest intermediate dimension granularity is an effective unit for both compression and ranking where capability concentrates in MoE models.

</details>


### [262] [Balancing Image Compression and Generation with Bootstrapped Tokenization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05552)
*Haozhe Chi,Jinghan Li,Hao Jiang,Wu Sheng,Yi Ma,Jing Wang,Yadong Mu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SelfBootTok通过将图像token显式拆分为全局和局部两类，利用自引导学习让生成器仅关注全局信息，从而在大幅降低计算开销的同时，显著提升了图像生成的效果与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像分词方法将不同粒度的信息混合在单个token中，导致冗余信息严重，且增加了生成器学习的难度。

Method: 提出SelfBootTok方法，将图像分块信息显式解耦为“全局”与“局部”两组token；采用自引导学习（Self-bootstrapped learning），强制生成器仅通过全局token推断局部细节，从而实现分层的表征学习。

Result: 该方法实现了约40%的计算量减少，同时提升了重建与生成质量；在仅使用64个token的情况下，取得了1.56的gFID分数，达到SOTA水平。

Conclusion: SelfBootTok通过解耦全局与局部信息，成功减轻了生成器的负担，并证明了该范式在视觉生成任务中具有极佳的扩展性和高效性。

Abstract: Despite progress in image tokenization, standard methods encode redundant information by mixing all granularities within each token, thus redundancy persists between tokens. The mix of information of different granularity also complicates the training of generators. This paper introduces SelfBootTok, a method that resolves this by cleanly decomposing information into global and local token groups. Through self-bootstrapped learning, the model predicts local details exclusively from global tokens, shifting the burden of visual details from the generator to the tokenizer. Consequently, our generator is far more efficient, requiring only global tokens and reducing computation by approximately 40%, while delivering superior reconstruction and generation. Moreover, this paradigm scales elegantly: by leveraging more data or parameters to self-supervise local representation learning, SelfBootTok achieves a new state-of-the-art gFID score of 1.56 using only 64 tokens.

### [263] [Representation Learning Enables Scalable Multitask Deep Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05555)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 MR.Q 的无模型强化学习算法，将其与预测性辅助目标相结合，构建了一个可扩展的行动者-评论者（Actor-Critic）架构。该方法侧重于利用高容量的价值函数逼近器，通过辅助任务学习环境的预测性表征，而非进行在线规划。

Result: 在多种多任务连续控制任务中，MR.Q 算法表现优于现有的基于世界模型的方法及多种深度强化学习基线模型。此外，该方法显著降低了计算开销，提升了挂钟时间（wall-clock）效率，且随着模型容量的增加表现出持续的性能提升。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，在多任务强化学习中，强大的表征学习（尤其是预测性表征）远比复杂的基于模型的控制和规划更为关键。通过将预测性辅助任务与高容量的无模型强化学习算法相结合，可以在无需显式规划的情况下实现卓越的性能和计算效率。

Abstract: Scaling reinforcement learning (RL) to diverse multitask settings remains a central challenge. While recent advances in model-based RL achieve strong performance, they rely on planning and complex training pipelines, making it unclear which components are essential for scalability. We revisit this question and argue that the primary driver of scalable multitask RL is not model-based control, but \emph{representation learning}. In particular, we show that combining predictive, model-based representations with high-capacity value function approximation is sufficient to achieve strong performance, even without planning. We evaluate a simple model-free algorithm, MR.Q, coupled with auxiliary predictive objectives into a scalable actor-critic architecture. This approach outperforms a recent world-model-based method and a range of deep RL baselines across a diverse suite of multitask continuous control tasks, while significantly reducing computational overhead and improving wall-clock efficiency. We observe consistent improvements with increased model capacity and show through ablations that predictive representation learning is critical for performance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用高斯噪声增强的数值模拟数据训练的多分辨率ConvLSTM框架，能够有效克服仿真与现实数据间的差异，在实际工程（如基坑支护结构变形预测）中展现出高精度与鲁棒性，为岩土工程的智能化监测与预测提供了可靠工具。

Abstract: This study presents a comprehensive field validation of a multi-resolution Convolutional Long Short-Term Memory (ConvLSTM) framework for predicting retaining wall deformation during staged excavation. The framework is trained on Gaussian noise-augmented numerical simulations and integrates ConvLSTM models operating at different temporal resolutions through a stacking ensemble strategy. The proposed framework is validated using field monitoring data from 34 inclinometers across 11 excavation sites in South Korea. Site-wise prediction performance is systematically evaluated using multiple evaluation metrics, with analyses of the influence of temporal deformation irregularity and spatiotemporal prediction characteristics on model performance. The results demonstrate that the framework predicts retaining wall deformation associated with up to 5.0 m of additional excavation with an average mean absolute error of 1.4 mm and a coefficient of determination of 0.93 across the excavation sites. These results indicate that the framework, although trained exclusively on numerically simulated and augmented database, can be effectively applied to diverse field excavation conditions and achieve a reliable level of prediction accuracy in practical retaining wall deformation prediction.

### [265] [Autoregressive Diffusion World Models for Off-Policy Evaluation of LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05558)
*Kaixuan Liu,Guojun Xiong,Weinan Zhang,Shengpu Tang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ADWM 是一个用于离线评估 LLM 智能体的扩散世界模型框架，它通过交互式地模拟智能体决策过程，实现了无需在线环境交互的高精度性能估计，有效解决了离散文本动作与评估累积误差的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多轮交互环境中评估大语言模型（LLM）智能体不仅成本高昂，而且存在风险。现有的离线策略评估（OPE）方法难以直接应用于 LLM 智能体，因为智能体需要根据环境观测动态生成离散文本动作，而传统的扩散模型无法有效处理这种交互性质。因此，亟需一种无需在线交互即可准确评估 LLM 智能体性能的离线方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ADWM（自回归扩散世界模型）的评估框架。该方法将每个环境转换建模为独立的去噪过程，避免了自回归模型常见的累积误差；同时，利用待评估 LLM 智能体作为策略条件引导扩散生成过程，通过交互式采样的方式实现对智能体决策模式的精确模拟。

Result: 实验结果表明，ADWM 在多个多轮智能体任务中均实现了准确的价值估计，并展现了极高的评估可靠性。与基准方法相比，ADWM 能够更好地反映智能体的真实性能，验证了其作为一种离线评估 LLM 智能体实用框架的潜力。

Conclusion: ADWM 是一种高效且可靠的离线评估框架，能够通过学习潜在扩散世界模型，准确模拟 LLM 智能体在多轮交互环境中的行为。该方法不仅克服了在线评估的高成本和高风险，还通过策略条件引导解决了传统扩散模型在处理离散动作序列时的局限性，为 LLM 智能体的评估提供了一种实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Evaluating large language model (LLM) agents in multi-turn interactive environments is expensive and risky, as it requires online environment interaction. We propose ADWM (Autoregressive Diffusion World Model), an evaluation framework that estimates the performance of a new LLM agent policy purely from pre-collected trajectories. The core idea is to learn a latent diffusion world model that simulates how the environment responds to the evaluation policy, without ever executing it in the real environment. Existing diffusion-based OPE methods guide full trajectories in a single pass by jointly diffusing states and actions, an assumption that breaks down for LLM agents whose actions are discrete text that must be sampled from the policy after observing the environment. Unlike autoregressive world models that suffer from compounding errors, ADWM models each transition as an independent denoising process, enabling reliable step-by-step rollouts where the world model and agent alternate in causal order. Crucially, the LLM agent under evaluation directly guides the diffusion generation at each step via a policy-conditioned score function, ensuring that simulated trajectories accurately reflect its decision-making patterns. Empirically, ADWM achieves accurate value estimates and evaluation reliability across diverse multi-turn agent tasks, demonstrating its promise as a practical framework for offline LLM agent evaluation.

### [266] [CLaaS: Continual learning as a service for sample efficient online learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05559)
*Kion Fallah,Silen Naihin,Barak Widawsky,Qingqing Mao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 CLaaS 系统，通过经验回放实现大模型智能体在动态环境中的在线持续学习，解决了环境无法重置带来的数据限制问题，并证明了参数更新在性能迁移和防止遗忘方面优于上下文学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 部署在大语言模型中的智能体需要适应动态环境下的分布偏移，且由于真实环境通常无法轻松重置（即每个场景只能采样一次），现有的学习范式难以兼顾“利用过往经验”与“适应未来任务”。因此，研究者旨在开发一种能在部署期间持续从数据流中学习，同时保持既有能力并实现迁移的在线学习框架。

Method: 提出了“持续学习即服务”（CLaaS）系统。该方法通过将智能体的执行轨迹存储在经验回放缓冲区（Experience Replay Buffer）中，支持在后台进行异步梯度更新，从而在不可重置的真实环境限制下，提高样本利用效率并实现模型在部署过程中的自我进化。

Result: 在对抗性任务上的评估结果显示，基于 CLaaS 的参数更新策略在样本效率、前向迁移能力以及遗忘抑制方面均优于传统的上下文学习方法，验证了经验回放机制对于在线持续学习的重要性。

Conclusion: CLaaS 架构证明了通过经验回放进行参数更新是实现大语言模型智能体在线持续学习的有效途径，在处理动态环境中的分布偏移问题上，比单纯的上下文学习（In-context learning）具有更好的前向迁移能力，且能有效缓解遗忘现象。

Abstract: Deployed large language model agents must adapt to distribution shift in dynamic environments. Ideally, adaptation can be performed from accumulated agent experiences and retain prior capabilities while transferring to future tasks. However, agent actions and environmental transitions can only be sampled once per scenario, as real-world environments cannot be trivially reset. To this end, we investigate an experiential and online continual learning setting in which agents learn from a stream of scenarios. We propose continual learning as-a-service (CLaaS), a system which enables agents to improve during deployment, abstracted behind a chat API. To increase sample efficiency, CLaaS stores rollouts in an experience replay buffer for gradient reuse during asynchronous training. We evaluate CLaaS on an adversarial task, demonstrating that parametric updates lead to superior forward transfer and less forgetting than in-context learning, with replay being a critical choice for sample efficiency.

</details>


### [267] [AsyncWebRL: Efficient Multi-Step RL for Visual Web Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05597)
*Hao Bai,Rui Yang,Chenlu Ye,Spencer Whitehead,Aviral Kumar,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AsyncWebRL 是一种通过异步并行优化和改进强化学习归一化策略的框架，显著降低了网页智能体训练的计算成本并大幅提升了任务成功率，有效解决了现有方法的效率瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 训练视觉-语言网页智能体时，使用多步强化学习存在两大效率低下的痛点：一是同步强化学习导致 GPU 空闲时间过长；二是训练轨迹中存在冗长的步骤和过多的标记（token）浪费。

Method: 1. 系统层面：采用异步设计（AsyncWebRL），通过重叠 rollout、梯度更新和策略刷新，结合“永久 rollout 池”和轻量级截图处理机制，显著提高了并行效率。2. 算法层面：修正了多步 GRPO 中的归一化项，将原本基于轨迹长度的归一化（1/|τi|）替换为常数（1/k），消除了因轨迹长度导致的梯度偏差，从而鼓励模型生成更简洁、高效的操作路径。

Result: 1. 训练吞吐量：相比现有的同步流水线（WebGym），端到端训练速度提升了 2.9 倍。2. 性能表现：在 WebGym 域外测试集上达到新的最先进（SOTA）水平，整体成功率提升 5.8%，在挑战性较高的任务切片上性能提升显著（中等难度提升 42%，高难度提升 48%）。

Conclusion: AsyncWebRL 通过系统与算法层面的双重优化，有效解决了 Web 智能体训练中的效率瓶颈，为多步强化学习训练网页智能体提供了一种高效、高性能的新标准。

Abstract: Training vision-language web agents with multi-step RL is compute-intensive, with two dominant forms of inefficiency: idle GPUs in synchronous RL, and trajectories that use more steps and tokens than necessary. We present AsyncWebRL, which addresses both. On the system side, an asynchronous design overlaps rollout, gradient update, and policy refresh across iterations, paired with two web-agent-specific adaptations, namely an everlasting rollout pool and lightweight screenshot handling, that together deliver up to a $2.9\times$ end-to-end training-throughput speedup over the previously fastest open synchronous pipeline (WebGym). On the algorithmic side, we identify the per-trajectory normalizer $1/|τ_i|$ in multi-step GRPO as the root cause of trajectory-level and token-level inefficiency: because failures are systematically longer than successes, it down-weights the negative gradient on failed tokens, so the policy keeps producing verbose memory schemas. Replacing $1/|τ_i|$ with a constant $1/k$ breaks this coupling, contracting trajectories while preserving aggregate success. Together, these contributions set a new open-source state of the art on the WebGym out-of-distribution test split (+5.8% relative over the 42.9% prior best), with the largest gains on the harder slices (+42% relative on Medium, +48% relative on Hard).

### [268] [Mitigating the Curse of Dimensionality in Uniform Convergence of Deep Neural Networks via Smooth Activations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05599)
*Yizhe Ding,Runze Li,Jia Liu,Lingzhou Xue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现 ReLU 神经网络在一致收敛性能上存在维度灾难，并提出利用平滑激活函数构建的 DNN 作为替代方案，证明了其能通过自适应利用函数结构优势，在多种回归任务中实现优于 ReLU 的一致收敛保障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然标准的 ReLU 神经网络在 $L^2(P)$ 范数下表现良好，但研究表明它们在处理一致收敛（uniform convergence）问题时容易受到“维度灾难”的影响，无法满足某些对最差情况可靠性（worst-case reliability）要求极高的下游任务需求。因此，研究需要寻求更稳健的替代模型。

Method: 本文分析了包含前馈和残差结构的平滑激活深度神经网络，推导了其伪维数（pseudo-dimension）界、非渐近逼近保证及 Hölder 范数界。在此基础上，作者为 Huber 回归、最小二乘回归、分位数回归和逻辑回归等多种统计背景推导了非渐近一致收敛速率。

Result: 理论研究证明，平滑激活神经网络通过自适应地利用目标函数的低维分层复合结构，成功减轻了一致收敛中的“维度灾难”；模拟研究和真实数据应用进一步验证了平滑 DNN 在需要一致性保障的统计学习任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论证明和实证分析，确立了平滑激活深度神经网络（Smooth DNNs）作为一类兼具理论保障与实践效果的估计器，能够有效克服 ReLU 网络在一致收敛性上的“维度灾难”问题，是实现高可靠性统计学习任务的理想选择。

Abstract: This paper establishes a theoretical framework for the uniform convergence of smoothly activated deep neural network (DNN) estimators. While standard ReLU networks achieve minimax-optimal rates in the $L^2(P)$ norm for various nonparametric regression tasks, we establish a theoretical lower bound demonstrating that least-squares ReLU estimators can suffer from the curse of dimensionality in their uniform convergence behavior. Motivated by the need for reliable uniform guarantees in downstream tasks requiring worst-case reliability, we address this limitation by analyzing smoothly activated DNNs (smooth DNNs), encompassing both feedforward and residual structures. We establish novel pseudo-dimension bounds, non-asymptotic approximation guarantees, and Hölder-norm bounds for the approximators of these models. Leveraging these results, we derive non-asymptotic uniform convergence rates for smooth DNN estimators across multiple statistical contexts, including Huber, least-squares, quantile, and logistic regression. We prove that smooth DNNs can mitigate the {curse of dimensionality} in uniform convergence by adaptively exploiting the low-dimensional hierarchical composition structure of the target function. Supported by both simulation studies and a real-world application, our results position smooth DNNs as a theoretically grounded and practically viable alternative to ReLU networks for statistical learning tasks requiring uniform guarantees.
