### [269] [From Prediction to Self: Developmental Conditions for Agency in Minimal Neural Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05605)
*Evan Ye*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过计算机模拟实验发现，自我感知的形成需满足特定的发育顺序，即先建立内部稳定性和因果反馈，再通过“代理增益”量化并区分自身行为与环境影响，打破了仅靠预测编码即可产生自我表征的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨纯粹的预测系统如何通过发育过程，从对世界的建模中区分出“自我”的因果影响，即自我意识（Self-awareness）与代理感（Agency）是如何从简单的预测行为中涌现出来的。

Method: 研究者利用一个192维的最小化GRU（门控循环单元）模型，通过设计40个受控实验构建发育序列。通过逐步添加组件，系统性地追踪模型如何区分“自身导致的变化”与“外部导致的变化”，并引入“代理增益”（Agency Gain）指标来评估模型的预测优势。此外，实验对比了不同的动作选择机制（如前向采样与基于梯度的方法），并验证了多种发育假设。

Result: 研究确定了实现自我区分的四个严格发育条件：稳定吸引子、因果循环、本体感受反馈以及感知学习先于动作学习的异步觉醒。实验证明，能够区分自身行为的预测器在周期性和混沌环境中均表现优于无法区分自身的预测器。同时，该研究揭示了单纯的预测编码无法产生自我表征，且只有前向采样能带来有效的代理增益。

Conclusion: 自我意识并非仅靠预测编码就能涌现。通过特定的发育路径（包括稳定吸引子、因果循环、本体感受反馈及异步觉醒），系统能够发展出区分自身行为与外部环境影响的能力。代理增益（Agency Gain）是量化这一过程的有效指标，且前向采样的动作选择机制对自我感知的形成至关重要。

Abstract: How does a system that merely predicts the world come to distinguish its own causal influence from everything else? We trace this transition in a minimal 192-dimensional GRU through 40 controlled experiments arranged as a developmental sequence, adding components one at a time and tracking whether the system can distinguish self-caused from world-caused changes.
  The developmental path reveals four conditions that must be satisfied in strict order: (1) persistent state forming stable attractors, (2) a causal action loop linking output to input, (3) proprioceptive feedback that makes implicit causal knowledge explicit, and (4) asynchronous awakening - perceptual learning must consolidate before action learning begins. We propose agency gain (A = Err_world - Err_self), the predictive advantage of knowing one's own action, as a metric to track this process. The self-aware predictor consistently outperforms the self-blind predictor across periodic (sinusoidal) and chaotic (Lorenz) environments, and the metric survives ablation of all auxiliary components. Only forward-sampled action selection produces meaningful agency gain; two gradient-based alternatives degenerate.
  Equally significant are 12 falsified hypotheses mapping where development stalls: predictive coding alone does not produce self-represent

</details>


### [270] [Cross-Epoch Adaptive Rollout Optimization for RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05606)
*Yiming Zong,Yige Wang,Jiashuo Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对 LLM 强化学习后训练中采样资源浪费的问题，提出了一种名为 CERO 的自适应采样分配算法，通过动态调整每个提示词的采样数量，显著提升了训练效率与模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）的强化学习后训练通常对所有提示词使用固定的采样数量，但不同提示词提供的训练信号质量差异巨大。为了在有限的全局计算预算下最大化学习效率，需要一种能够根据提示词难易度自适应分配采样资源的方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为 CERO（Computing-efficient Evaluation and Rollout Optimization）的自适应资源分配方法。该方法：1. 为每个提示词维护一个 Beta 后验分布，用期望伯努利方差来估计增加采样价值；2. 构建一个具有收益递减效应的凹效用函数；3. 将该问题转化为非时间可分的资源分配问题，并通过 Fenchel 对偶重构，利用投影在线梯度下降法（Online Gradient Descent）动态更新对偶变量以实现全局预算约束下的最优分配。

Result: 在数学推理任务上的实验表明，CERO 在多个开源 LLM 模型及基准测试中表现均优于传统的 GRPO 算法，且在理论上证明了其算法相对于离线分配基准具有 O(√K) 的遗憾界（regret bound），有效提升了样本利用效率。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 CERO 方法证明了在有限计算资源下，根据提示词（prompt）的难易程度动态分配采样数量（rollout）是一种比固定分配更优的策略。通过贝叶斯估计与在线梯度下降法的结合，CERO 不仅提升了模型训练的样本效率，还为强化学习在 LLM 后训练中的资源分配问题提供了一个稳健的理论框架。

Abstract: LLM post-training often relies on reinforcement learning methods that sample multiple rollouts per prompt, yet most existing approaches use a fixed rollout budget for every prompt, despite large differences in the training signal different prompts provide. In this paper, we study adaptive rollout allocation under a fixed global budget and formulate the problem as online resource allocation with prompt-level diminishing returns. Our method, CERO, maintains a Beta posterior over each prompt's success probability and uses the posterior expected Bernoulli variance as a Bayesian estimate of the value of additional rollouts. We use this estimate to construct a concave, saturating utility over cumulative allocations, yielding an objective in which decisions across prompts and epochs are coupled by the global budget. Since the resulting objective is temporally nonseparable, we derive a Fenchel-dual reformulation and update both prompt-level and budget-level dual variables via projected online gradient descent. Under fixed prompt utilities, we prove an $O(\sqrt{K})$ regret bound against the offline allocation benchmark. Experiments on mathematical-reasoning problems show that CERO consistently outperforms GRPO across multiple open-weight LLMs and benchmarks, demonstrating that adaptive rollout budgeting can improve sample efficiency.

### [271] [StableRCA: Robust Graph-Agnostic Mechanism-Level Root Cause Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05636)
*Xiaoyu Lin,Nicholas Tagliapietra,Kehan Li,Lavdim Halilaj,Juergen Luettin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的根本原因分析（RCA）方法存在局限性：基于图的方法依赖于已知或精确估计的因果图，而无需图的方法要么只能定位边缘异常，要么对图结构或函数形式有严格限制。因此，需要一种能够避开全局图发现且在复杂系统中依然有效的 RCA 方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 StableRCA 的局部机制级 RCA 框架。该方法避开了复杂的全局因果图发现过程，转而通过估计局部马尔可夫边界并检测其中的条件分布偏移来识别干预目标。该方法基于“独立因果机制”原则，在样本量增大时具有指数级的收敛性。

Result: 实验结果表明，StableRCA 在合成基准测试和五个真实世界数据集上表现出色，不仅对图错误指定具有鲁棒性，能够有效识别多重干预目标，而且具有良好的可扩展性和跨领域的可靠性。

Conclusion: StableRCA 为复杂系统中的根本原因分析（RCA）提供了一种稳健、可扩展且无需全局因果图的解决方案。通过利用局部马尔可夫边界和独立因果机制原则，该方法在处理多重干预目标时表现出优越的性能和可靠性。

Abstract: Root-Cause Analysis (RCA) seeks to identify the variables responsible for abnormal system behavior in complex domains such as manufacturing, cloud computing, and healthcare. Existing approaches face a critical bottleneck: graph-based causal methods can identify intervention targets but typically require a known or accurately estimated causal graph, while graph-free statistical methods either localize marginal anomalies rather than structural causes, or rely on restrictive assumptions about graph structure or functional form. We propose StableRCA, a local mechanism-level RCA framework that avoids global graph discovery by estimating local Markov boundaries and detecting conditional distribution shifts within them. Leveraging the Independent Causal Mechanism principle, we show that intervention targets can be identified with probability converging exponentially in sample size under faithful Markov boundary recovery and non-degenerate mechanism shifts. Experiments on synthetic benchmarks and five real-world datasets demonstrate that StableRCA is robust to graph misspecification, effective under multiple intervention targets, scalable to large systems, and reliable across diverse application domains. Code is available at: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/StableRCA-E362

To this end, we incorporate query entity information into the reasoning process from two perspectives: the first is structural context, i.e., the neighboring structure and relation patterns around the entity, which is encoded by a dedicated context encoder and used to modulate messages; the second is semantic type of the entity, inferred by a large language model, which is incorporated into attention computation and final scoring to provide type-level prior constraints. ### [273] [Two-Way Is Better Than One: Bidirectional Alignment with Cycle Consistency for Exemplar-Free Class-Incremental Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05675)
*Hongye Xu,Bartosz Krawczyk*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的无样本类增量学习（EFCIL）方法中，基于原型的投影补偿方案通常采用单向投影，这会导致系统性偏差，破坏当前的特征几何结构或产生局部对齐问题，从而引发跨任务累积的循环不一致性，加剧灾难性遗忘。

Method: 提出了一种名为 BiCyc 的双向投影对齐方法，包含从旧到新和从新到旧的两个映射，并结合循环一致性目标函数，利用停止梯度门控机制实现表征的协同演化。该方法通过损失函数将白化空间中的奇异谱收缩至单位矩阵附近，从而保持类均值和协方差的稳定性。

Conclusion: BiCyc 通过双向投影对齐和循环一致性约束，有效解决了原型法在无样本类增量学习中因表征漂移导致的灾难性遗忘问题，在标准基准测试中展现出卓越的性能。

Abstract: Continual learning (CL) seeks models that acquire new skills without erasing prior knowledge. In exemplar-free class-incremental learning (EFCIL), this challenge is amplified because past data cannot be stored, making representation drift for old classes particularly harmful. Prototype-based EFCIL is attractive for its efficiency, yet prototypes drift as the embedding space evolves; therefore, projection-based drift compensation has become a popular remedy. We show, however, that existing one-directional projections introduce systematic bias: they either retroactively distort the current feature geometry or align past classes only locally, leaving cycle inconsistencies that accumulate across tasks. We introduce BiCyc, a bidirectional projector alignment approach with a cycle-consistency objective. BiCyc jointly optimizes two maps, old-to-new and new-to-old, with stop-gradient gating so that transport and representation co-evolve. Analytically, we show that the cycle loss contracts the singular spectrum toward unity in whitened space, and that improved transport of class means and covariances yields smaller perturbations of classification log-odds, preserving old-class decisions and mitigating catastrophic forgetting. Empirically, across standard EFCIL benchmarks, BiCyc substantially reduces forgetting and improves accuracy in from-scratch settings, while remaining competitive in the pretrained fine-grained regime.

Method: 作者提出了一种专门刻画演化选择的新型图模型，并开发了一套针对该模型的因果发现程序。该程序能够从单一或多个环境/代际的数据中，完整且准确地识别出潜在的因果机制。

Abstract: Understanding potential selection in data is crucial for causal discovery; we argue that "selection" in common narratives takes two forms, which we term static and evolutionary selection, respectively. Static selection refers to a one-shot filtering process where observed data consist of a subset of the population of interest, as in survey volunteer bias. Evolutionary selection, in contrast, operates through repeated rounds of differential fitness in reproduction, where observed data constitute the latest generation shaped by a historical trajectory, as in immune adaptation, antibiotic resistance, and social norm emergence. Existing methods largely conflate these two forms and rely on an identical graphical model of selection. We show that this model is valid for static settings but fails to characterize data under evolution, yielding false discovery results. To address this, we introduce a new model that specifically characterizes evolutionary selection, and develop a sound and complete procedure for identifying such models from data across one or multiple environments or generations. Experimental results validate the method's ability to uncover the relevant mechanisms underlying evolution from data.

### [276] [Revisiting Prototype Rehearsal for Exemplar-Free Continual Learning: Manifold-Aware Boundary Sampling with Adaptive Class-Balanced Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05695)
*Hongye Xu,Bartosz Krawczyk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过改进原型重演机制，利用流形感知采样和自适应类平衡损失，解决了传统EFCIL方法中类边界模糊和严重不平衡的问题，从而使原型重演法重新成为一种高效且具备竞争力的解决策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的EFCIL研究中，漂移补偿方法在性能上持续优于传统的原型重演法，导致人们质疑原型重演法的局限性。作者认为，这种性能差距并非源于重演这一策略本身，而是源于传统实现方式中忽略了类间边界信息及严重的类不平衡问题。因此，作者旨在通过改进原型重演机制来弥合这一差距。

Method: 1. 提出约束性扩张过采样（Constrained Expansive Over-Sampling）：通过将旧类原型向新类中的最近邻“敌对”特征进行插值，生成边界感知的重演样本，从而更好地拟合数据流形并保持类间可分性。
2. 设计自适应类平衡损失（Adaptive Class-Balanced loss）：引入基于时间的类加权机制，根据任务进程动态调整对旧类原型的梯度关注度，平衡新旧任务间的监督信息。

Result: 该方法在多个EFCIL基准测试上均实现了最先进（SOTA）的性能。实验结果表明，通过流形感知和类平衡优化，原型重演机制能够有效地抵御漂移并处理类不平衡，其效果不仅闭合了与漂移补偿方法之间的性能鸿沟，在多种场景下甚至表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了原型重演法在无样本类增量学习（EFCIL）中依然具备强大的潜力。通过引入流形感知策略来解决边界信息缺失和类别不平衡问题，研究成功克服了重演法的固有缺陷，使其性能达到甚至超过了现有的漂移补偿方法。

Abstract: Exemplar-free class-incremental learning (EFCIL) aims to acquire new classes over time without storing raw data. Historically, prototype rehearsal, which samples around stored class prototypes and mixes them with current-task data, has been a popular strategy to reduce catastrophic forgetting. However, recent drift-compensation methods that explicitly realign prototypes in the evolving feature space consistently outperform prototype-based rehearsal, raising the question of whether rehearsal itself is fundamentally limited. We argue that the performance gap stems not from the idea of prototype rehearsal per se, but from how it is typically instantiated: existing approaches treat prototypes as isolated class summaries that ignore information from nearby enemy classes, and fail to correct the emerging class imbalance between a handful of synthetic old-class samples and hundreds of real instances from newly introduced classes. Building on this hypothesis, we revisit prototype rehearsal and propose a manifold-aware variant that restores its competitiveness in EFCIL. First, we introduce Constrained Expansive Over-Sampling, which interpolates each old-class prototype toward its nearest enemy features from new classes, generating boundary-aware rehearsal samples that better follow the underlying data manifold while preserving inter-class separation. Second, we design an Adaptive Class-Balanced loss that performs time-based class weighting, amplifying gradients from older prototypes when they are most informative and gradually annealing their influence as richer supervision from later tasks accumulates. Together, these components turn prototype rehearsal into a drift-resilient, imbalance-aware mechanism that closes, and often reverses, the gap to recent drift-compensation methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance across multiple EFCIL benchmarks.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有作物分类产品（如USDA CDL）通常在收获后才发布，滞后性强，无法满足应对极端气候威胁时的实时决策需求。此外，缺乏针对不同机器学习算法在处理年际变异性时优劣的系统性评估。

Method: 研究利用归一化Landsat-Sentinel表面反射率时间序列数据，结合作物轮作历史信息，对十种机器学习算法进行了比较。采用了基于年际交叉验证（year-wise cross-validation）的方法，并进行了广泛的超参数搜索，以量化物候和作物分布带来的不确定性。

Result: 在6月初（收获前）的预测任务中，支持向量机（SVM）表现最优。在加州杏仁和爱荷华州玉米的未见年份验证中，平均F1分数分别达到0.74和0.59。研究量化了年际变异作为不确定性的主要来源，并证明了该方法在提前预判作物类型方面的可行性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了结合多源遥感影像与作物轮作历史，能够在收获前实现作物类型的精确预测。尽管存在跨年度的性能波动，但支持向量机（SVM）在提前识别作物方面表现出稳健性。该方法为农业监测提供了关键工具，未来可通过集成学习及多源数据扩展至全国范围及产量预测。

Abstract: In-season crop type mapping is critical for food security in the face of increasingly extreme climate-related threats to crops. Currently, the USDA Cropland Data Layer provides crop type labels at 30m resolution and is available the February after harvest, but no product exists that maps crop types before harvest with satisfactory accuracy that would allow emergency managers to respond to crop threats in near real time. Furthermore, the relative advantages of a wide range of algorithms have not been evaluated in a way that accounts for interannual variability, until this study. Here, Harmonized Landsat-Sentinel surface reflectance imagery time series and crop rotation history information are combined to map corn in Iowa and almonds in California at 30m resolution accurately by early June in unseen years, with robust quantification of uncertainty due to phenology and crop distribution. Thousands of model configurations across ten machine learning algorithms were compared using a year-wise cross-validation and a suite of metrics. Hyperparameter search revealed Support Vector Machines to be the most successful algorithm overall, with a mean F1 score of 0.74 (0.59) across five unseen validation years for almonds by early June in California (corn by early June in Iowa). Interannual variation was a large source of uncertainty, but patterns showed the potential to further improve performance with ensemble approaches or ancillary data. Future work may extend these methods to include multiclass maps of all crop types, CONUS-wide maps, and in-season crop yield forecasting.

### [278] [Zero-Copy Semantic Contagion: An In-Memory Streaming Architecture for Evolving Attention Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05733)
*Kabir Murjani*

Method: 提出了一种异构Rust-Python流式架构。前端采用Rust实现零拷贝解析，以纳秒级速度处理新闻和扫描股票；后端采用多变量神经霍克斯过程（Neural Hawkes Process），结合每个节点的连续时间LSTM状态和双线性潜在投影来传播定向影响，并利用自适应剪枝规则控制计算开销。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了跨公司动态注意力机制对于捕捉金融市场中非线性、跨资产的关联性至关重要。通过构建基于文本驱动的连续时间图模型，系统能够成功识别并利用传统的单资产预测模型所忽略的突发事件连锁反应，从而提升金融预测的准确性。

Abstract: Per-ticker forecasting models dominate financial time-series work yet remain blind to cross-company propagation: a foundry disruption in Taiwan does not register in a single-asset model until Apple's own price has already moved. To address this limitation, we introduce a heterogeneous Rust-Python streaming architecture that maps cross-company attention as a continuous-time graph driven directly from text. We show that on the ingestion side, a zero-copy Rust edge parses news records in $\sim$100 ns and scans the target equity universe in $\sim$1.2 $μ$s. On the inference end, a multivariate Neural Hawkes Process featuring per-node continuous-time LSTM states and a bilinear latent projection propagates directed excitation, while an adaptive pruning rule bounds the computational cost of dynamic neighborhood updates. Combining these stages, we demonstrate an end-to-end processing latency of $\sim$13 ms per incoming news record on a single commodity CPU. Evaluated on a one-month temporal holdout of the FNSPID corpus (638 articles across 47 tickers), the system delivers a $1.70\times$ precision lift over random at the 90th-percentile next-day return threshold, and $3.36\times$ over a same-sector baseline. Crucially, removing the graph topology collapses precision to zero, confirming that the dynamic attention network is the sole driver of cross-company signal in this architecture.

### [279] [Beyond Soft Masks: Hard-Perturbation Mixup Explainer for Robust GNN Explainability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05756)
*Jialiang Yin,Zheng Zhao,Linsey Pang,Bo Dong,Bin Shi,Jiaxing Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有图神经网络解释方法因软掩码噪声导致解释保真度不足和分布外问题，本文提出了 HPME 框架，通过图信息瓶颈引导的离散子图提取和结构级混合策略，实现了更精准、鲁棒的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 GNN 后验解释方法多依赖软掩码（soft masks），无法完全剔除与标签无关的冗余信息，导致在混合训练过程中引入噪声，从而引发分布外（OOD）问题并降低了解释的保真度。因此，需要一种能够更彻底剔除无关信息并解决分布偏移问题的解释框架。

Method: 提出了 HPME（Hard-Perturbation Mixup Explanation）框架：1. 利用图池化技术提取离散的解释性子图（硬掩码），以彻底滤除与标签无关的噪声；2. 结合广义图信息瓶颈（GIB）理论来优化子图的信息压缩；3. 引入基于结构级替换（structure-level replacement）的混合（mixup）策略，通过生成分布内（in-distribution）的解释样本，有效缓解了分布偏移问题。

Result: 在多个合成数据集和真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，HPME 在生成鲁棒且具有高保真度的解释方面达到了当前最优（SOTA）水平，显著优于现有的基准模型。

Conclusion: HPME 通过基于图信息瓶颈的离散子图提取和结构级替换混合策略，成功解决了现有解释方法在处理带噪子图和分布外问题上的局限性，为图神经网络提供了更具可信度和鲁棒性的解释方案。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) have demonstrated remarkable performance across a range of applications involving graph-structured data, particularly in high-stakes domains. However, the opaque nature of their decision-making processes limits their trustworthiness and broader adoption. Existing post-hoc explanation methods aim to improve explainability by identifying subgraphs that influence GNN predictions and adopt mixup strategies to alleviate the out-of-distribution (OOD) issue caused by using subgraphs for prediction. Yet, these approaches typically rely on soft masks, which are inherently unable to fully eliminate label-irrelevant information, allowing redundant structures to leak into the mixup process and hindering the resolution of the OOD problem, thereby degrading explanation fidelity. In this work, we propose HPME, a Hard-Perturbation Mixup Explanation framework grounded in a generalized Graph Information Bottleneck, which leverages graph pooling to extract discrete explanatory subgraphs and to yield an information-capacity bound to thoroughly compress label-irrelevant components. Furthermore, we introduce a novel mixup strategy built upon structure-level replacement, generating in-distribution explanations to effectively mitigate the distribution shift. Extensive experiments on diverse tasks demonstrate that HPME achieves state-of-the-art performance in generating robust and interpretable explanations across both synthetic and real-world datasets.

Abstract: Longitudinal treatment decisions require predicting potential outcomes under future treatment sequences in the presence of time-varying confounding, heterogeneous patient dynamics, and limited domain-specific data. Existing longitudinal causal estimators typically train a new model for each cohort or simulator. We introduce Causal Longitudinal Prior-Fitted Networks (CausalLongPFN), a prior-fitted in-context predictor for longitudinal causal prediction. The model is pretrained entirely on synthetic episodes sampled from a broad prior over temporal structural causal models, exposing it to treatment-confounder feedback, latent heterogeneity, nonlinear state evolution, delayed effects, and cumulative treatment responses. At test time, CausalLongPFN is frozen: it conditions on support trajectories, a query history, and a proposed future treatment sequence, and returns a predictive distribution over future outcomes without gradient updates or propensity-model fitting. Multi-step predictions are obtained by recursively applying the one-step predictor under the specified treatment sequence. We evaluate on branchable cancer, HIV, and warfarin benchmarks with ground-truth counterfactual labels, and on factual-only rolling-origin prediction in MIMIC-III ICU trajectories. CausalLongPFN is competitive with domain-trained longitudinal baselines on counterfactual benchmarks and performs strongly on factual MIMIC-III prediction, suggesting that broad synthetic causal pretraining can provide a useful frozen alternative when repeated domain-specific training is costly or impractical.

### [282] [CaliDist: Calibrating Large Language Models via Behavioral Robustness to Distraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05799)
*Mohammad Anas Jawad,Cornelia Caragea*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型易受无关信息干扰的问题，研究提出 \textsc{CaliDist} 方法，通过量化模型对干扰项的行为鲁棒性来校准置信度，显著提升了模型预测的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的校准方法多关注预测准确性，忽略了模型在面对无关或误导性信息时的“行为鲁棒性”。作者认为，一个模型真正的置信度应当反映其在认知压力下保持稳定预测的能力。

Method: 提出了 \textsc{CaliDist} 后置校准方法。该方法首先通过在输入提示词中引入语义“干扰项”（distractors）来检测大模型的预测和置信度变化，量化其对无关或误导性信息的敏感度，随后利用这种行为稳定性（或波动性）信号，自适应地调整模型原始的置信度评分。

Result: 在7个自然语言理解分类基准和6种不同大模型上的实验表明，\textsc{CaliDist} 显著降低了预期校准误差（ECE）和 Brier 分数。平均而言，该方法将 ECE 从 23% 降至 7%，实现了约 70% 的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了“行为鲁棒性”是衡量大语言模型可信度的一个关键且被忽视的维度。通过将稳定性信号引入校准流程，可以显著提升模型在处理复杂指令时的不确定性估计准确性，从而实现更可靠的置信度输出。

Abstract: Existing calibration methods for Large Language Models (LLMs) often overlook a critical dimension of trustworthiness: a model's {\em behavioral robustness} to irrelevant or misleading information. In this paper, we argue that a model's true confidence should reflect its stability under cognitive pressure. We introduce \textsc{CaliDist}, a novel post-hoc calibration approach that directly measures and penalizes a model's susceptibility to distraction. \textsc{CaliDist} quantifies how an LLM's predictions and uncertainty change when its input prompt is perturbed with semantic \textit{distractors}. This stability (or lack thereof) signal is then used to adaptively scale the model's initial confidence score. Our extensive experiments on seven Natural Language Understanding classification benchmarks using six distinct LLMs show that \textsc{CaliDist} consistently achieves lower Expected Calibration Error (ECE) and Brier Score compared with strong baselines. Remarkably, our method reduces the ECE from 23\% to 7\% on average--a relative improvement of 70\%--demonstrating that behavioral stability is a powerful signal for calibration. We make our code and datasets available at github.com/m-anas-j/CaliDist.

### [283] [SALT: When More Rollouts Don't Help in Group-Based Policy Optimization and How to Make Them Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05800)
*Powei Chang,Jinpeng Zhang,Chaoqun Sun,MiniWell Tsao,Lianrui Li,Jianxiang Xiang,Chenyu Wang,Yukang Gao,Dongying Kong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 GRPO 强化学习中采样增加导致梯度抵消的问题，本文提出了 SALT 插件，通过自适应调整梯度几何结构来放大有效更新信号，在不增加额外训练开销的前提下显著提升了模型推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究发现，在使用 GRPO 进行强化学习训练时，单纯增加采样数并不总能提升性能。这是因为在组归一化过程中，策略梯度的特征会集中在一个低秩、带有符号的几何空间中，导致在聚合时发生严重的梯度抵消，削弱了模型的有效学习。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SALT（子空间自适应几何插件）的方法。该方法通过分析小批量样本的梯度几何结构（Gram 矩阵），估计出一个主导的共享子空间，将组相对更新的系数分解为共享通道和残差通道，并根据样本间的符号抵消程度自适应地放大残差分量，从而提升更新效率。

Result: 在多个推理导向的 RLVR 基准测试中，无论模型规模如何，SALT 均在无需修改奖励模型或采样过程的情况下，改善了梯度更新的几何结构，显著提升了模型性能。

Conclusion: SALT 通过优化组相对更新的几何结构，有效解决了 GRPO 在大规模采样中存在的梯度抵消问题，为强化学习在推理任务中的训练提供了一种高效、即插即用的改进方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) often adopts GRPO-style group-relative updates, sampling multiple rollouts per prompt to construct normalized learning signals. However, merely increasing the number of rollouts does not reliably strengthen learning: under GRPO-style group normalization, per-rollout policy-gradient features can concentrate into a low-rank, signed geometry, causing substantial cancellation during aggregation and weakening the effective update. We address this failure mode with SALT, a Subspace-Adaptive geometry pLug-in componenT that uses sample-wise gradient geometry to reweight the coefficients of group-relative updates. SALT estimates a dominant shared subspace from the mini-batch Gram geometry, decomposes group-relative coefficients into shared and residual channels, and adaptively amplifies the residual channel when signed cancellation is severe. Across diverse reasoning-oriented RLVR benchmarks and model scales, SALT improves effective update geometry and performance without modifying the reward model or the rollout sampling procedure

</details>


### [284] [Robust and sparse support vector machine via hybrid truncated loss for supervised classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05814)
*Yuliang Yang,Chen Chen,Yuxiang Liu,Huiru Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型混合截断损失函数Lht及其SVM模型，有效解决了传统SVM在处理噪声时的敏感性与计算复杂度之间的矛盾，并在单视图和多视图分类任务中表现出优异的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的支持向量机（SVM）模型存在缺陷：凸损失函数（如铰链损失）对异常值敏感，而有界非凸损失函数通常计算成本过高。因此，作者旨在设计一种既能保持稀疏性又能有效处理噪声，同时具备高计算效率的损失函数。

Method: 1. 提出一种新型的混合截断损失函数（Lht），兼具稀疏性与有界性。
2. 定义P-驻点（P-stationary point）以推导一阶最优性条件。
3. 设计基于交替方向乘子法（ADMM）及工作集策略的优化算法，确保全局收敛。
4. 引入结构信息与视图权重，将模型扩展为多视图学习框架（MvLht-SVM），遵循共识与互补原则。

Result: 实验结果表明，Lht-SVM在单视图任务中比对比方法拥有更高的准确率、更少的支持向量以及更强的抗噪能力；MvLht-SVM在多视图任务中，在准确率、精确率、召回率和F1值方面均优于现有的六种多视图学习方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的混合截断损失函数（Lht）有效地平衡了计算效率、稀疏性和噪声鲁棒性。Lht-SVM及其多视图扩展MvLht-SVM在保持高性能的同时，通过P-驻点理论和工作集策略实现了理论上的完备性和计算上的高效性。

Abstract: The support vector machine (SVM) is a widely used classifier, but choosing an appropriate loss function remains difficult. Convex losses such as the hinge loss and least-squares loss are sensitive to outliers, while bounded non-convex losses often lead to high computational cost. To address this, we propose a hybrid truncated loss function ($L_{\mathrm{ht}}$) that is both sparse and bounded, and build the $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM model for single-view classification. We introduce the P-stationary point and use it to establish the first-order necessary and sufficient optimality conditions. Based on these conditions, we design an alternating direction method of multipliers with a working-set strategy that reduces computational cost and achieves global convergence. We further extend $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM to multi-view learning by adding structural information and view weights, resulting in Mv$L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM, which follows both the consensus and complementarity principles. Experiments on synthetic, real-world, and image datasets show that $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM achieves higher accuracy with fewer support vectors and better noise robustness than five single-view methods, while Mv$L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM outperforms six multi-view methods in accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score.

</details>


### [285] [Consistency Training Along the Transformer Stack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05817)
*Sukrati Gautam,Neil Shah,Arav Dhoot,Bryan Maruyama,Caroline Wei,Rohan Kapoor,Robert Sidey,Prakhar Gupta,Zi Cheng Huang,David Demitri Africa*

Conclusion: 一致性训练是一个灵活且可扩展的对齐框架，能够统一应对多种模型病态行为。研究揭示了不同一致性目标（ACT, MLPCT, AttCT）共享底层的残差流机制，为构建更稳健的对齐方法提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Consistency training encourages models to behave similarly across different contexts, and has shown promise for reducing misalignment. We broaden the scope of consistency training in two ways. First, we introduce two new internal consistency targets: MLP Consistency Training (MLPCT), which matches post-activation MLP states, and Attention Consistency Training (AttCT), which matches per-head attention distributions. Second, we apply consistency training to four additional safety threats: persona in-context learning attacks, adversarial frustration, prefill attacks, and conditional misalignment. Across several models and threat settings, we find that consistency training reduces misalignment well beyond the sycophancy and jailbreak settings studied in prior work. We also find cases of cross-threat generalization, where training against one failure mode improves robustness to another, and identify a shared residual-stream mechanism underlying ACT, MLPCT, and AttCT, while distinguishing BCT as mechanistically distinct. Our results suggest that consistency training is a flexible and extensible framework for alignment, capable of unifying defenses against a broader class of model pathologies.

We present GenAutoML, an agentic framework that leverages Large Language Models (LLMs) as neural architects to bridge natural-language requirements and executable PyTorch implementations. Experiments on the ETTh1, ETTm1, and Weather benchmarks demonstrate that GenAutoML can dynamically generate task-specific neural architectures tailored to dataset characteristics. Among the generated models, WaveInterferenceNet achieves inference latency below 0.01 ms per sample while maintaining competitive predictive performance. ### [287] [Deciphering Two Training Clocks in Grokking via Deep Linear Network Theory with Conditional ReLU Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05863)
*Hu Tan,Kuo Gai,Shihua Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“双训练时钟”理论，通过数学建模证明了神经网络在训练过程中存在“先拟合、后简化”的动力学差异，成功解释了Grokking现象中测试准确率延迟提升的深层机理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Grokking现象表现为模型在训练误差趋近于零后，经过漫长的训练周期，测试准确率才从随机水平突变至完美泛化。本文旨在从数学上解析这一现象背后的训练动力学，解释拟合数据与学习潜在简单规则为何发生在不同的时间尺度上。

Method: 1. 形式化定义“双训练时钟”，将分类损失的衰减与表征简化的过程分离；2. 在深度线性网络中，利用后边缘间隙增长（post-margin gap-growth）和Schatten类正则化分析损失与结构能量的收敛速度；3. 将该机制扩展至ReLU多层感知机（MLP），通过分析激活模式固定的区域，并利用链式法则估计分类头与嵌入层梯度幅值的差异，论证了拟合与表征简化阶段的先后顺序。

Result: 研究发现，对于深度线性网络，分类损失在对数时间尺度上趋于收敛，而受权重衰减影响的表征结构能量在多项式时间尺度上收敛。对于ReLU MLP，分类头在特定条件下比嵌入块获得更大的有效梯度，从而导致模型先快速拟合数据，随后通过较长的表征简化过程实现泛化。实验以模运算（modular addition）作为主要验证场景。

Conclusion: 本文通过提出“双训练时钟”理论，从动力学层面量化解释了Grokking现象：即训练过程中损失的快速下降（拟合阶段）与随后表征的缓慢简化（泛化阶段）存在明显的时间尺度差异。该模型为深度神经网络在极度过参数化条件下的泛化行为提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Grokking suggests that fitting the training data and learning a simple underlying rule may occur on different time scales. We formalize this phenomenon by separating the fast decay of the classification loss from the slower simplification of the learned representation, and we call the resulting pair of stopping times two training clocks. For deep linear networks, we show that a post-margin gap-growth or one-step tail-contraction condition reduces the cross-entropy loss to level epsilon on a logarithmic time scale. In contrast, when layerwise weight decay is present, the induced regularization on the end-to-end map can be expressed as a Schatten-type penalty; under a sharp late-time Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz tail, this structural energy closes on a polynomial time scale. The two clocks, therefore, separate fitting from representation simplification. We then explain how the same mechanism can appear in ReLU MLPs. In regions where the activation patterns on the training set remain fixed, the network reduces to a linear model in the active coordinates. In a two-layer ReLU embedding model, chain-rule estimates further show that the classifier head can receive larger effective gradients than the embedding block under controlled downstream norms. This supports a two-stage mechanism in which the classifier fits first, while the representation continues to simplify later. We use modular addition as the main experimental setting. The deep linear theory provides the rigorous core of the analysis. But the ReLU results are formulated as conditional reductions that account for empirical behavior without claiming a global proof for nonlinear training dynamics.

</details>


### [288] [TS-ICL: A Flexible Time-Indexed Foundation Model for Time Series via In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05878)
*Etienne Le Naour,Tahar Nabil,Adrien Petralia*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 TS-ICL 模型，这是一种基于概率的“上下文学习（In-Context Learning）”编码器-回归器 Transformer 架构。该方法将时序任务形式化为时间戳对齐的回归问题，并通过引入一种新的因果数据先验（causal data prior）来生成合成依赖结构，从而实现对协变量和不规则数据的统一处理。

Conclusion: TS-ICL 通过统一时序预测与缺失值填补任务，并利用因果数据先验进行训练，成功构建了一个具备强泛化能力的通用时序基础模型，为处理复杂、不规则观测的时序数据提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Foundation models mark a profound paradigm shift in time series modeling, with task-specific models being superseded by general-purpose zero-shot models. Yet, current approaches primarily focus on forecasting, while real-world time series are often irregularly and partially observed, requiring models that can jointly forecast, impute missing values, and handle degraded sampling conditions. To address these challenges, we introduce TS-ICL, a novel probabilistic In-Context Learning encoder--regressor Transformer that unifies forecasting and imputation. TS-ICL formulates time series tasks as timestamp-aligned regression and naturally incorporates covariates by training on synthetic dependency structures generated from a novel causal data prior. Empirically, TS-ICL achieves a new state-of-the-art in imputation, while remaining competitive with leading forecasting foundation models across both univariate and covariate-aware benchmarks. It shows particularly strong performance in forecasting with partially observed look-back windows.

### [289] [When Denser Credit Is Not Enough: Evidence-Calibrated Policy Optimization for Long-Horizon LLM Agent Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05885)
*Yuanfan Li,Qi Zhou,Wenjing Duan,Lu Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了证据校准策略优化（ECPO）算法，通过对步骤级信用进行校准和去噪，有效解决了长跨度智能体在强化学习中因统计偏差导致的训练不稳定问题，实现了性能和效率的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长跨度大语言模型智能体在稀疏和延迟奖励下进行强化学习时，现有的基于分组的信用分配方法（如 GiGPO）在有限样本下容易产生统计上的不可靠性，即偶然发生的“幸运动作”会获得过大的优势估计，从而引发锚定偏差和后期训练震荡。

Method: ECPO 引入了两项核心机制：1. 证据校准动作优势（Evidence-Calibrated Action Advantage）：通过按规范动作对轨迹进行分组，并对低样本量的估计值进行收缩处理，以减少偶发性“幸运动作”带来的偏差；2. 方差门控信用加权（Variance-Gated Credit Weighting）：通过抑制由动作内噪声主导的锚定状态，降低由于统计不可靠导致的训练震荡。

Result: 在 ALFWorld 和 WebShop 基准测试中，使用 Qwen2.5-1.5B/7B 模型进行实验，ECPO 表现出持续且显著的优越性。以 Qwen2.5-1.5B 为例，ECPO 相比 GiGPO 在 ALFWorld 上提升了 5.2 个成功点，在 WebShop 上提升了 7.3 个成功点，且计算开销仅增加了 0.1%。

Conclusion: ECPO 是一种无需 Critic 的高效策略优化算法，通过证据校准动作优势和方差门控信用加权，解决了长跨度智能体在稀疏奖励下因不稳定的步骤级信用分配而导致的训练发散问题，在复杂任务中实现了稳健的性能提升。

Abstract: Long-horizon LLM agents require reinforcement learning methods that can assign credit to intermediate decisions under sparse and delayed rewards. Recent group-based methods such as GiGPO improve over GRPO by constructing step-level advantages at repeated anchor states. However, we show that such dense credit can be statistically unreliable: under limited rollouts, rare but lucky actions may receive overly large advantages, producing divergent anchor bias and late-stage training oscillation. We propose Evidence-Calibrated Policy Optimization (ECPO), a critic-free policy optimization algorithm that calibrates step-level credit before policy updates. ECPO combines Evidence-Calibrated Action Advantage, which groups rollouts by canonical actions and shrinks low-count estimates, with Variance-Gated Credit Weighting, which suppresses anchor states dominated by within-action noise. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop with Qwen2.5-1.5B/7B show that ECPO consistently outperforms strong baselines, improving GiGPO by +5.2/+7.3 success points on ALFWorld/WebShop with Qwen2.5-1.5B while adding only 0.1% additional advantage-computation overhead.

</details>


### [290] [High-Dimensional Theory of LoRA Fine-Tuning in a Solvable Attention Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05899)
*O. Duranthon,F. Boncoraglio,L. Zdeborová*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LoRA应用缺乏系统的统计理论支持，研究者希望通过构建高维统计理论，理解预训练与微调之间的相互作用机制，并为优化LoRA微调过程提供理论指导。

Method: 建立了一个可解的单头注意力层理论框架，分析预训练与秩一（rank-one）LoRA更新的过程。在超高维极限下，通过一组有限的阶参数（order parameters）对这两个阶段进行精确的渐近表征，从而获得关于测试误差和表征对齐的明确预测。

Result: 理论推导出了测试误差和表征对齐的渐近表达式，量化了预训练对LoRA微调的影响，识别出了测试误差与表征质量不匹配的特定机制，并为基于此理论的主动微调提供了实用建议。

Conclusion: 该理论框架揭示了预训练与微调之间复杂的相互作用。预训练对LoRA的影响可概括为一个有效的噪声项，基于此可以导出最优预训练过程的准则。此外，研究还发现了测试误差与表征质量不一致的现象，并将其应用于主动微调策略中。

Abstract: We develop a high-dimensional statistical theory of low-rank adaptation (LoRA) in attention models, capturing the interplay between pre-training and fine-tuning. We introduce a solvable framework in which a single-head attention layer is first pre-trained on a data-abundant task and subsequently adapted via a rank-one LoRA update on limited data. In the high-dimensional limit, both stages admit a sharp asymptotic characterization in terms of a finite set of order parameters, yielding explicit predictions for test errors and representation alignment. Our analysis shows that the impact of pre-training on LoRA is summarized by an effective noise term, from which we derive prescriptions for the optimal pre-training procedure. We also demonstrate a regime with a mismatch between the value of the test error and representation quality, and propose an application of our theory to active fine-tuning.

### [291] [Addressing Imbalance in Multi-Label Data via Label-Specific Distance-based Oversampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05927)
*Bin Liu,Jun Wu,Haoyu Peng,Ao Zhou,Jin Wang,QiaoSong Chen,Grigorios Tsoumakas*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多标签过采样方法大多基于全局欧几里得距离，忽视了不同特征对不同标签的语义相关性差异，导致合成样本出现标签不一致、标签混淆以及模型过拟合等问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为LSDMLO（基于标签特定距离的多标签过采样）的新方法。该方法通过在加权的标签相关特征空间中计算“标签特定距离”来识别标签一致的邻居，从而在决策边界区域选择更具代表性的种子样本，并生成与原始标签分布一致的合成样本。

Result: 实验结果表明，LSDMLO方法在处理多标签数据不平衡问题时，相比现有主流的多标签采样方法取得了更好的分类性能，并能有效提升不同基分类器的预测效果。

Conclusion: LSDMLO通过引入标签特定距离度量，有效解决了多标签分类中数据不平衡和合成样本标签冲突的问题，在多种基分类器上表现优于现有主流采样算法，证明了该方法的有效性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: The complex imbalanced label distribution poses a crucial challenge to multi-label classification, as most classifiers are biased towards the majority class and high-frequent labels. Oversampling is an efficient and flexible solution that augments instances to provide a more balanced training dataset for multi-label classifiers. Most existing oversampling methods create synthetic instances in a heuristic way that essentially relies on neighborhood information retrieved using Euclidean distance within the entire feature space. However, they fail to consider the varying semantic relevance of features to different labels, leading to label inconsistency among proximate neighbors and further introducing label confusion and overfitting to synthetic instances. To overcome the above issue, we propose a novel sampling approach called Label-Specific Distance-based Multi-Label Oversampling (LSDMLO) that creates more useful and well-labeled synthetic instances to address the imbalance in multi-label datasets. LSDMLO derives the label-specific distance to identify label-consistent neighbors based on the weighted pertinent feature space, which facilitates selecting seed instances that express more label correlations in boundary areas and generating synthetic instances aligned with the label distribution of original data. The comprehensive experiments verify that the proposed LSDMLO outperforms the state-of-the-art multi-label sampling approaches under various base classifiers.

### [292] [Short paper: Models in the dark -- Rectification and erasure under GDPR in ML supply chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05946)
*Henrik Graßhoff,Malte Hansen,Meiko Jensen,Sara Ramezanian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了机器学习供应链中实施GDPR更正权与删除权的法律与技术困境，提出了“暗箱模型”概念，强调了跨学科方法在构建可信人工智能中的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GDPR更正权和删除权在机器学习系统中的落实面临严峻挑战，且既有研究多将法律与技术视角割裂，忽略了现实中机器学习模型在复杂的开发、分发与部署供应链中所涉及的多个参与方，导致许多合规要求在实践中无法落实。

Method: 采用跨学科的综述分析方法，结合学术文献调研与数据保护机构的指导原则，对机器学习系统在实施GDPR数据主体权利时面临的法律与技术双重障碍进行了系统性评估，并提出了“暗箱模型”（models in the dark）的概念模型以分析供应链下游的合规痛点。

Result: 研究发现，当前技术水平难以完全满足GDPR的相关要求，尤其是供应链下游产生的“暗箱模型”缺乏足够的透明度和可追溯性，这成为落实数据主体权利的主要技术与法律盲区，且现有研究对该问题的关注严重不足。

Conclusion: 实现机器学习中的数据主体权利（更正权与删除权）不仅仅是一个技术问题，更是一个复杂的跨学科挑战。必须在法律合规与技术实践之间建立桥梁，特别是在涉及复杂供应链的“暗箱模型”环境下，提升模型的可追溯性与透明度是实现可信人工智能的关键。

Abstract: The rights to rectification and erasure, as established under the General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR), are central to protecting individuals' privacy. However, their effective enforcement in machine learning (ML) systems remains challenging. Existing work has largely addressed these rights from either a legal or a technical perspective in isolation and disregards the fact that models are produced in complex supply chains involving multiple actors across development, distribution, and deployment. This paper presents a holistic survey of challenges in implementing the rights to rectification and erasure in ML models. Drawing on academic literature and guidance from data protection authorities, we find that many GDPR requirements cannot yet be technically met in practice. Our findings further suggest that issues arising in ML supply chains are insufficiently addressed in research. To tackle this gap, we introduce the notion of models in the dark -- derived models created further downstream in an ML chain without sufficient transparency or traceability -- and analyse the urgent challenges posed by this phenomenon. By adopting an interdisciplinary perspective, this work contributes to bridging the gap between legal requirements and the technical implementation of data subject rights in ML, ultimately supporting the development of trustworthy artificial intelligence.

</details>


### [293] [Dead Directions: Geometric Singular Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05957)
*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究架起了奇异学习理论与信息几何之间的桥梁，通过“死亡方向”概念，实现在无需奇异点消解的情况下，直接从深度神经网络的原参数空间中提取其奇异性几何特征，并据此改进了优化算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异学习理论和信息几何虽然都研究参数空间，但两者在词汇和适用范围上长期分离：前者依赖复杂的奇异点消解，后者通常假设非退化性，无法应对深度学习中普遍存在的过参数化和模型奇异性问题。研究旨在搭建理论桥梁，实现在无需高昂计算成本的奇异点消解前提下，直接量化模型的几何特性。

Method: 1. 引入“死亡方向”（Dead Direction）作为连接奇异学习理论与信息几何的通用基元，利用定向Fisher曲率在奇异点附近的衰减率来表征KL散度的阶数；
2. 提出一种在不依赖Hironaka消解的情况下，直接从原始坐标参数中提取实对数正则阈值（RLCT）及其相关参数（多重性m，奇异涨落ν）的方法；
3. 将几何速率提升至深度神经网络结构，推导了基于K-FAC分解的层级Fisher块衰减率计算方法；
4. 证明了在梯度流下的商空间动力学，并据此设计了满足G-等变性的优化器DDCAdam。

Result: 1. 实现了在原始参数坐标下，通过单次训练检查点（Checkpoint）的前向和后向传播，直接读取Watanabe三元组（λ, m, ν），无需进行昂贵的后验采样；
2. 构建了针对深度网络架构的封闭式几何预测公式，揭示了激活侧与梯度侧衰减率之间的对偶性；
3. 提出了DDCAdam算法，通过在商空间保持梯度流的几何不变性，解决了标准Adam在处理奇异几何时的不匹配问题。

Conclusion: 本研究通过构建“死亡方向”这一桥梁，成功统一了奇异学习理论与信息几何在处理过参数化模型时的视角。通过无需奇异点消解（Resolution of Singularities）的方法，直接在原参数坐标下提取出刻画模型奇异性的几何不变量（Watanabe三元组），为理解深度神经网络的训练动力学、模型复杂度和优化过程提供了坚实的几何理论基础，并为设计针对性优化算法提供了新思路。

Abstract: Singular learning theory and information geometry have studied the same parameter spaces in mostly separate vocabularies: the former computes Bayesian invariants in resolved coordinates, the latter works in original coordinates under a non-degeneracy assumption that overparameterised models routinely violate. We bridge them through one primitive, the dead direction: a unit vector along which the Fisher metric degenerates, equivalently a tangent to the analytic singular set with a definite KL order, set by how fast the KL divergence vanishes. The two readings name the same vector; our central move shows its KL order is recoverable as the decay rate of the directional Fisher curvature approaching the singularity, in original parameter coordinates and without a Hironaka resolution. A selection rule on smooth fibres translates this rate into Watanabe's single-direction contribution to the real log canonical threshold, and we extend the recovery to multi-component crossings, multiplicity $m$, the singular fluctuation $ν$ (universal in the KL order for 1D directions), prior-RLCT shifts, and tempered posteriors. We then lift this rate to a deep network: a multi-layer K-FAC factorisation writes each Fisher block as a product of activation- and gradient-side rates with a duality between them, instantiated at modern-network primitives (residual streams, layer normalisation, attention). A quotient theorem carries the rate to the gauge quotient $Θ/G$ under gradient flow on a $G$-invariant metric; SGD qualifies, standard Adam does not, and we construct a $G$-equivariant Adam-family preconditioner (DDCAdam) that does. The bridge yields a parameter-coordinate handle on singular geometry, closed-form per-architecture predictions, and a trajectory-rate readout of Watanabe's triple $(λ, m, ν)$ from one checkpoint's forward and backward passes, without posterior sampling.

</details>


### [294] [Steering Vectors are an Adversarial Attack Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05958)
*Abzal Aidakhmetov,Donato Crisostomi,Tommaso Mencattini,Adrian Robert Minut,Iacopo Masi,Emanuele Rodolà*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了流行的大模型“激活转向”技术存在隐蔽投毒漏洞，攻击者可诱导模型越狱。研究提出了攻击方式并验证了通过“拒绝方向正交化”可有效防御此风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激活转向作为一种无需微调即可控制大模型行为的方法日益流行，但其开源共享的数据集和预计算向量生态系统缺乏安全审查，存在被恶意篡改以实现模型越狱（jailbreak）的风险。

Method: 提出了一种针对激活转向数据的“隐蔽数据投毒攻击”，通过替换转向数据集中4-6%的标记（tokens），使生成的转向向量在保持原有功能的同时隐含反拒绝（anti-refusal）指令；并提出了一种通过拒绝方向正交化（refusal-direction orthogonalization）来检测和防御该攻击的方法。

Result: 实验表明，通过投毒生成的向量在八种模型-属性组合上实现了20%-55%的绝对攻击成功率（ASR），比未投毒的干净向量高出19%-51%；采用正交化防御策略后，能够恢复约82%的安全性，且不影响模型在良性提示词上的表现。

Conclusion: 激活转向技术存在数据投毒的安全隐患，攻击者可通过微小的恶意数据篡改绕过模型安全防御。研究验证了该漏洞的广泛存在性，并证明了正交化防御策略在保持模型正常功能的同时，能够有效缓解此类投毒攻击。

Abstract: Activation steering has become a popular way to control Large Language Model (LLM) behavior without fine-tuning. Since the technique is plug-and-play, users share datasets and precomputed vectors to steer model activations. However, we show that a \emph{stealth data poisoning attack} silently compromises this pipeline. By substituting $4{-}6\%$ of tokens in the steering dataset, an attacker can silently align the resulting vector with an anti-refusal direction. This jailbreaks the target model while preserving the intended steering effect on benign prompts. Under this threat model, a malicious actor can distribute an apparently safe bundle containing texts, vectors, and weights, alongside an equivalence certificate that the end-user can verify. We test the attack on two open-weight model families and eight model-attribute combinations, observing that poisoned vectors reach an absolute attack success rate (ASR) of $20{-}55\%$, $+19\%$ to $+51\%$ over a clean reference. Finally, we find that a refusal-direction orthogonalization defense can recover ${\approx}82\%$ of the ASR gap without harming benign behavior.

### [295] [LLM Explainability with Counterfactual Chains and Causal Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05972)
*Nirit Nussbaum-Hoffer,Nitay Calderon,Liat Ein-Dor,Roi Reichart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用因果图解释大语言模型（LLM）推理过程的新方法，通过反事实数据增强和因果发现算法，将LLM的内部推理机制转化为人类可理解的概念图谱，从而提升了模型的可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多利用LLM提取外部世界的因果关系，但缺乏对LLM自身内部推理机制的透明化解读。本文旨在利用因果图建模LLM的推理过程，使利益相关者能够直观理解模型如何感知和组织高层概念以产生预测。

Method: 本文提出了一种四阶段方法：首先识别类别判别性且人类可理解的概念；其次将输入映射到LLM感知的概念状态；随后引入受MCMC启发的反事实增强程序，通过构建反事实链扩展稀疏观测数据；最后利用σ-CG算法进行稳定的因果发现，构建出描述模型推理机制的因果图。

Result: 实验表明，通过该方法构建的因果图在疾病诊断、情感分析和LLM作为判官等任务中，能够捕捉到与LLM推理逻辑一致的有意义依赖关系。评估证明了该图在预测保真度和结构稳定性方面的有效性，且反事实增强方法提升了因果发现的收敛性和实用价值。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了因果图是理解LLM推理机制的有效工具，不仅增强了模型的可解释性，还能揭示模型在处理特定任务时对高层概念的组织逻辑，为AI系统的透明度提供了新的方法论基础。

Abstract: Causal graphs provide a high-level language for making mechanisms transparent. Recent work uses Large Language Models (LLMs) to recover causal graphs of external-world processes. Instead, in this paper, we use causal graphs to model LLM inference itself, providing stakeholders with a transparent view of how the model perceives and organizes high-level concepts to produce a prediction. We propose a four-phase method for constructing such graphs. Given a target LLM and a set of textual examples, our method discovers class-discriminative, human-interpretable concepts and maps each input to LLM-perceived concept states. We then introduce an MCMC-inspired counterfactual augmentation procedure that expands the sparse observational data through chains of counterfactuals. This enables stable causal discovery with $σ$-CG, yielding informative, interpretable graphs. We apply our method to three LLMs across disease diagnosis, sentiment analysis, and LLM-as-a-judge classification tasks. We evaluate the learned graphs for predictive fidelity and structural stability, and the MCMC-inspired augmentation for convergence and downstream utility. Our results show that the discovered causal graphs capture meaningful dependencies consistent with LLMs' reasoning. Together, this paper provides a foundation for concept-level explainability of LLMs.

### [296] [Compress-Distill: Reasoning Trace Compression for Efficient Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05988)
*Maxime Griot,Paul Steven Scotti,Tanishq Mathew Abraham*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了推理模型思维链的事后压缩技术，证明通过压缩训练数据可以显著提升模型训练速度和推理效率，虽然在最高准确率上略逊于原始长链，但在权衡效率与性能时具有极高的应用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理模型生成的长思维链（Chain-of-Thought）虽然有助于模型学习复杂推理，但存在蒸馏成本高昂、导致学生模型输出冗长且推理效率低下等问题。因此，研究者旨在探索是否可以通过事后压缩这些思维链，在保持模型推理能力的同时，提升训练速度并减少推理过程中的冗余输出。

Method: 本研究采用了事后压缩（post-hoc compression）方法。首先利用Qwen3.5-397B-A17B和gpt-oss-120B生成约283k条正确推理路径；随后使用两个经过指令微调的模型对这些路径进行压缩，将其字符长度缩减至原始的8.6%到21.0%；最后在多种模型规模下评估这些压缩路径对学生模型训练效果及推理性能的影响，并与原始长链及简单截断（naive truncation）方法进行对比。

Result: 实验表明，压缩路径可将训练标记（tokens）减少至原始的12%-30%，训练速度提升2.0-7.6倍，推理输出长度缩短3-19倍。尽管压缩路径在准确率上无法完全匹配原始长链，但其表现通常优于同长度的简单截断方案。在极小规模（如0.8B）模型下，压缩路径能显著缩小与原始路径训练模型的性能差距，实现了高效率的轻量化部署。

Conclusion: 推理链压缩提供了一种准确率与效率之间的权衡（trade-off），而非无损优化。虽然压缩后的跟踪可以保留高达96%的原始准确率，并在推理效率上获得巨大提升，但在所有规模下，使用原始长链条训练的模型仍能保持最高的下游任务准确率。对于追求极致性能的场景，原始长链仍是首选；而对于计算资源受限或对推理延迟敏感的场景，压缩则是有效的优化手段。

Abstract: Reasoning models produce long chain-of-thought traces that are costly to distill and encourage verbose student outputs. We study post-hoc compression of such traces before knowledge distillation. Two teachers, Qwen3.5-397B-A17B and gpt-oss-120B, generate about 283k correct traces each; two instruction-tuned models then compress them to 8.6-21.0% of their original character length. Across a 48-run main grid plus seven Qwen-teacher truncation ablations, compressed traces reduce training tokens to 12-30% of raw, speed up training by 2.0-7.6x, and shorten inference outputs by 3-19x with smaller reductions under the shorter gpt-oss teacher. However, raw traces retain the highest downstream accuracy at every scale and for both teachers. A length-matched raw-trace truncation ablation shows that compression is not merely benefiting from a smaller token budget: model-compressed traces usually beat or match naive truncation, especially for smaller students, while maintaining shorter inference outputs. Overall, reasoning-trace compression offers an accuracy-efficiency trade-off rather than a free improvement: students retain up to 96% of raw-trace accuracy while gaining up to 18x higher per-token efficiency, and at the 0.8B scale under LoRA compressed traces narrow the raw-vs-compressed gap but do not exceed raw.

</details>


### [297] [HoT-SSM:Higher-order Temporal Knowledge Graph Reasoning with State Space Models for Health Care](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05994)
*Thummaluru Siddartha Reddy,Vempalli Naga Sai Saketh,Yash Punjabi,Mahesh Chandran*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有医学知识图谱方法无法有效处理临床概念高阶关联和长程时间依赖的问题，本文提出了HoT-SSM框架，通过超图与状态空间模型的结合，实现了更准确的临床预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于医学知识图谱（MKG）的方法在捕捉临床概念间高阶交互方面能力不足，且在处理电子病历时往往丢失时间信息或缺乏对长程时间依赖的建模，难以支持高精度的临床预测。

Method: 提出了一种名为HoT-SSM的架构：1. 构建基于领域知识的超图，将相关临床概念分组为超边，以保留就诊级别的临床上下文；2. 引入动态超图状态空间模型，通过状态演化显式捕捉患者病情的长程时间依赖关系。

Result: 在MIMIC-III和MIMIC-IV数据集上的实验结果表明，HoT-SSM在性能上显著优于当前的各种先进模型，验证了同时建模高阶临床交互与长程时间依赖的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的HoT-SSM模型成功通过超图结构和状态空间模型的结合，解决了医学知识图谱在处理高阶临床概念关联以及捕捉长程时间依赖性方面的局限性，为医疗电子病历分析提供了更精确、可解释的建模方案。

Abstract: Medical knowledge graphs (MKGs) infused with clinical knowledge have been increasingly used to model electronic health records (EHRs) to support interpretable predictions in healthcare domain. However, existing MKG-based approaches are limited in capturing pairwise relations between clinical concepts (e.g., conditions, procedures, and medications), and restricts their ability to model higher-order interactions among co-occurring or semantically related concepts. In addition, most representation learning methods that leverage MKGs either collapse temporal information across visits or lack an explicit mechanism for modeling long-range temporal dependencies, which is critical for clinical tasks such as mortality prediction. To mitigate these limitations, we propose HoT-SSM, a parameter efficient and higher-order temporal graph reasoning with state space models. For each visit, HoT-SSM constructs hypergraphs by grouping semantically related clinical concepts into hyperedges using domain knowledge, thereby preserving visit-level clinical context. Further, to model the temporal dynamics while learning the representations, we introduce a novel dynamic hypergraph-based state space model that explicitly captures patients latent state evolution over time while preserving long-range information. The learned representations are used for downstream clinical prediction and reasoning. Experiments on MIMIC-III and MIMIC-IV datasets shows significant performance improvement over the current state-of-the-art models, demonstrating the effectiveness of jointly modeling higher-order clinical interactions and long-range temporal dependencies.

### [298] [Diffusion Models for Adaptive Sequential Data Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06007)
*Haoyang Cao,Minshuo Chen,Yinbin Han,Renyuan Xu*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种适用于序列数据生成的顺序前向-后向扩散框架，通过引入条件历史信息和创新的分数匹配目标，实现了具备因果适应性的高质量序列生成，并验证了其在金融组合优化中的实用价值。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种顺序前向-后向扩散框架（Sequential Forward-Backward Diffusion Framework），通过在序列上逐步注入和去除噪声，并调节之前的历史信息来确保生成的适应性（Adaptiveness）。此外，引入了一种新的分数匹配（Score-matching）目标函数以实现高效的并行训练，并利用ReLU网络作为实例导出了统计收敛性保证。

Result: 该方法在ARMA模型和高斯过程等合成数据上表现良好。实验结果表明，该框架在构建均值-方差最优投资组合方面具有显著的有效性，且在理论层面证明了其在分数近似和分布估计方面的收敛能力。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种适应性强且具有理论保证的序列生成框架，证明了在保持时间因果关系的前提下，扩散模型能够有效处理复杂的序列数据建模任务，并在金融组合优化等实际应用中展现了优越性。

Abstract: Generating realistic synthetic sequential data is critical in real-world applications across operations research, finance, healthcare, energy systems, and scientific computing, where time-indexed observations are used for prediction, simulation, risk assessment, and data-driven decision-making. While diffusion models have achieved remarkable success in generating static data, their direct extensions to sequential settings often fail to capture temporal dependence and information structure. Designing diffusion models that can simulate sequential data in an adapted manner, and hence without anticipation of future information, therefore remains an open challenge.
  In this work, we propose a sequential forward-backward diffusion framework for adapted time series generation. Our approach progressively injects and removes noise along the sequence, conditioning on the previously generated history to ensure adaptiveness. A novel score-matching objective is introduced for efficient parallel training. We derive rigorous statistical guarantees under a generic framework, then establish score approximation, score estimation, and distribution estimation results with ReLU networks serving as a concrete instance. Empirically, we validate our method on synthetic data, including ARMA models and Gaussian processes, and demonstrate its effectiveness in constructing mean-variance optimal portfolios.

### [299] [Adaptive Oscillatory-State Alignment for Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06010)
*Zhangyao Song,Ziqiong Li,Xiangfei Qiu,Chao Zha,Yinfei Xu,Tao Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AOSNET 是一种新型的时间序列预测框架，它通过将固定周期模板匹配转换为自适应的振荡状态对齐，有效克服了传统方法在处理非平稳、非严格周期性数据时的建模局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的时间序列通常表现出非平稳性，如幅值调制、相位漂移和局部频率变化，而传统的周期性预测方法（如固定周期或全局谱方法）在面对这些动态变化时往往因模板僵化而表现不佳。

Method: 提出了一种基于希尔伯特变换的预测框架 AOSNET。该方法不依赖固定的周期模板，而是从观测序列和可学习的全局振荡先验中提取解析信号描述符，通过描述符条件门控机制，实现局部振荡状态的自适应对齐，从而在保留可靠信息的同时动态修正失配区域。

Result: 在八个公开基准测试中达到了领先或极具竞争力的预测精度，同时保持了较快的推理速度。合成数据实验进一步验证了随着非平稳性程度的加深，该模型在处理幅值调制和相位漂移等问题上的性能优势愈发明显。

Conclusion: AOSNET 通过引入希尔伯特变换引导的自适应振荡状态对齐机制，成功解决了传统周期性时间序列模型在处理幅值调制、相位漂移和局部频率变化等非平稳动态时的局限性，为长期时间序列预测提供了一种更灵活、鲁棒且高效的框架。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting benefits from inductive biases that expose recurring temporal structure. Existing periodic forecasting methods typically model recurrence through predefined periods, global spectral components, or fixed learnable templates. However, real-world temporal dynamics are rarely rigidly periodic: oscillatory behavior often evolves through amplitude modulation, phase drift, and local frequency variation. Under these conditions, fixed-template periodic modeling can become fundamentally mismatched to the underlying temporal states. We propose AOSNET, a Hilbert-guided forecasting framework that reformulates periodic forecasting from fixed template matching to adaptive oscillatory-state alignment. AOSNET extracts analytic-signal descriptors from both the observed sequence and a learnable global oscillatory prior, then adaptively aligns local states through a descriptor-conditioned gate that selectively preserves reliable observations while softly correcting mismatched regions. The learned prior serves not as a rigid repeated template but as a flexible oscillatory reference interpreted through local state dynamics. Experiments on eight benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art or highly competitive accuracy with fast inference speed. Controlled synthetic studies isolating amplitude modulation, phase drift, and local frequency variation confirm that the advantage of oscillatory-state alignment consistently increases as non-stationarity intensifies.

</details>


### [300] [OPRD: On-Policy Representation Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06021)
*Shenzhi Yang,Guangcheng Zhu,Bowen Song,Haobo Wang,Mingxuan Xia,Xing Zheng,Yingfan Ma,Zhongqi Chen,Weiqiang Wang,Gang Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 OPRD 方法，通过对齐教师和学生模型的隐藏状态（而非仅输出概率），解决了传统策略内蒸馏中采样方差大和信息利用率低的问题，实现了在复杂推理任务中性能的提升以及训练开销的显著下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的策略内蒸馏（OPD）方法存在两大局限：一是由于词表规模巨大导致的 Monte Carlo KL 估计存在严重的采样方差；二是仅在输出空间对齐，将教师模型视为黑盒，丢失了大量中间层级的有用特征。

Method: 提出了一种名为“策略内表示蒸馏”（OPRD）的方法。该方法跳过语言模型头部，直接在选定层级上对齐学生模型和教师模型的隐藏状态表示。这种方法在相同的 Rollout 数据上进行训练，旨在消除 Monte Carlo KL 估计带来的采样方差，并利用教师模型中更丰富的层级结构信息。

Result: 在 AIME 2024/2025 和 AIMO 基准测试中，OPRD 成功弥合了学生与教师模型之间的性能差距，优于传统的输出空间 OPD 基线；同时，在训练效率方面，相比 Top-k OPD，其训练速度提升了 1.44 倍，内存占用降低了 54%。

Conclusion: OPRD 是一种高效且有效的蒸馏范式，通过将知识蒸馏从输出空间提升到隐藏状态空间，克服了传统策略内蒸馏的采样方差问题，并充分利用了教师模型的中间层信息，实现了性能与效率的双重提升。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) supervises the student only in output space by matching next-token probabilities. This output-only paradigm has two limits: (1) sampling variance from Monte Carlo KL estimates over large vocabularies (e.g., Qwen's ~150k tokens) persists throughout training, and (2) it treats the teacher as a black-box, discarding all intermediate hidden states after the LM head. We propose On-Policy Representation Distillation (OPRD), which lifts distillation into hidden-state space by aligning student and teacher representations across selected layers on the same rollouts, bypassing the LM head entirely. Theoretically, OPRD eliminates sampling variance and provides richer per-layer structural information. Empirically, OPRD closes the student-teacher gap on AIME 2024/2025 and AIMO, while output-space OPD baselines plateau below the teacher. OPRD also trains 1.44x faster and uses 54% less memory than top-k OPD. Code: https://github.com/ShenzhiYang2000/OPRD.

### [301] [Catastrophic Forgetting as Accessibility Collapse: A Three-Level Framework for Knowledge Persistence in Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06032)
*Ayushman Trivedi,Bhavika Melwani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示灾难性遗忘本质上并非旧知识被彻底破坏，而是模型失去了对所保留知识的访问能力，这意味着旧信息仍以分布式表征的形式深埋于网络中，可通过修复分类器或访问机制予以恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点将灾难性遗忘视为学习新任务时对旧知识的不可逆抹除。本文旨在挑战这一观点，探讨遗忘是否更源于模型虽然保留了知识，但失去了对这些知识的访问途径（可访问性失效），从而试图揭示持续学习过程中表征演变的本质。

Method: 构建了一个包含知识存储、表征和可访问性的三级分析框架，并在顺序CIFAR-100分类任务上使用ResNet-18进行实验。采用了检查点持久性评估、线性探测（Linear Probing）、表征几何分析、分类器重置恢复以及层级可恢复性分析等多种手段，深入剖析遗忘发生时模型内部的状态。

Result: 实验表明，即使在模型表现出完全的灾难性遗忘（任务准确率降至0%）时，线性探测依然保留了约76%的原有表征信息；仅通过重置并微调分类器，即可恢复约75.7%的原始任务性能。此外，层级分析证实早期和中间层保留了高度可恢复的信息，且遗忘的知识以分布式高维表征的形式存在，而非仅依赖于少数主导子空间。

Conclusion: 灾难性遗忘并非旧知识的彻底物理抹除，而更应被理解为一种“可访问性丧失”。神经网络在经历遗忘后，深层特征中仍保留了大量可恢复的任务信息，通过简单的分类器重置即可实现显著性能恢复。这一发现挑战了传统认为知识被破坏的观点，为改进持续学习算法提供了新思路。

Abstract: Catastrophic forgetting is commonly interpreted as the irreversible erasure of previously acquired knowledge during sequential learning. In this work, we investigate an alternative perspective: that forgetting may arise not from complete destruction of task representations but from a loss of accessibility to preserved information. We introduce a three-level framework separating knowledge storage, representation, and accessibility, and evaluate each component through a series of continual-learning experiments on sequential CIFAR-100 classification using ResNet-18. Our analysis combines checkpoint persistence, linear probing, representation geometry, classifier-reset recovery, and layer-wise recoverability experiments. We observe complete behavioral forgetting of earlier tasks, with task accuracy collapsing from 54.8% to 0%, while linear probe performance retains approximately 76% of the original representational information. Furthermore, retraining only the final classifier restores 75.7% of the original task performance without modifying the backbone network. Layer-wise analysis reveals that early and intermediate layers preserve highly recoverable task information despite severe degradation at later stages. Projection-energy and principal-angle analyses indicate that retained knowledge persists as distributed high-dimensional representations rather than through preservation of a small dominant subspace. These findings suggest that catastrophic forgetting is better characterized as an accessibility failure than complete representational erasure, and that substantial task-relevant information remains embedded within neural representations even after functional forgetting has occurred.

### [302] [When Good Enough Is Optimal: Multiplication-Only Matrix Inversion Approximation for Quantized Gated DeltaNet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06034)
*Luoming Zhang,Yuwei Ren,Kui Zhang,Tian Liu,Lingjuan Ge,Denghao Li,Matthew Harper Langston,Yin Huang,Weiliang Will Zeng,Liang Zhang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 采用截断的纽曼级数（Neumann series）展开来逼近下三角矩阵的逆；
2. 利用结构化掩码（structural masking）和并行残差校正（parallel residual correction）消除前向代换算法中的序列依赖；
3. 针对低比特量化（INT）设计了动态范围压缩策略，缓解了矩阵幂运算带来的数值溢出问题；
4. 根据分块大小动态调整近似阶数和残差步骤，以在计算代价和精度之间取得平衡。

Result: 在Qwen3.5系列模型上的实验表明，该算法在核函数级别实现了最高5倍的加速，推理解码层的开销降低了20%，同时在浮点运算和低精度量化推理中均保持了良好的模型精度。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种基于矩阵乘法（MatMul）的线性注意力机制逆矩阵计算算法，通过利用纽曼级数展开和残差校正，有效解决了分块线性注意力中矩阵求逆的计算瓶颈。该方法不仅在提升计算并行度和硬件利用率方面表现优异，还通过支持低比特量化实现了高效推理，为长上下文建模提供了一种高性能的算子优化方案。

Abstract: Matrix inversion in chunk-wise parallel linear attention is a major bottleneck for long-context modeling, particularly on NPUs, where forward-substitution-based methods exhibit limited parallelism and poor hardware utilization. We propose a fast, Matrix Multiplication (MatMul)-based algorithm tailored for strictly lower-triangular matrices arising in chunk-wise linear attention. Motivated by the rapid growth of Neumann-series terms and the diagonal concentration of the inverse matrix, we employ a truncated Neumann expansion with structural masking and parallel residual correction to eliminate sequential dependencies. We further extend our method to low-bits INT by mitigating the dynamic range expansion arising from repeated matrix power operations, and adapt the approximation order and residual step to the chunk size to minimize computational cost while preserving the model's accuracy. Experiments on Qwen3.5-family models demonstrate up to 5$\times$ kernel-level speedup and a 20% reduction in decode-layer overhead, while preserving accuracy under both floating-point and low-precision inference. Our method offers an efficient and hardware-friendly solution for scalable linear attention.

Method: 本文采用了基于KL散度正则化的方法，通过KL散度定量描述模型误设定。在算法层面，研究了结合Gibbs策略更新的回归算法（regression-based algorithms），并针对情境赌博机（contextual bandits）和情境强化学习（episodic RL）推导了高概率下的KL-悔值保证。

Result: 研究建立了在存在模型误设定情况下的高概率KL-悔值保证，并给出了明确的误设定误差项。该结果不仅涵盖了经典的可实现情形，也为模型不完全匹配的环境提供了量化分析，证明了算法在面对模型偏差时的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入KL散度衡量模型偏差，为存在模型误设定的情境下，情境赌博机和情境强化学习提供了理论保证。研究表明，基于回归的Gibbs策略更新算法能够适应模型误设定，并成功恢复了理想状态下的标准悔值界，这为处理复杂实际应用中模型不精确的问题提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study KL-regularized contextual bandits and episodic reinforcement learning (RL) under general function approximation with model misspecification. This work introduces KL misspecification formulations for contextual bandits and episodic RL and analyzes regression-based algorithms with Gibbs policy updates. High-probability KL-regret guarantees with explicit misspecification terms are established, recovering the standard realizable KL-regularized setting as a special case.

### [304] [MDP-GRPO: Stabilized Group Relative Policy Optimization for Multi-Constraint Instruction Following](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06058)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的组相对策略优化（GRPO）在处理离散且低方差的奖励时会出现不稳定性，主要表现为低方差放大、均值中心化盲点和零方差崩溃等问题，难以有效完成多约束指令遵循任务。

Method: 本文提出了 MDP-GRPO 方法，包含四个核心优化策略：1) 多温度采样以增加奖励分布的离散度；2) 双锚定优势函数以纠正偏差并恢复梯度；3) 基于前景理论的奖励重塑以限制更新幅度；4) 非对称 KL 正则化。

Result: 在 FollowBench、IFEval 及多个多约束数据集上的实验结果表明，MDP-GRPO 显著优于标准 GRPO，在 Llama-3.2-3B 模型上严格约束满足率提升了 5.0%，并在保持模型通用能力（如 MMLU 和 ARC）的同时实现了更小的组规模下的稳定收敛。

Conclusion: MDP-GRPO 通过解决离散低方差奖励环境下的优化不稳定性，为受限指令微调提供了一种更稳健的强化学习方案，且在不牺牲通用能力的前提下显著提升了指令遵循的性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is ideal for multi-constraint instruction following, yet standard group-relative policy optimization (GRPO) becomes unstable under discrete, low-dispersion rewards, where within-group reward distributions are frequently homogeneous. We identify and formalize three pathologies of z-score group normalization in this regime: low-variance amplification, mean-centering blindness, and zero-variance collapse. To address them, we propose MDP-GRPO, which stabilizes learning through (1) multi-temperature sampling to increase reward dispersion, (2) dual-anchor advantages to restore gradients in homogeneous groups and stop mean-centering blindness, (3) prospect-theoretic shaping to bound updates and penalize violations based on Kahneman and Tversky's theory, and (4) asymmetric KL regularization. Evaluated on FollowBench, IFEval, and a curated multi-constraint dataset, MDP-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO, improving strict constraint satisfaction by up to 5.0% on Llama-3.2-3B. Our method also enables stable convergence with small group sizes while preserving general capabilities on MMLU and ARC.

### [305] [On Advantage Estimates for Max@K Policy Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06080)
*Shota Takashiro,Soichiro Nishimori,Paavo Parmas,Yongmin Kim,Kohsei Matsutani,Gouki Minegishi,Yusuke Iwasawa,Takeshi Kojima,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对大模型推理优化中梯度估计不统一及方差大的问题，提出了MaxPO方法。通过创新的L2O基线设计实现优势函数的精确中心化，在保持策略梯度无偏的同时有效提升了训练性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型后训练中，强化学习受限于稀疏奖励带来的探索难题。直接优化推理时目标（如pass@K, max@K）虽是有效补充，但现有方法在策略梯度估计、基线设计和归一化方面缺乏统一标准且存在效率与方差问题。

Method: 研究首先分析了现有推理时间目标（如pass@K和max@K）的策略梯度估计器，指出其存在的非中心化问题。随后，提出了Leave-Two-Out（L2O）基线设计，通过在计算优势时排除当前样本及其配对样本，实现了无偏且中心化的梯度估计，并开发了高效的二次时间复杂度实现方案MaxPO。

Result: 实验表明，MaxPO方法显著降低了梯度估计的方差，在LLM后训练的推理任务中优于现有的非中心化基线方法，并成功构建了针对max@K目标的规范化有限批次优势估计框架。

Conclusion: 通过引入“留二法”（Leave-Two-Out, L2O）基线，MaxPO方法在保持策略梯度无偏性的前提下实现了对批量优势函数的精确中心化，显著降低了梯度方差并提升了在大模型后训练推理任务中的性能。该研究统一了针对max@K等推理目标的多样化梯度估计方法。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is widely used for post-training reasoning models, but sparse outcome rewards make exploration difficult. A complementary approach is to optimize inference-time objectives such as pass@K and max@K directly, yet existing policy-gradient estimators for these objectives use different signals, baselines, and normalizations, making their relationships unclear. We study this issue through baseline design and advantage centering. Starting from the advantage estimator of a leading method in the field, we show that it is policy-gradient unbiased but yields a non-centered advantage. We then introduce a Leave-Two-Out baseline that preserves policy-gradient unbiasedness while making realized batch advantages exactly centered. The resulting method, MaxPO, has an efficient quadratic-time implementation and integrates naturally into group-based RL for LLM post-training. We further derive the canonical finite-batch advantage for max@K, providing a unified view of existing advantage estimators. Empirically, we verify that the L2O baseline reduces gradient variance and outperforms non-centered alternatives.

### [306] [OrderGrad: Optimizing Beyond the Mean with Order-Statistic Policy Gradient Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06096)
*Paavo Parmas,Yongmin Kim,Kohsei Matsutani,Shota Takashiro,Soichiro Nishimori,Takeshi Kojima,Yusuke Iwasawa,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OrderGrad 是一种通用的强化学习梯度估计器，通过奖励重加权实现对顺序统计量（如 CVaR、中位数等）的优化，从而有效地解决传统期望回报优化无法处理的风险规避和鲁棒性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的策略梯度方法主要优化期望回报，但在许多现实场景中，人们更关注回报的分布特性，例如尾部风险控制、离群点鲁棒性，或者在多种可能结果中寻找最优解（如最佳 K 个结果）。现有的方法难以直接、统一地处理这些分布属性，因此作者提出了 OrderGrad。

Method: OrderGrad 提出了一系列针对顺序统计（order-statistic）目标的似然比和重参数化梯度估计器。该方法的核心是通过对有限样本的奖励进行排序，并应用特定的秩权重（rank weights）来计算加权平均值，从而将非凸的顺序统计目标转化为标准的策略梯度优化问题。它通过简单的奖励变换，实现了对 VaR、CVaR、截尾均值等目标函数的无偏梯度估计。

Result: 实验结果表明，OrderGrad 在包括大语言模型（LLM）数学推理后训练在内的多项任务中表现优异。在那些期望值优化与部署目标不匹配的任务中，OrderGrad 能够通过优化特定的顺序统计量（如 CVaR 或 Top-m），有效提升系统的性能，并展示了在风险规避、鲁棒性提升和探索性学习方面的实用性。

Conclusion: OrderGrad 提供了一种通用且易于实现的框架，用于优化各种顺序统计目标（如 VaR、CVaR、中位数等）。它通过简单的奖励重加权机制，解决了传统策略梯度方法难以处理复杂分布属性（如尾部风险、鲁棒性或最佳样本发现）的问题，为强化学习在实际应用中的部署提供了更灵活的优化手段。

Abstract: Policy-gradient methods usually optimize expected return, but many real world applications care about distributional properties of returns: tail risk, outlier robustness, or best-of-K discovery. We introduce OrderGrad, a family of likelihood-ratio and reparameterization gradient estimators for order-statistic objectives. OrderGrad optimizes finite-sample L-statistics, i.e., weighted averages of sorted rewards or costs, recovering objectives such as VaR, CVaR, trimmed means, medians, and top-m/best-of-K criteria by changing only the rank weights. For any fixed sample size and rank-weight vector, OrderGrad provides an unbiased gradient estimator for the corresponding order-statistic objective. The method is implemented as a simple reward transformation that can then be used in an otherwise standard policy-gradient or reparameterized update. We study the resulting estimator's variance behavior and evaluate it on tasks where mean optimization is mismatched to the deployment objective, including LLM math post-training and other tasks. OrderGrad provides a unified, plug-and-play route to risk-averse, robust, and exploratory learning.
  Code: https://github.com/paavo5/ordergrad

### [307] [A Sliced-Wasserstein Framework on Correlation Matrices for EEG Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06104)
*Chen Hu,Rui Wang,Jiale Zhou,Jingjun Yi,Shaocheng Jin,Yidong Song,Yefeng Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于拉回欧几里得度量的切片Wasserstein（PEMSW）框架，用于处理全秩相关矩阵流形上的EEG解码问题。通过构建相关切片Wasserstein（CorSW）度量，实现了在无需增加推理成本的前提下，显著提升了脑电图在不同分布间的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的EEG解码方法多依赖于协方差描述符，但其对通道缩放较为敏感。尽管全秩相关矩阵提供了尺度不变性，但在该流形上缺乏有效的度量方式。因此，本文旨在开发一种能够处理相关矩阵流形几何特性的度量方法，以提升EEG解码在分布偏移下的泛化能力。

Method: 1. 提出了基于拉回欧几里得度量（PEMs）的切片Wasserstein（SW）差异通用框架（PEMSW）；2. 在此框架下，针对全秩相关矩阵流形，实例化了两种相关切片Wasserstein（CorSW）差异度量：离对数度量（OLM）和对数缩放度量（LSM）；3. 基于CorSW构建了一个用于脑电图（EEG）解码的领域泛化（DG）框架。

Result: 在三个EEG数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在应对数据分布偏移时具有更好的泛化性能，且训练开销较低，推理阶段无额外计算成本。

Conclusion: 通过在全秩相关矩阵流形上引入PEMSW框架和CorSW差异度量，本文为脑电图解码提供了一种能够应对分布偏移、具有鲁棒性的领域泛化方法。该方法不仅在理论上严谨，且在实际应用中展现了优越的性能，且不增加推理成本。

Abstract: Electroencephalography (EEG) offers noninvasive, millisecond resolution recordings of neuronal activity and is widely used in neuroscience and healthcare. Many EEG decoding pipelines rely on covariance descriptors for their robustness to noise, but such representations are sensitive to channel-wise scaling. Recent studies have therefore advocated full-rank correlation matrices as a scale-invariant alternative for EEG decoding. In this paper, we propose a general framework for Sliced Wasserstein (SW) discrepancies on manifolds endowed with Pullback Euclidean Metrics (PEMs), termed Pullback Euclidean Metric Sliced Wasserstein (PEMSW). Within this framework, we instantiate two Correlation Sliced-Wasserstein (CorSW) discrepancies on the manifold of full-rank correlation matrices under two recently introduced correlation geometries, \textit{i.e.}, the Off-Log Metric (OLM) and Log-Scaled Metric (LSM). Building on CorSW, we further develop a domain generalization (DG) framework for EEG decoding. Experiments on three EEG datasets demonstrate improved generalization under distribution shifts, with low training overhead and no additional inference cost. The source code is available at https://github.com/ChenHu-ML/CorSW.

### [308] [Adaptive state-action abstractions via rate-distortion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06123)
*Fernando E. Rosas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种强化学习中动态调整抽象粒度的新原则，即当学习误差与抽象误差相当时进行模型细化。该方法通过结合Bellman残差与互模拟度量实现误差解耦，并在保证性能的同时实现了高效的状态-动作压缩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习缺乏在复杂任务学习过程中动态调整抽象粒度的通用准则。受婴儿学习走路时由粗到细的策略启发，本文旨在解决如何通过权衡抽象损失与学习误差，实现计算效率与任务性能的最优平衡。

Method: 提出了一种基于“学习误差与抽象误差相当时进行细化”的自适应抽象原则。具体方法包括：1. 利用性能证书将价值误差分解为Bellman残差（学习误差）和互模拟度量（抽象误差）；2. 采用基于速率失真理论构建的软状态-动作抽象机制，允许在学习过程中连续调整状态和动作空间的抽象粒度。

Result: 在多个表格化实验环境中，该方法展示了即便在状态和动作信息经过大幅有损压缩的情况下，智能体依然能够维持接近最优的学习性能。实验证明了所提出的切换策略能够有效指导抽象粒度的动态演化。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过在学习误差（Bellman残差）和抽象误差（互模拟度量）之间建立动态平衡，智能体能够实现从粗粒度到细粒度的自适应学习。这种基于速率失真理论的抽象调整策略，在保证近最优性能的同时，大幅降低了计算复杂度和状态/动作空间维度。

Abstract: When learning to walk, infants seem to address a coarse version of the problem first - stay upright, reach the caregiver - and refine it only when further practice at that resolution stops paying off. Reinforcement learning offers multiple techniques for building simple versions of complex tasks, but lacks general principles for how to dynamically adjust the granularity of these abstractions during learning. This paper proposes one such principle: refine the abstraction as soon as the learning error within it becomes comparable to the error induced by the abstraction itself. Here, we investigate one way of formalising this principle via a performance certificate that decomposes value error into two terms: a learning error bound captured by a Bellman residual, and an abstraction error bound given by a bisimulation metric. The resulting switching strategy is implemented by soft state-action abstractions built from rate-distortion principles, whose resolution along state and action axes can be continuously adjusted. We validate this construction in a range of tabular settings, showing that near-optimal performance can be achieved under substantial lossy compression of state and action information.

### [309] [Tight list replicability bounds via a novel sphere covering theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06148)
*Ari Blondal,Hamed Hatami,Pooya Hatami,Chavdar Lalov,Sivan Tretiak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文利用新的拓扑球面覆盖定理，解决了列表可复制性中的核心边界问题，确立了VC类及大间隔半空间下的最优列表大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨机器学习中列表可复制性（list replicability）的理论框架，核心目标是量化实现特定精度所需的列表大小与假设类的自然复杂度指标（如VC维）之间的关系。

Method: 提出了一种基于Borsuk-Ulam定理的拓扑球面覆盖定理：若$d$维球面被一组开集覆盖，且每个开集都位于一个开半球内，则这些开集中必然有$d+1$个具有公共交集。以此为理论基础，推导了VC类在列表可复制性下的精确界限。

Result: 获得了VC类中列表大小与精度关系的精确界；对于大间隔半空间，证明了当间隔适中时，最优列表大小等于环境维度$d$；而在间隔足够大时，设计出了一种仅需$\lceil d/2 \rceil + 1$大小列表的可复制算法。

Conclusion: 该研究通过建立列表可复制性与学习理论中的经典复杂度指标之间的联系，不仅为理解列表可复制性的本质提供了深刻的拓扑学视角，还揭示了特定算法约束下最优列表大小的界限。

Abstract: In recent years, list replicability has emerged as a framework for formalizing reproducibility in learning theory. A central question is how the required list size relates to the accuracy parameter and natural complexity measures of the hypothesis class.
  To achieve sharp bounds on list replicability, we prove a novel topological sphere covering theorem, derived from the Borsuk-Ulam theorem. Specifically, if the $d$-sphere is covered by open sets, each of which lies in an open hemisphere, then $d+1$ of these sets must have a common intersection. Using this result, we obtain a sharp bound on the relationship between list size and accuracy for VC classes. We also show that for large-margin half-spaces, provided the margin is not too large, the optimal list size equals the ambient dimension. However, when the margin is taken to be very large, we devise a replicable algorithm achieving the minimal list size of $\lceil d/2 \rceil + 1$.

</details>


### [310] [Trust-Aware Predictive Emissions Monitoring for Gas Turbine Fleets with Limited Labelled Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06156)
*Rebecca Potts,Aiden Durrant,Rick Hackney,Georgios Leontidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对燃气轮机机队排放预测中标签数据稀缺的问题，本文提出了一种信任感知概率框架，通过多维度的不确定性评估和置信度估计，实现了对未标注资产的高可靠性预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种结合了多头循环预测模型、学习型置信度估计、基于集成的不确定性量化、辅助特征预测、特征空间距离分析以及运行范围诊断的信任感知概率框架。该框架利用少量标签数据校准，生成可解释的样本级信任分数，用于评估无标签涡轮机上的预测可靠性。

Result: 实验结果表明，该框架能显著提升性能，通过置信度过滤，平均绝对误差（MAE）从全覆盖时的0.202降低至最高置信度10%时的0.070。此外，该框架能够正确识别分布外样本并表现出较高的不确定性，验证了置信度估计与预测误差之间的强相关性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的信任感知概率框架有效解决了燃气轮机机队在标签数据有限的情况下的排放预测难题。通过提供样本级的可信度评分，该框架能够识别不可靠的预测，从而在实际工业部署中增强了系统的透明度和可信度。

Abstract: Machine learning-based predictive emissions monitoring systems offer a practical alternative to direct emissions measurement, but their deployment across gas turbine fleets is challenging when emissions labels are available for only a small subset of assets. In this work, a trust-aware probabilistic framework is proposed for fleet-level gas turbine NOx prediction under limited labelled supervision. The framework combines a multi-head recurrent prediction model with learned confidence estimation, ensemble-based uncertainty quantification, auxiliary feature prediction, feature-space distance analysis, and operating-range diagnostics. These signals are calibrated on labelled data to produce interpretable per-sample trust scores, providing indicators of prediction reliability on unlabelled turbines, supporting the identification of predictions that should be treated with greater caution during fleet-level deployment. Confidence-based filtering reduces MAE from 0.202 at full coverage to 0.070 for the highest-confidence 10\% of predictions, demonstrating that confidence estimates are meaningfully related to prediction error. Unlabelled and out-of-distribution samples exhibit increased uncertainty and reduced confidence, indicating that the framework responds appropriately to distributional shift. The results show that the proposed trust framework provides actionable reliability information for emissions prediction on unlabelled turbines, supporting more transparent and trustworthy deployment of PEMS across industrial fleets.
