### [311] [On the training of physics-informed neural operators for solving parametric partial differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06164)
*Nanxi Chen,Chuanjie Cui,Airong Chen,Sifan Wang,Rujin Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了物理信息神经算子（PINO）的训练瓶颈，验证了CViT架构的优越性，并揭示了PINN的优化策略可有效提升PINO的性能，为构建稳健的算子学习模型提供了实践框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Physics-informed neural operators (PINOs) aim to learn solution operators for partial differential equations by using the governing physics as supervision, rather than relying solely on paired input-output simulation data. By incorporating physical constraints into the training objective, PINOs combine the cross-instance generalization of neural operators with the data efficiency of physics-informed learning. Despite this promise, how to train PINOs efficiently and robustly remains less well-understood than the training of either data-driven neural operators or physics-informed neural networks (PINNs). To bridge this gap, we examine key components of the PINO training pipeline, including architecture design, optimizer choice, loss balancing, and collocation-point sampling strategy. We study three representative operator backbones, Deep Operator Network (DeepONet), Fourier Neural Operator (FNO), and Continuous Vision Transformer (CViT), across five diverse parametric PDE systems. Our results show that CViT provides consistently strong and stable performance across the considered benchmarks. Beyond architecture, we find that several optimization pathologies previously identified in PINN training naturally arise in PINOs, including gradient conflicts and causal violation. We also find that mitigation algorithms developed for PINNs remain effective in the PINO setting. We further compare physics-informed and data-driven training under different data regimes, revealing that a carefully designed physics-informed training pipeline can match, and in some cases, outperform purely data-driven neural operators. Taken together, these findings provide a systematic empirical understanding of the optimization challenges in PINO training and inform a practical pipeline for efficient and robust physics-informed operator learning. Code and data are available at https://github.com/NanxiiChen/PI-CViT.

### [314] [A Machine Learning-Based Framework for Discovering Huntington's Disease Stages: Integrating Graph Representation Learning and clustering to Uncover Progression Dynamics in Longitudinal Enroll-HD Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06196)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该研究采用了一种基于动态图表示学习（Dynamic Graph Representation Learning）的无监督机器学习框架，旨在从纵向临床测量数据中捕获患者内部及患者间的时空依赖关系。研究利用学到的数据表示，应用K-means++聚类算法，并通过稳定性分析（Stability Analysis）迭代增加聚类数（k），以确定稳健且具有临床意义的疾病阶段划分。数据源自Enroll-HD队列中302名参与者的1,477次随访数据（每个随访包含44个临床变量）。

Result: 该框架在四维潜在空间中实现了稳健的聚类效果，成功识别出四个统计学上显著且临床意义明确的疾病阶段。与既往的临床分期方法相比，该模型生成的阶段边界定义更加清晰，且组间重叠程度显著降低，证明了该方法在捕捉HD自然疾病进程方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，基于动态图表示学习的无监督机器学习框架能够通过纵向临床数据，客观且稳健地识别亨廷顿舞蹈病（HD）的临床阶段。该方法克服了传统依赖阈值的临床分期局限性，提供了一种更具数据驱动和客观性的疾病分期工具，有助于更精确地表征疾病进程并支持个性化医疗研究。

Abstract: Huntington's disease (HD) is a progressive brain disorder that gradually affects movement, cognitive function, and behavior. Identifying the stage of the disease accurately and consistently is important for understanding its course, grouping patients, personalized care, and discovering treatment. Existing clinical staging frameworks rely primarily on predefined clinical measurement thresholds and clinical expert decisions, yet these discrete cut-offs may obscure meaningful intra-stage variability and remain vulnerable to inter-rater differences, especially in motor and functional assessments. To address these limitations, we developed an unsupervised machine learning framework based on dynamic graph representation learning to capture temporal relationships within and across patients from longitudinal clinical measurements. Using the learned representations, we applied K-means++ clustering to identify well-separated groups. We then iteratively increased the number of clusters (k), using stability analysis to assess robustness and reveal additional meaningful clusters beyond the initial optimal solution. We applied the framework to 302 individuals from the Enroll-HD cohort (1,477 visits, 44 clinical variables per visit; 80% manifest participants), enabling data-driven discovery of HD stages reflecting natural clinical progression. Despite the limited cohort size, the proposed framework achieved robust clustering performance using a four-dimensional latent space, identifying four meaningful and statistically distinct disease stages through clustering stability analysis. Each stage corresponded to well-defined clinical measurement boundaries, with minimal overlap compared to previously established clinical staging methods.

</details>

*Raphaël Romero*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EventNMF是一种新型的连续时间非负矩阵分解模型，它直接在事件发生的时间点上进行建模，通过B样条分解避免了数据分箱带来的信息丢失，实现了更精准且高效的时间模式提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非负矩阵分解（NMF）处理事件数据时，通常需要对数据进行分箱或平滑处理，这会导致实体层面的异质性和细粒度时间特征的丢失。为了解决这一问题，研究者旨在开发一种能直接在连续时间上运行的分解模型。

Method: 提出EventNMF模型，将每个实体的事件建模为泊松过程，其强度函数通过非负B样条基进行分解，利用简单的估计过程恢复实体间共享的通用时间模板。

Result: 实验证明，EventNMF比传统的分箱计数方法更具优势，能有效处理偏差-方差权衡，并在合成数据和真实世界应用（如神经科学、地震学等）中展现出良好的解释性和计算效率。

Conclusion: EventNMF提供了一种直接处理连续时间事件数据的矩阵分解方法，通过引入B样条基，在保留精细时间特征的同时实现了可解释的模式提取，优于传统的离散化（分箱）方法。

Abstract: Continuous-time event data, in which entities emit instantaneous events over time, arises naturally across many domains such as neuroscience, seismology, and social networks. Non-negative matrix factorization (NMF) is a natural tool to uncover interpretable structure in such data, but it has so far only been applied after binning or smoothing the entity-level counting measures. This preprocessing step comes with the risk of erasing entity-level heterogeneities and fine-grained temporal features. In this paper, we introduce EventNMF, a continuous-time non-negative factorization model that operates directly on event times: each entity's events are modeled as a Poisson process whose intensity factorizes through a non-negative B-spline basis, and a simple estimation procedure recovers interpretable temporal templates shared across entities. The resulting method is mathematically principled, easy to implement, and computationally efficient. We further show that standard binned-count approaches arise as the special case of degree-zero splines, explore bias-variance tradeoffs and compare against existing methods on a synthetic latent factor model, and demonstrate the effectiveness of EventNMF on several real-world applications.

### [317] [Tracing the Oracle: Improving Diffusion Timestep Scheduling for 3D CT Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06236)
*Yujia Wu,Zhaoqiang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 TrO（Tracing the Oracle）框架，通过动态规划优化扩散模型的时间步调度，解决了 3D CT 重建中因截断误差导致的性能瓶颈，在极低计算预算下实现了更高质量的图像重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练扩散模型在解决 3D CT 逆问题时计算开销巨大，且现有的均匀时间步调度无法适配反向条件扩散随机微分方程的非均匀演化过程，导致严重的截断误差。为了在极少采样步数下提升重建质量，需要设计更优的时间步调度策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Tracing the Oracle (TrO)”的即插即用时间步调度框架。该方法首先对少量样本进行密集采样以生成参考“预言（Oracle）”轨迹，随后利用动态规划算法，通过最小化多步近似与预言轨迹之间的累积误差，全局优化采样时间步的分配。

Result: 在 AAPM 数据集上的实验结果表明，与现有的启发式调度相比，TrO 结合 DDS 方法在严格限制为 10 步以内的采样步数下，显著提升了 3D CT 重建的保真度与计算效率。

Conclusion: TrO 框架通过动态规划优化的时间步调度，为 3D CT 重建任务提供了一种在极低采样步数限制下仍能保持高重建质量的高效解决方案，证明了非均匀时间步调度对于减少扩散模型截断误差的重要性。

Abstract: Pretrained diffusion models demonstrate impressive potential in solving highly ill-posed 3D computed tomography (CT) inverse problems, while the inference process suffers from significant computational overhead. Furthermore, existing uniform timestep schedules fail to capture the non-uniform evolution of the reverse conditional diffusion stochastic differential equation, thereby introducing substantial truncation errors. To overcome this limitation, we propose Tracing the Oracle (TrO), a plug-and-play framework for improved timestep scheduling. Specifically, we treat densely sampled numerical integration trajectories on a few samples as the reference oracle. The optimized schedule is extracted by leveraging dynamic programming to globally minimize the cumulative error between the few-step approximation and the oracle. This mechanism precisely allocates the limited sampling steps to critical evolution stages that are highly susceptible to truncation errors. Our extensive experiments on the AAPM dataset across multiple 3D CT reconstruction tasks demonstrate that, when combined with the state-of-the-art 3D CT reconstruction method DDS, our optimized timesteps significantly improve reconstruction fidelity and computational efficiency compared to existing heuristic schedules, especially under a strict budget of no more than 10 sampling steps.

Method: 提出了一个统计场论框架，将LLM生成的Token嵌入向量视为一维链上的连续自旋变量；定义了基于双点关联函数的磁化率和基于系综平均嵌入场的序参量；利用TwoNN（最近邻）方法估算内在维度；并在不同参数规模（Qwen3：0.6B-32B）的模型上进行验证。

Abstract: We propose a statistical-field framework for text generated by large language models (LLMs), treating token embeddings as continuous spin variables on a one-dimensional chain. Defining a susceptibility from the connected two-point correlator and an order parameter from the ensemble-averaged embedding field, we vary the \texttt{softmax} temperature $T$ and observe a sharp susceptibility peak near a characteristic $T_c$ with power-law-like scaling, a concurrent rapid change in the order parameter, and a collapse onto a single semantic direction below $T_c$. The intrinsic dimension estimated by the two nearest neighbor (TwoNN) method independently corroborates these findings, reaching a minimum near $T_c$. Results are robust across model scales (Qwen3: 0.6B--32B) and prompt categories. While the phenomenology closely resembles a continuous phase transition, the non-equilibrium nature of autoregressive generation warrants further investigation. Our framework provides quantitative tools for probing the collective statistical structure of LLM outputs and suggests connections between decoding strategies and critical phenomena.

Our formulation enables applying the GFlowNet learning framework to OT problems on large graphs via edge flows and neural parameterization. ### [320] [PAC-Bayesian Adversarially Robust Generalization for Message Passing Graph Neural Networks: A Sensitivity Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06293)
*Ziling Liang,Xinping Yi,Qingsong Wen,Shi Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对消息传递图神经网络的改进型PAC-Bayesian分析框架，通过考虑参数的灵敏度异构性并利用雅可比矩阵的低秩特性，推导出了比现有研究更为紧致的对抗性泛化边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图神经网络对抗性泛化分析主要依赖各向同性高斯后验，无法有效捕捉参数的异构灵敏度，且复杂性项往往依赖于隐藏层宽度，导致泛化边界不够紧致。研究旨在克服这些限制，提供更精确的对抗性泛化保障。

Method: 研究者将灵敏度感知PAC-Bayesian框架推广至消息传递图神经网络（MPGNNs）。通过计算网络输出对权重的雅可比矩阵（Jacobians），量化不同参数块的灵敏度，并利用雅可比矩阵的低秩特性（秩不超过类别数K），构建了雅可比对齐的灵敏度矩阵。随后，使用经过优化的各向异性高斯后验分布替代传统的各向同性分布，以实现更紧致的KL散度上界。

Result: 理论分析表明，该方法成功将泛化边界中与隐藏层宽度相关的因子降低至与类别数K相关，显著提高了MPGNNs对抗性泛化边界的紧致性，能够更准确地描述模型在对抗攻击下的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入灵敏度感知框架，显著改善了图神经网络在对抗性环境下的鲁棒泛化边界理论，为设计更具鲁棒性的图神经网络提供了坚实的理论支持和指导。

Abstract: Whilst the vulnerability of graph neural networks (GNNs) to adversarial attacks poses a critical threat to graph representation learning, the understanding of the robust generalization behavior remains a fundamental challenge in the adversarial setting. Recently, PAC-Bayesian margin-based generalization analysis substantially advances this line of research by providing a flexible and data-dependent analytical framework. However, existing robust analyses often rely on isotropic Gaussian posteriors and control weight perturbations in the full parameter space, which limits the ability to capture heterogeneous parameter sensitivity yet hinges on hidden-width-dependent complexity terms, resulting in not-tight-enough generalization bounds. In this paper, we extend a recently proposed sensitivity-aware PAC-Bayesian framework from deep neural networks to message passing GNNs (MPGNNs) and derive a tighter robust generalization bound in the adversarial setting. Specifically, we first quantify how sensitive the perturbations across different parameter blocks are to the network outputs by deriving the output Jacobians with respect to the weight parameters. Exploiting the fact that these Jacobian matrices have rank at most $K$ in $K$-class graph classification, we then construct Jacobian-aligned sensitivity matrices and use anisotropic Gaussian posteriors with optimized covariances to upper bound the KL divergence in a tight way. Notably, by refining the spectral-norm dependence on the learned weights and reducing the leading dimension factor from hidden-width-dependent terms to the number of classes $K$, our analysis yields much tighter robust generalization guarantees for MPGNNs, thereby guiding their designs to enhance adversarial robustness.

### [321] [Reactive Flux Matching: Mechanism Discovery and Adaptive Sampling of Rare Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06295)
*Rishal Aggarwal,David Ryan Koes,Nicholas M. Boffi,Eric Vanden-Eijnden*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“通量匹配”框架，通过学习反应轨迹数据中的电流速度场和标量势函数，在无需已知系统动力学的情况下，实现了反应机制的解析、高效反应坐标的构建以及采样性能的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的路径采样方法虽然能生成反应轨迹集合，但难以从中直观且高效地提取反应机理（如主反应路径）以及构建有效的反应坐标。此外，传统的基于提交概率（committor）的方法在投影到非马尔可夫集体变量时存在局限性。

Method: 提出“通量匹配（Flux Matching）”框架，通过对反应轨迹集合进行加权 Helmholtz-Hodge 分解，学习电流速度场 u(z) 和标量势函数 h(z)。该方法通过最小化类似于生成模型中流匹配（flow matching）的二次泛函来实现。

Result: 通过分子系统验证，证明了该方法能够准确生成电流速度轨迹并计算反应速率常数，且其导出的势函数层集可作为增强采样方法的自适应界面。

Conclusion: Flux Matching 提供了一种无需先验动力学知识、且适用于非马尔可夫投影的强大框架，能有效解析复杂系统的反应机理，并为增强采样提供自适应的坐标构建方法。

Abstract: Path sampling methods generate ensembles of reactive trajectories connecting metastable states, but extracting mechanistic insight from these data remains nontrivial. We introduce Flux Matching, a framework that learns two complementary objects directly from reactive trajectory data: a current velocity $u(z)$, whose streamlines trace the dominant reaction pathways, and a scalar potential $h(z)$, obtained from a weighted Helmholtz-Hodge decomposition of the reactive current, that serves as a data-driven reaction coordinate. Both minimize quadratic functionals over the reactive path ensemble, analogous to the flow matching loss in generative modeling, and require no knowledge of the underlying dynamics or stationary distribution. Unlike committor-based methods, $u$ and $h$ remain well-defined under projection onto non-Markovian collective variables, and their level sets in turn provide adaptive interfaces for improved sampling with enhanced sampling methods. Flux Matching is validated through the generation of current velocity trajectories and rate constant calculations on molecular systems.

### [322] [Tangram: Unlocking Non-Uniform KV Cache for Efficient Multi-turn LLM Serving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06302)
*Hyungmin Kim,Minsoo Kim,Hongseok Kim,Jungwook Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Tangram 是一款专为高效处理非均匀 KV 缓存而设计的大模型推理服务系统，通过确定性内存分配、头组分页和预先负载均衡等技术，解决了传统系统在内存管理和调度上的低效问题，实现了显著的吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多轮大模型服务中，KV 缓存的线性增长给 GPU 内存和带宽带来了巨大压力。尽管非均匀 KV 压缩能够保留重要信息，但它会引入内存碎片化、调度复杂和内核利用率下降等系统性挑战，降低了现有服务的效率。

Method: Tangram 采用了三种核心技术：1. 确定性预算分配（Deterministic Budget Allocation）：通过为每个注意力头分配静态内存空间，消除动态调度开销；2. 头组分页（Head Group Page）：将具有相似保留需求的注意力头聚类，并利用向量化页表进行管理，最大化内存回收效率；3. 预先（AOT）负载均衡：利用静态预算配置，在无运行时开销的前提下确保 GPU 利用率均匀。

Result: 实验结果显示，与现有的基准系统相比，Tangram 在完全保持模型精度的前提下，能够将推理吞吐量提升至最高 2.6 倍。

Conclusion: Tangram 通过创新的内存管理策略，证明了非均匀 KV 缓存压缩在生产环境中的可行性，在不损失模型精度的前提下，显著提升了多轮对话 LLM 的推理吞吐量，为解决大规模部署下的内存瓶颈提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Multi-turn Large Language Model (LLM) serving is critical for consistent user experiences, yet the linear growth of the Key-Value (KV) cache imposes significant pressure on GPU memory and bandwidth. Non-uniform KV compression effectively preserves more information by considering the individual importance of each KV cache. However, such KV cache heterogeneity introduces various systemic challenges - including memory fragmentation, scheduling complexities, and diminished kernel utilization - which collectively lead to significant inefficiencies in existing LLM serving systems.
  To overcome these challenges, we present Tangram, a novel serving system designed to make Non-uniform KV caches practical. Tangram addresses systemic inefficiencies through three core techniques: (1) Deterministic Budget Allocation assigns a static memory footprint to each head based on its intrinsic pattern, entirely eliminating dynamic scheduling overhead and prefill stalls; (2) Head Group Page clusters attention heads with similar retention demands and manages them with independent, vectorized page tables, thereby maximizing physical memory reclamation; and (3) Ahead-of-Time (AOT) Load Balancing leverages static budget profiles to ensure uniform GPU utilization without runtime overhead. Experimental results show that Tangram improves throughput by up to 2.6x compared to existing baselines, while fully preserving model accuracy. Our implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/aiha-lab/TANGRAM.

</details>

Result: 在 DNA、蛋白质序列及分子生成任务中，GILC 均达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能水平，且在不进行额外训练的情况下，表现优于多种微调方法。

Abstract: Controllable generation with discrete diffusion models is often hindered by high computational overhead or the need for retraining. In this paper, we present \underline{\textbf{G}}radient-\underline{\textbf{I}}nformed \underline{\textbf{L}}ogit \underline{\textbf{C}}orrection (\textbf{GILC}), a plug-and-play framework that efficiently estimates guidance signals by repurposing the pretrained denoising network as a variational proxy. To circumvent the gradient instability inherent in high-dimensional discrete spaces, we introduce a Jacobian-free mechanism that directly corrects the clean prediction logits, facilitating stable and effective guidance. Our method accommodates both differentiable and non-differentiable reward functions. Extensive experiments across DNA, protein sequence, and molecular generation tasks demonstrate that GILC achieves state-of-the-art performance without additional training, frequently outperforming fine-tuning approaches.

### [324] [Learning What to Forget: Improving LLM Unlearning via Learned Token-Level Importance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06320)
*Gizem Yüce,Giorgos Nikolaou,Nicolas Flammarion*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为ATWU的机器遗忘框架，通过分析Token在遗忘和保留目标之间的冲突来自动识别需要遗忘的特定Token，实现了无需外部监督的高效、精准的语言模型知识清除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器遗忘方法在处理自回归语言模型时，通常忽视了样本内不同Token对遗忘目标贡献的差异性（异质性），或者过于依赖辅助模型、启发式规则及外部标注，导致计算复杂且效果受限。因此，研究者旨在寻找一种更有效、更直接的方法来评估Token级别的遗忘必要性。

Method: 提出了一种名为“交替Token加权遗忘（ATWU）”的方法。该方法将Token的遗忘特异性定义为“在该Token上最小化遗忘损失不与保留目标冲突的程度”。ATWU通过联合优化模型参数和基于隐藏状态的线性评分器（Token权重），在无需外部监督或辅助模型的情况下，动态学习每个Token的遗忘重要性，并以此对模型进行更新。

Result: 在TOFU和RWKU数据集上的实验表明，ATWU实现了最先进的遗忘与保留权衡（forget-retain trade-offs）。该方法不仅优于现有的样本级方法和基于概率的启发式方法，且其学习到的Token权重与真实遗忘区间高度一致，证明了其在识别语义化遗忘信号方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的ATWU框架证明了保留目标（retain objective）与遗忘目标之间的冲突是识别模型应遗忘知识的有效标准。通过无需外部监督的联合优化，模型能够自动学习Token级别的遗忘特异性，从而实现高效的机器遗忘，并显著优于现有的样本级及启发式方法。

Abstract: Machine unlearning aims to remove targeted knowledge from a trained model while preserving its general capabilities. For autoregressive language models, not all tokens in a forget sample are equally relevant to forgetting. Existing approaches either ignore this heterogeneity or rely on auxiliary models, heuristics, or external annotations to estimate each token's relevance for forgetting. We instead characterize it through the interaction with the retain objective: a token is forget-specific to the extent that minimizing the forget loss on that token does not conflict with retain optimality. We formalize this perspective as a joint optimization problem over the model parameters and the token weights and show that, under a natural separation condition, the resulting objective recovers the oracle forget-specific token support. Motivated by this formulation, we introduce Alternating Token-Weighted Unlearning (ATWU), a lightweight framework that jointly learns token forget-specificity and model parameters during unlearning using a simple linear scorer over the hidden states, without external token level supervision. Across TOFU and RWKU, ATWU achieves state of the art forget-retain trade-offs, outperforming sample-level methods, probability-based token weighting heuristics, and auxiliary-model-based approaches. Moreover, the learned scores align substantially better with ground truth forget-specific spans, indicating that ATWU identifies semantically meaningful token level forgetting signals. Overall, our results suggest that retain conflict provides an effective criterion for identifying what language models should forget, enabling unsupervised learning of token level forget-specificity directly from model representations with minimal computational overhead.

### [325] [PAMF: Prior-Aware Multimodal Fusion for Incomplete Time Series Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06328)
*Ziwen Kan,Wugeng Zheng,Tianlong Chen,Song Wang*

TL;DR: 针对医疗多模态时间序列中复杂的缺失问题，本文提出了 PAMF 框架，通过引入先验感知的流匹配技术区分不同缺失模式，并将补全与预测任务深度耦合，显著提升了数据缺失情况下的模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗多模态时间序列中普遍存在“模态内缺失”和“模态级缺失”两种结构截然不同的缺失模式。现有方法通常忽略了缺失模式的结构差异，且缺失补全与下游任务往往相互独立，导致补全过程无法利用任务相关信息，影响了最终预测效果。

Method: 提出 PAMF（Prior-Aware Flow Matching）框架：1. 使用基于类型特定先验的流匹配（Flow Matching）模型显式补全缺失数据，以区分两种缺失模式；2. 通过共享权重和架构匹配的编码器，将下游预测任务的表征反馈到补全过程中，实现任务间的耦合。

Result: 在多个多模态医疗时间序列基准测试中，PAMF 在各种缺失情境下均优于现有的主流补全和预测方法，表现出最强的综合性能。

Conclusion: PAMF 框架通过区分模态内和模态级缺失，并实现补全任务与下游预测任务的深度耦合，有效提升了多模态医疗时间序列在处理缺失数据时的预测性能。

Abstract: In healthcare, multimodal time series tasks often operate on incomplete observations in practice, for example when ECG segments are lost because electrodes detach or an entire respiratory channel is unavailable during overnight monitoring. Such missingness typically appears in two structurally distinct patterns: within-modality missing, where values are absent within an otherwise observed modality, and modality-level missing, where an entire modality is unavailable. Existing methods typically represent unobserved data implicitly through masks or missing embeddings, without learning instance-specific missing information, and most are designed for only one missingness pattern. A natural approach is to explicitly estimate the missing data; however, existing imputation methods treat missingness uniformly despite their different structural priors, and the imputation process is often isolated from downstream tasks, preventing downstream tasks from guiding imputation toward more informative representations. To address these limitations, we present PAMF, a multimodal time-series framework that explicitly handles different missingness patterns while coupling imputation with downstream prediction through prior-aware flow matching and weight sharing. Specifically, the method initializes the flow-matching source state with type-specific priors to distinguish two missing types. It further connects imputation and classification through architecturally matched encoders with weight sharing, transferring task-relevant representations into the imputation process. Experiments on multiple multimodal healthcare time-series benchmarks show that the proposed method achieves the strongest overall downstream performance across diverse datasets and missing settings compared with existing baselines.

### [326] [Efficient Mean Curvature Computation on High-Dimensional Data Manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06329)
*Alexandre L. M. Levada*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的高维数据局部平均曲率估计算法，通过代数简化与低秩近似技术，将计算复杂度从O(m⁴)降低至O(k²m)，实现了数量级的性能提升，为大规模几何感知机器学习提供了可行工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的局部平均曲率估计方法（如MCBP）在处理高维数据时，由于计算局部形状算子的复杂度高达O(m⁴)，导致在大规模特征集上无法高效应用，限制了几何感知机器学习方法的发展。

Method: 1. 代数简化：利用协方差矩阵特征向量的正交性和迹算子的循环性，推导出一个精确代数恒等式，绕过矩阵H的构造，将复杂度降低至O(m²)。2. 计算加速：利用局部协方差矩阵的低秩特性，采用截断SVD代替全特征分解；并基于哈尔测度下零空间外积的期望值，提出了一种解析近似方法，将计算复杂度进一步优化至O(k²m + kmp²)。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在真实数据集上的计算速度较原方法提升了50至300倍，且在保持高精度的同时，实现了曲率估计的规模化。

Conclusion: 该研究通过数学上的代数简化与奇异值分解优化，成功将局部平均曲率的计算复杂度从高阶降至近线性，使得在高维数据集上应用几何感知学习算法变得可行，极大拓展了曲率特征在现代机器学习中的应用前景。

Abstract: Estimating local mean curvature at each point of a high-dimensional dataset is a key ingredient of geometry-aware machine learning algorithms, such as the Mean Curvature Boundary Points (MCBP) method. The naive implementation of this computation, based on a local shape operator approximated from k-nearest neighbor patches, involves an explicit construction of a matrix $H$ whose trace form yields an $O(m^4)$ cost per point, rendering the approach intractable for datasets with more than a few dozen features. This paper introduces two complementary contributions that together reduce this cost by several orders of magnitude. The first contribution is an exact algebraic identity. This identity, derived from the orthogonality of the eigenvectors of the covariance matrix and the cyclicity of the trace operator, eliminates $H$ entirely and reduces the per-point cost to $O(m^2)$ after the eigendecomposition. The second contribution addresses the remaining $O(m^3)$ bottleneck of the full eigendecomposition. Since the local covariance matrix has rank at most $k-1 \ll m$, we replace it with a truncated SVD of the $k \times m$ centered data matrix, an $O(k^2 m)$ operation, and derive an analytical approximation for the contribution of the null-space eigenvectors based on the expected value of their outer product under the Haar measure. The resulting estimator has total cost $O(k^2 m + k m p^2)$, where $p = k-1$. Experiments on real-world datasets confirm speedups of 50 to 300 times relative to the original implementation, with negligible loss when the fast estimator is used to replace the original version. By providing a scalable and data-driven estimate of local curvature, the proposed method establishes curvature as a practical geometric feature for a broad range of machine learning tasks, from classical to modern deep learning pipelines.

### [327] [Subspace-Aware Sparse Autoencoders for Effective Mechanistic Interpretability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06333)
*Seyed Arshan Dalili,Mehrdad Mahdavi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对稀疏自编码器（SAE）因强行将特征建模为一维向量而导致的“特征分裂”问题，本文提出了一种子空间感知稀疏自编码器（SASA）。该方法通过引入多维解码子空间与块稀疏约束，显著提高了特征的可解释性，同时将训练效率提升至多项式复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稀疏自编码器（SAE）将每个潜在特征建模为一维向量，这与大型语言模型中特征本质上是多维的结构不匹配。这种建模假设会导致“特征分裂”现象，即单一的高维特征被强行拆解为多个近乎共线的维数，导致特征表征冗余、产生虚假多重性，并增加了训练负担。

Method: 提出了子空间感知稀疏自编码器（SASA）。该方法将传统的单向量解码器替换为可学习的解码子空间；通过“Top-s”组门控机制强制实施块稀疏性；并利用核范数正则化来适应每个特征组的有效秩，从而能够以多维方式精确表示模型特征。

Result: 理论证明了SASA能够将表示复杂特征的样本复杂度从指数级降低至多项式级。在GPT-2和Mistral-7B上的实验结果表明，SASA在仅使用约一半训练数据的情况下，能够有效减少特征分裂与吸收，并达到甚至超过标准SAE的单义性和可解释性表现。

Conclusion: 研究表明，传统的稀疏自编码器（SAE）因假设特征是一维的，导致模型中存在严重的特征分裂现象。通过引入“子空间感知稀疏自编码器（SASA）”，利用子空间解码器代替单一向量，并结合块稀疏与核范数正则化，能够有效解决特征分裂问题，在降低训练成本的同时显著提升了特征的可解释性与单义性，为大规模语言模型的机理可解释性提供了更高效的工具。

Abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) are widely used for mechanistic interpretability in large language models, yet their formulation assigns each latent feature a single decoder direction, implicitly assuming features to be one-dimensional. We show that this assumption mismatches with the multi-dimensional structure of model features, provably inducing feature splitting through two distinct mechanisms. Geometrically, reconstructing a feature of intrinsic dimension $d_i \ge 2$ to error $\varepsilon$ with single-direction decoders forces a number of atoms that is exponential in $d_i$. From an end-to-end optimization perspective, this splitting is not merely possible but actively preferred. We prove that there exists a continuous path from the true $d_i$-dimensional basis to a strictly lower risk of the $\ell_1$-regularized SAE objective, whose descent directions drive any trained dictionary into that exponential regime. A single coherent feature is therefore fragmented across many near-collinear latents, producing spurious multiplicity and obscuring the intrinsic geometry. Motivated by this, we introduce Subspace-Aware Sparse Autoencoders (SASA), which replace single-vector decoders with learned decoder subspaces, enforce block sparsity via Top-$s$ group gating, and adapt each group's effective rank with a nuclear-norm regularizer. We then show that once the block size satisfies $r \ge d_i$, a single group not only can represent the entire feature slice but is the global minimizer of the SASA objective. This consolidation yields a sample complexity polynomial in $d_i$ rather than exponential -- a decisive advantage given that every training activation costs an LLM forward pass. Empirically, on GPT-2 and Mistral-7B, SASA reduces feature splitting and absorption, improves monosemanticity and interpretability, and matches or exceeds standard SAEs while training on roughly half the token budget.

</details>


### [328] [Quantifying the Privacy of Counterfactuals by Leveraging Membership Inference Attacks Against Synthetic Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06334)
*Maryam Babaei,Yingke Wang,Hadrien Lautraite,Heber H. Arcolezi,Ulrich Aivodji,Sebastien Gambs*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了反事实解释带来的隐私安全风险，证明了即便没有模型访问权限，攻击者也可以利用反事实样本进行成员推理攻击，从而危及原始模型的训练数据隐私。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反事实解释常用于高风险决策场景以提高模型透明度，但这种解释方式可能被滥用以窃取隐私。研究者旨在探讨反事实解释是否会被当作泄露模型训练数据隐私的工具，并评估在缺乏模型访问权限时隐私泄露的风险。

Method: 本研究将反事实样本视为一种类合成数据，通过借鉴针对合成数据的成员推理攻击方法，评估其在不同类型反事实上的有效性。特别是在无须直接访问原始模型（黑盒场景）的情况下，仅利用公开的离线反事实样本集合，验证了成员推理攻击的可行性。

Result: 实验结果表明，针对合成数据设计的成员推理攻击同样适用于反事实样本。即使在无法直接查询原始模型的情况下，仅通过获取的一组反事实样本，攻击者仍能实现有效的成员推理攻击，证明了反事实解释具有显著的隐私泄露风险。

Conclusion: 反事实解释可能成为隐私泄露的途径。研究强调模型开发者在向用户公开反事实解释时必须谨慎，因为即使在无法访问原始模型的情况下，攻击者也能仅利用一组反事实样本成功实施成员推理攻击，从而危及训练数据的隐私。

Abstract: Counterfactuals are typically used in high-stakes decision areas to explain a machine learning model by showing how changes to the user profiles result in the desired outcome. However, explaining the model's decisions through counterfactuals can also be exploited by an adversary to conduct privacy attacks against the model or its training data. Drawing on the analogy that counterfactuals provide realistic substitutes for real training data, similar to synthetic data, we demonstrate in this paper how it is possible to successfully perform privacy attacks on counterfactuals by drawing on the attacks developed against synthetic data. More precisely, we investigate the effectiveness of the membership inference attacks designed for synthetic data on various types of counterfactuals. Additionally, while existing membership inference attacks against counterfactuals usually require to be able to query the model, we show how it is possible to perform successful membership inference attacks using only a set of counterfactuals, with no access to the model from which they are generated. Our results demonstrate that model developers should be more cautious when releasing counterfactuals to various users, as it can lead to a privacy breach.

### [329] [Bridging Domain Expertise and Generalization for Performance Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06335)
*Shuxuan Li,Zhilin Zhao,Quyu Kong,Wei-Shi Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决分布偏移下模型性能估计不准确的问题，本文提出了 FRAP 方法，通过巧妙融合外部基础模型的鲁棒性与基准模型的领域专长，构建了更可靠的性能参考标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的分布偏移下的性能估计方法往往过度依赖模型自身的预测输出，而当发生分布偏移时，模型自身的偏差会被放大，导致预测结果与真实性能之间的相关性显著下降。因此，需要引入外部信息来构建更可靠的“真实标签”替代指标。

Method: 提出了一种名为“融合参考对齐预测”（FRAP）的新框架。该方法首先通过温度缩放校准来对齐基础模型（Foundation Model）与基准模型（Base Model）的预测分布，随后利用基于置信度的加权机制将两者融合，构建出更可靠的参考分布，最后通过衡量基准模型与该参考分布的契合度来实现性能估计。

Result: 在多种数据集和模型架构上的广泛实验表明，FRAP 在分布偏移环境下相较于现有的代表性性能估计方法，能够提供持续且显著的性能提升。

Conclusion: FRAP 通过融合基础模型和基准模型的预测分布，有效缓解了在分布偏移场景下仅依赖模型自身输出所带来的偏差，为无标签数据下的模型性能估计提供了一种鲁棒且准确的解决方案。

Abstract: Performance estimation under distribution shift aims to predict how a model behaves on an unlabeled test set whose distribution differs from the training data, a scenario that requires reliable indicators that can faithfully reflect model behavior without ground-truth labels. Existing approaches rely solely on the outputs of the given model whose biases are amplified once the distribution shifts, weakening the correlation with the true performance. Motivated by this limitation, we propose Fused Reference Alignment Prediction (FRAP), which leverages the complementary strengths of an external foundation model and the base model to construct a more reliable surrogate of the ground-truth labels. FRAP aligns the prediction distribution of the foundation model with that of the base model by applying temperature-scaled calibration that minimizes their divergence. The aligned predictions are fused through confidence-based weighting into a refined reference distribution that integrates robustness from the foundation model and domain-specific expertise from the base model, and performance estimation is obtained by measuring how closely the base model predictions agree with this reference. Extensive experiments across diverse datasets and architectures show that FRAP provides consistent and substantial improvements over representative performance-estimation methods under distribution shift.

### [330] [Equivariant Neural Belief Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06344)

Motivation: 现有的等变网络通常只能处理标量或向量，无法表达各向异性的不确定性（即二阶精度张量），且在处理多模态能量景观时容易导致物理意义缺失的平均化，难以胜任空间嵌入变量的概率推断任务。

Method: 提出了等变神经置信传播（ENBP）框架。主要创新点包括：1. 消息表示采用等变高斯混合模型；2. 利用等变外积构建二阶精度矩阵；3. 使用可微分谱分解处理矩阵；4. 设计了与 SE(3) 对称性相容的贪婪 KL 散度混合模型简化算法。

Result: 在 GEOM-QM9 和 GEOM-Drugs 数据集上，ENBP 实现了 98.9% 的构象覆盖率，误差仅为 0.090 Å，且推理速度比扩散模型基线快 100 倍以上。在多智能体机器人推断中，ENBP 表现出极高的收敛性和碰撞规避能力，等变误差低至 10^-7 级别。

Conclusion: ENBP 通过引入 SE(3) 等变高斯混合模型，有效解决了空间嵌入变量推断中的各向异性不确定性建模与多模态分布表示问题。该方法在分子构象生成和多智能体机器人任务中均表现出极高的效率、精度与鲁棒性，证明了对称性约束在复杂概率推断中的核心价值。

Abstract: Probabilistic inference over spatially embedded variables requires beliefs that respect $SE(3)$ symmetry, yet existing equivariant networks produce only scalars and vectors -- not the rank-2 precision tensors needed for anisotropic uncertainty, and single-component messages collapse multi-modal energy landscapes to physically meaningless averages. We introduce Equivariant Neural Belief Propagation (ENBP), a factor-graph framework whose messages are equivariant Gaussian mixture models with sufficient statistics that transform exactly under $SE(3)$. Rank-2 precision matrices are synthesised via equivariant outer products, ingested through differentiable spectral decomposition, and kept tractable by a greedy KL-based mixture reduction that provably commutes with $SE(3)$. On GEOM-QM9 and GEOM-Drugs, ENBP achieves 98.9% conformational coverage at 0.090 $\mathring{A}$ error with sub-second latency -- over $100\times$ faster than diffusion baselines at higher accuracy. On multi-body robotic inference, vanilla loopy BP diverges at 15+ agents while ENBP converges with near-zero collision rates and machine-precision equivariance error (${\sim}10^{-7}$ vs.\ $10^{-1}$ for augmented baselines).

</details>


### [331] [Performance Evaluation of GraphCast for Medium-Range Weather Forecasting over Brazil](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06348)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现，GraphCast在巴西表现出明显的季节性差异：在南半球冬季，针对南部地区的斜压系统，GraphCast在2-7天的中短期预报中表现逊于IFS，但在延伸期预报中具有平滑误差的优势；在夏季雨季，GraphCast能准确捕捉大尺度水汽输送，并有效抑制了导致确定性预报偏差的高频对流变率。

Conclusion: GraphCast在巴西地区的预测表现具有显著的区域和季节依赖性。虽然在处理小尺度对流和部分快速移动天气系统时存在局限，但在湿季大尺度水汽传输预测方面表现优异。本研究明确了AI气象预报模型在热带地区的物理边界，为未来针对性的“热带化”改进提供了关键依据。

Abstract: The paradigm of global weather forecasting is rapidly shifting with the emergence of Machine Learning Weather Prediction models (MLWP). While these data-driven architectures demonstrate remarkable global skill, regional benchmarks in the Global South remain scarce, leaving their efficacy in complex, highly convective environments largely unverified. This study evaluates the performance of GraphCast operational against the deterministic ECMWF IFS HRES as baseline across four distinct Brazilian climatic sub-regions. Utilizing a scalable, cloud-native pipeline and the WeatherBench-X framework for benchmarking weather models, we assess selected tropospheric variables ($T_{850}$, $Q_{850}$, $Z_{500}$) over four selected seasonal windows, employing the operational IFS analysis as the ground truth to calculate the statistical metrics for both models. Results reveal a regime-dependent skill profile. During the austral winter, GraphCast underperforms in the medium range (lead days 2-7) for $Z_{500}$ when resolving fast-propagating baroclinic systems over southern Brazil, but regains an advantage in the extended range, where its inherent smoothing of chaotic small-scale variability becomes beneficial under deterministic skill metrics. Conversely, during the austral summer wet season, GraphCast accurately captures large-scale moisture transport while intrinsically dampening the high-frequency convective variability that degrades deterministic NWP temperature forecasts. These findings establish a baseline for Brazil and define the specific physical boundaries that will guide future ``tropicalization'' efforts, aiming to optimize these foundational AI models for regional resilience.

To tackle this, we focus on optimising corner kick routines, and formulate a decision-making problem in which a central policy makes adjustments to attacking player positions and velocities to maximise first contact shot probability. ### [333] [End-to-End Subgraph Detection with GraphDETR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06364)
*Dexiong Chen,Till Hendrik Schulz,Karsten Borgwardt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GraphDETR 是一种基于 Transformer 的深度学习框架，它将子图检测视为集合预测问题，通过端到端训练实现了大图中复杂模式的高效、准确及近似匹配，突破了传统组合算法的性能瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 子图检测问题（如子图同构）本质上是 NP 完全问题，传统的组合优化算法在处理大图或复杂模式时计算复杂度过高，难以应对实际需求。此外，现有方法难以自然地支持近似匹配，因此需要一种更高效、更具扩展性的机器学习方法来解决该问题。

Method: 作者引入了 GraphDETR 框架，将子图检测问题转化为集合预测问题（类似于计算机视觉中的 DETR 模型）。该方法利用图神经网络对目标图进行编码，通过一组可学习的查询向量（Query Vectors）输入 Transformer 解码器，并结合二分匹配（Bipartite Matching）进行端到端的联合训练，从而实现单次前向传递中完成所有模式实例的识别。

Result: 实验表明，GraphDETR 能有效识别包含高达 50 个节点的模式（如分子结构、团、环及模糊模式），且能处理 1000 个节点的大型目标图。在 ChEMBL 数据集的分子功能组检测任务中，该模型表现出色，平均精度（AP100）达到 91.2。

Conclusion: GraphDETR 证明了将子图检测建模为集合预测问题不仅可行，而且在处理大规模图和复杂模式识别时，比传统的组合搜索方法更具效率和灵活性。该框架为图数据中的模式匹配提供了一种强大的端到端深度学习替代方案。

Abstract: Subgraph detection seeks to identify whether and where instances of query patterns occur within a larger graph. This problem is fundamental across scientific domains and is closely related to subgraph isomorphism, which is NP-complete, limiting combinatorial approaches to small patterns or moderately sized graphs. We introduce GraphDETR, a deep learning framework that formulates subgraph detection as a set prediction problem, analogous to DETR in object detection. GraphDETR encodes the target graph with a graph neural network, and employs a fixed set of learnable query vectors, decoded via a transformer decoder, to predict all pattern occurrences jointly in a single forward pass. This is enabled by training the model end-to-end with bipartite matching. Unlike traditional combinatorial methods that only solve exact structural matching, GraphDETR naturally extends to approximate matching, enabling detection beyond exact pattern correspondence. Empirically, we show that GraphDETR can detect diverse patterns, such as molecular structures, cycles, cliques, and fuzzy patterns of up to 50 nodes, in target graphs with up to 1000 nodes. We further evaluate on molecular functional group detection over the ChEMBL dataset, where GraphDETR predicts the complete set of functional groups per molecule, achieving a strong performance of $\text{AP}_{100} = 91.2$.

### [334] [Learned Response-Field Inertia Operator for HEC-RAS 2D Water-Surface Elevation Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06385)
*Edward Holmberg,Elias Ioup,Md Meftahul Ferdaus,Mahdi Abdelguerfi,Julian Simeonov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为LRFIO的机器学习代理模型，用于直接在HEC-RAS 2D的原始非结构化网格上进行高效水位预测。通过分层增量学习和自适应模型复杂度控制，该方法在保持高精度的同时，实现了比传统数值求解器快数万倍的推理速度，且避免了传统方法中的数据重映射误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的HEC-RAS 2D水力模拟计算代价高昂。现有的代理模型常受限于栅格重映射误差和信息访问混淆，无法直接在原始非均匀计算网格上进行一致性预测。因此，本研究旨在开发一种高效、能够直接在原生网格上运行、且能根据任务复杂度自适应调整的代理模型，以加速水面高程（WSE）的预测过程。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“学习响应场惯性算子”（LRFIO）的方法，旨在HEC-RAS 2D的非结构化原生网格上直接进行水位预测，避免了栅格重映射带来的误差。该方法采用一种基于增量的策略，通过学习求解器轨迹来校准惯性响应算子。模型构建采用了分层评估策略（持久性、全局校准惯性、分段响应场惯性），并引入了模型选择器来平衡预测精度与复杂性，仅在验证证据支持时增加模型复杂度。

Result: LRFIO在四个不同的HEC-RAS 2D基准测试中表现出良好的适应性和模型复杂度控制，最大验证遗憾值仅为4.30%。在部署阶段，LRFIO实现了显著的计算加速，推演时间控制在0.003秒到0.242秒之间；在Beaver Bayou测试案例中，相比传统HEC-RAS求解器，实现了约2.75万倍的视界归一化加速。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于原生网格的增量预测是一种强大的求解器条件化预测框架。对于复杂的建模组件（如神经网络或空间复杂度），仅当经验证据显示其具有显著性能增益时才应引入，以保持模型的简洁性与鲁棒性。该方法证明了在计算流体动力学中利用机器学习实现高效、高保真代理模型的潜力。

Abstract: This article presents a cross-dataset evaluation of learned native-cell surrogate models for solver-consistent water-surface elevation (WSE) prediction in HEC-RAS 2D. To avoid raster remapping error and information-access confounding, surrogates are evaluated directly on the original nonuniform computational cells under an explicit policy that separates static project inputs, current hydraulic state, project-input forcing, calibration-derived quantities, and future solver-output targets. We introduce the Learned Response-Field Inertia Operator (LRFIO), a no-forcing, increment-based learned surrogate that calibrates an inertial response operator from solved HEC-RAS trajectories and deploys the retained operator through closed-form native-cell rollout. LRFIO evaluates a base-case-first response hierarchy consisting of persistence, global calibrated inertia, and segmented response-field inertia. Segmentation, residual correction, and neuralized inertia are treated as learnable modeling choices, with added complexity retained only when validation evidence justifies its cost. Evaluated across four diverse HEC-RAS 2D benchmarks, LRFIO retains different response structures for different domains, demonstrating adaptive learned complexity. The selector audit shows controlled complexity with a maximum validation regret of 4.30%. During deployment, retained rollout times range from 0.003 s to 0.242 s, and the Beaver Bayou measured-solve comparison gives an estimated 2.75 x 10^4 horizon-normalized speedup over HEC-RAS. These results indicate that the current native-cell increment is a strong solver-conditioned predictive scaffold and that added response-field, neural, or spatial complexity should be retained only when empirically justified.

### [335] [Proper Scoring Rules for Right-Censored Survival Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06393)
*Jef Jonkers,Glenn Van Wallendael,Luc Duchateau,Sofie Van Hoecke*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种处理右删失生存数据的通用正则评分框架，通过将预测分布映射至观测数据空间，实现了对多种生存评估指标的标准化处理，有效解决了模型训练与评估中的偏倚与排序问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 正则评分规则（Proper scoring rules）是概率预测训练与评估的理论基石，但在处理生存分析中常见的右删失数据（Right censoring）时，由于事件时间仅被部分观测，传统的评分规则无法直接适用，因此需要开发适用于删失数据的正则评分方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于映射的评分框架：首先将预测分布通过删失机制进行映射，进而在诱导出的观测数据分布上应用原始的正则评分规则。针对不同的删失情况，该框架推导出了局部评分（针对固定删失时间）和边际评分（针对随机或部分观测的删失时间），并进一步扩展至多变量生存建模中的“删失回归”（censored engression）。

Result: 理论上证明了边际评分在条件独立删失假设下是正则的，且在可识别区域内是严格正则的。实验表明，该方法在多种删失环境下能正确对最优预测（Oracle）进行排序，避免了现有加权评分方法中常见的排序逆转问题，且“删失回归”显著提升了模型在删失数据上的训练效果。

Conclusion: 该研究通过一种通用的框架，解决了生存分析中右删失数据无法直接应用传统评分规则的问题。该方法不仅统一了现有的似然和IPCW类准则，还扩展了CRPS和Brier Score等常用评估指标，证明了其在模型训练和性能评估中的理论严谨性和实践有效性。

Abstract: Proper scoring rules provide a rigorous theoretical basis for the training and evaluation of probabilistic forecasts. However, in the presence of right censoring, the event time is only partially observed, rendering conventional scoring rules inapplicable in their standard form. We propose a framework for proper scoring of right-censored survival outcomes based on a simple idea: first, map the predictive distribution through the censoring mechanism, then apply the underlying proper score on the induced observed-data law. This yields localized scores for fixed censoring times and marginalized scores when the censoring time is random or only partially observed. The resulting construction recovers familiar right-censored likelihood and IPCW-type criteria within a coherent framework, while also yielding right-censored versions of the CRPS, pinball loss, Brier score, and energy score. We show that the marginalized score is proper under conditional independent censoring and strictly proper on the identifiable region. The same principle also leads to censored engression, a sample-based learning objective for multivariate right-censored survival modeling. In experiments, our scores correctly rank the oracle forecast across several censoring regimes, whereas forecast-dependent plug-in weighted scores can exhibit ranking reversals. Censored engression likewise substantially improves over naive training on censored outcomes.

### [336] [The Post-GCN Decade Revisited: Curvature-Stratified Evaluation of Relational Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06397)
*Shuo Wang,Xiangyu Wang,Quanxin Wang,Bailin Wu,Bokui Wang,Shunyang Huang,Boyan Deng,Haonan Liu,Ruiyi Fang,Zhenxiang Xu,Boyu Wang,Zhao Kang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出，当前关系学习的统一排行榜忽略了数据的内在几何结构（如曲率），导致评价指标具有误导性。为此，作者提出了曲率分层评估框架，证实了模型表现高度依赖于数据的几何特性，并呼吁建立更具几何感知力的评估范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的关系学习评估体系过度依赖对异构数据集的平均性能表现，这种做法忽略了数据集底层的几何结构差异，导致系统性偏差，使得评价结果无法准确反映模型的真实泛化能力。

Method: 作者提出了一种“曲率分层评估框架”（curvature-stratified evaluation framework），将数据集根据曲率（正、负、零）进行划分。研究在14个数据集上评估了18种代表性模型（包括GCN、图基础模型及表格学习方法），通过对比不同曲率区间内的模型表现来验证几何属性对模型有效性的影响。

Result: 研究发现，模型在特定曲率区间内的排名相对稳定，但在跨区间时会发生显著变化；这证实了性能表现是几何依赖性的。此外，研究指出在某些特定几何环境下，昂贵的图基础模型（GFMs）相比针对几何结构优化的图神经网络（GNNs）收益递减。

Conclusion: 模型在关系学习中的性能并非普适的，而是高度依赖于数据集的几何结构（如曲率）。传统的平均评估方法掩盖了这一关键特性。研究强调，未来的模型评估应当采用考虑几何特性的分层框架，以实现更公平、准确和可解释的性能对比。

Abstract: Current evaluation practices in relational learning rely heavily on flat leaderboards that average performance across heterogeneous datasets, implicitly assuming a uniform underlying structure. We show that this assumption introduces systematic bias: it obscures geometry-dependent performance variations and can lead to misleading conclusions about model generalization. In this work, we identify intrinsic geometry as a key latent factor governing model effectiveness. We demonstrate that conventional aggregated metrics mask critical performance trade-offs that only become visible when datasets are stratified by their geometric properties. To address this issue, we introduce a curvature-stratified evaluation framework that partitions datasets into positive, negative, and near-zero curvature regimes. Our benchmark evaluates 18 representative models including Graph Convolutional Networks (GCNs), Graph Foundation Models (GFMs), and tabular learning methods across 14 datasets. We find that model rankings are highly stable within each curvature regime but shift significantly across regimes, indicating that performance is fundamentally geometry-dependent rather than universally transferable. Notably, we identify regimes where GFMs offer diminishing returns compared to geometry-aligned GNNs. Based on these findings, we propose a geometry-aware evaluation protocol that yields more reliable and interpretable comparisons than standard aggregated benchmarks. We release all code, curvature-stratified dataset splits, and evaluation tools to support reproducible and rigorous assessment of future relational learning methods. Code and datasets are provided in our project homepage: https://sirbabbage.github.io/CurvBench_HOME/.

</details>


### [337] [Double Preconditioning (DoPr): Optimization for Test-Time Performance, not Validation Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06418)
*Thomas T. Zhang,Alok Shah,Yifei Zhang,Vincent Zhang,Nikolai Matni,Max Simchowitz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对深度学习中“训练与部署方式不匹配”导致的误差累积问题（TTF），提出了双重预处理（DoPr）优化算法，通过结合梯度与激活预处理，显著提升了模型在自回归任务中的实际表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代深度学习应用（如语言模型、机器人策略学习）常采用“单步预测损失训练、多步滚动部署”的范式。这种范式会导致“测试时反馈（TTF）”现象，即训练指标与下游任务表现之间出现偏离，且随任务长度增加而加剧。现有研究多关注数据、架构或损失函数设计，而本文旨在通过改进优化策略来解决这一问题。

Method: 作者引入了双重预处理（DoPr）优化方法。该方法结合了基于梯度的预处理（如 Adam 和 Muon）与基于激活的预处理（Activation-wise Preconditioning, AP，类似于 KFAC）。DoPr 旨在通过在优化层面直接干预，以缓解模型在自回归部署过程中产生的误差累积。

Result: 实验证明，将激活预处理（AP）加入到现有优化器中，能有效提升模型在多种 TTF 场景下的下游任务表现。值得注意的是，这些性能提升并不总是伴随着验证集损失的改善，这表明传统的单步监督损失评估方式存在局限性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种针对测试时反馈（TTF）现象的新优化范式“双重预处理（DoPr）”。研究表明，仅依靠改善验证集损失并不足以保证下游任务性能的提升，优化方法本身应被视为缓解误差累积的关键设计轴。这一发现对深度学习模型的评估和训练目标设计提出了新的挑战。

Abstract: Many modern applications of deep learning involve training a neural network via a one-step prediction loss (e.g., $L^2$ regression, cross-entropy), but deploy the network by rolling out along its own predictions. Key examples include autoregressive language modeling, flow-based generative modeling, and robot policy learning. It is well-documented that these settings induce a phenomenon we call test-time feedback (TTF): the mismatch between the training/validation loss and downstream metrics of interest, such as task success rate and generation quality, which grows with task length. While data curation, architecture, and objective design have been proposed to combat train-test shift in TTF settings, this paper proposes optimization as a new design axis to mitigate error accumulation. Specifically, we introduce a new optimization paradigm called double-preconditioning (DoPr) uniquely tailored to the challenges of TTF. DoPr combines gradient-wise preconditioning, as in Adam and Muon, with activation-wise preconditioning (AP), such as in KFAC. We show that the addition of AP yields a drop-in intervention for increasing downstream model performance across a range of TTF settings. Interestingly, these gains in test-time performance do not consistently accompany improvements in validation loss, opening new questions about how to properly evaluate models trained with one-step supervised objectives.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于优化的贝叶斯网络构建方法往往忽略了数据中可能存在的多种因果链条，且倾向于输出单一的有向无环图（DAG），这可能无法真实反映复杂系统数据中固有的因果不确定性与多重性。

Method: 提出了一种基于信息熵的推断方法，通过对图结构进行最大熵抽样，构建出与数据一致的“因果关系图谱”（atlases of plausible causal relationships），并将其应用于2节点和20节点的线性结构方程模型模拟数据中进行验证。

Conclusion: 通过最大熵推断构建因果关系图谱，不仅能够量化因果关系中的结构模糊性，还能避免单一优化方法可能引入的虚假因果伪影，为理解复杂系统中的多重因果路径提供了更稳健的框架。

Abstract: Data-driven causal relationship identification is pertinent to advancing understanding of complex systems both within and beyond science. Bayesian networks offer a probabilistic method for modelling generic causal relationships via directed acyclic graphs (DAGs). However, typical techniques for constructing Bayesian networks rely on optimization, which can be ill-suited for learning causal relationships because the underlying data may admit multiple chains of causation. More data-faithful representations of causal relationships would provide frameworks for constructing multiple causal maps that are consistent with the variability that is inherent in underlying data. Here, we show that entropy-based inference generates atlases of plausible causal relationships that are consistent with underlying data. On simulated noisy data of 2- and 20-node linear structural equation models, we sample a maximum-entropy ensemble of graphs that allow us to quantify the inherent structural ambiguity in underlying causal relationships. Our method shows that "optimized" DAGs can contain causal artifacts are not consistent across equivalently accurate topologies.

When these functions interact, they can interfere with one another in ways that are difficult to detect from raw network data alone. A key missing piece for managing such interactions is a reliable, interpretable dependency structure that captures which control parameters are actively influencing which network performance outcomes at any given time. This paper focuses on the event-detection step needed to support such dependency learning by converting noisy continuous telemetry into binary indicators of parameter activity and KPI response. The central difficulty is that not every fluctuation in the data reflects a genuine control interaction, so the method must distinguish real parameter-outcome relationships from background variation. Because real AI-RAN traffic traces with known parameter-KPI ground truth are difficult to obtain, we introduce a synthetic closed-loop traffic generator with planted latent dependencies. We use this controlled telemetry to evaluate a machine-learning-based dependency recovery pipeline that formulates the conversion of continuous traces into binary event indicators as a significance-detection problem. Experimental evaluation shows that the proposed pipeline reliably recovers the latent dependency structure from noisy continuous traces when the signal is sufficiently separated from background variation, while highlighting threshold calibration as the key factor controlling event-detection quality. These results constitute a foundational step toward interpretable dependency learning for adaptive AI-RAN control systems.

### [341] [PC Layer: Polynomial Weight Preconditioning for Improving LLM Pre-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06470)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决大语言模型训练过程中权重矩阵条件数不稳定导致收敛困难或训练不稳定的问题，旨在通过一种轻量级且无额外推理开销的方式来优化权重参数的谱特性。

Method: 提出了预处理层（Preconditioning layer, PC layer），利用低次多项式参数化权重矩阵，从而在训练过程中重塑权重的奇异值谱。该模块在训练完成后可直接合并至原始权重中，确保推理阶段零额外开销；此外，通过对深度线性网络的研究，在理论上证明了奇异值控制对梯度下降收敛至全局最小值的保障作用。

Abstract: We propose a preconditioning (PC) layer, a weight parameterization via polynomial preconditioner that ensures stable weight conditioning throughout LLM training. The PC module reshapes the singular-value spectrum of weight matrices via low-degree polynomial preconditioning. After training, the preconditioned weights can be merged back into the original architecture, incurring no inference overhead. We demonstrate the advantage of the proposed PC layer over standard transformers in Llama-1B pre-training, for both the AdamW and Muon optimizers. Theoretically, we justify this spectrum-control principle by proving that uniformly bounding each layer's singular values ensures geometric convergence of gradient descent to global minima, for certain deep linear networks. Our code is available at https://github.com/Empath-aln/PC-layer.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于强化学习（如 GRPO）的推理模型训练面临延迟奖励导致的高方差问题；而传统的蒙特卡洛方法用于信用分配时计算开销巨大，无法满足长上下文下的高效训练需求。

Method: 提出了 RREDCoT（思维链奖励重分配）方法，利用模型自身对思维链步骤进行价值评估，从而在无需额外生成采样的前提下，通过学习分配信用权重来优化奖励信号，替代了传统的高方差蒙特卡洛（MC）方法。

Abstract: Recent advancements in reasoning language models have been driven by Reinforcement Learning (RL) fine-tuning. Most often, these rely on the Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) algorithm or modifications thereof to steer the models to produce Chain-of-Thought (CoT) traces. The final answer can only be verified, and the reward assigned, after the CoT trace is complete, making it a delayed reward problem. GRPO and its modifications correspond to Monte Carlo methods in standard RL, which are known to suffer from high variance. A possible solution to this problem is the redistribution of rewards through credit assignment, where segments of the CoT trace that are important for arriving at the desirable solution are emphasized by assigning a higher reward. While Monte Carlo sampling can be used to provide an unbiased estimate of intermediate state values, its computational overhead makes it unsuitable for train-time credit assignment in long contexts at high granularity. We introduce RREDCoT (Reward REDistribution for Chain of Thoughts), which utilizes the model itself to approximate the optimal reward redistribution without additional generation. We investigate the advantages of our method compared to MC sampling and several attribution methods. We further analyze several aspects relevant to the construction of the redistribution such as segmentation of CoT traces and state value estimation.

### [343] [Pretraining Recurrent Networks without Recurrence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06479)
*Akarsh Kumar,Phillip Isola*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 SMT 的 RNN 训练新方法，通过将递归训练简化为一步记忆转移的监督学习任务，消除了传统 BPTT 的序列计算限制，实现了时间并行化训练，并有效解决了长期依赖学习难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统递归神经网络（RNN）训练依赖于时间反向传播（BPTT），该方法受限于序列计算无法并行化，且存在梯度消失或爆炸问题，导致难以学习长距离依赖。因此，研究旨在寻找一种能绕过递归信用传播、支持并行训练且梯度稳定的 RNN 训练方法。

Method: 提出了监督记忆训练（Supervised Memory Training, SMT）方法。该方法将 RNN 训练转化为对一步记忆转移标签 (m_t, x_{t+1}) -> m_{t+1} 的监督学习，避免了通过时间反向传播（BPTT）。它利用基于 Transformer 的编码器训练预测状态目标，仅保留预测未来所需的过去信息，从而实现时间并行训练并保持 O(1) 的梯度路径长度。

Result: 在语言建模和像素序列建模等任务中，SMT 在预训练各种 RNN 架构时表现均优于传统的 BPTT 方法，且能显著提升模型捕捉长距离依赖的能力。

Conclusion: SMT 通过解耦“记忆内容”与“更新机制”，成功解决了传统 RNN 训练中的序列依赖和梯度问题，证明了非线性 RNN 在通过监督学习进行时间并行训练时，能够更有效地捕捉长距离依赖，从而为大规模时间序列建模提供了新路径。

Abstract: Training recurrent neural networks (RNNs) requires assigning credit across long sequences of computations. Standard backpropagation through time (BPTT) addresses this problem poorly: it is sequential in time, limiting parallelism, and suffers from vanishing or exploding gradients, making long-range associations difficult to learn. We propose Supervised Memory Training (SMT), a method for training nonlinear RNNs that sidesteps recurrent credit propagation entirely by reducing RNN training to supervised learning on one-step memory transition labels $(m_t, x_{t+1}) \rightarrow m_{t+1}$. SMT acquires these memory labels by training a Transformer-based encoder on a predictive state objective--retaining only information from the past necessary to predict the future. By decoupling what to remember from how to update memory, SMT enables time-parallel RNN training with a stable $O(1)$ length gradient path between any two tokens--without ever unrolling the RNN. We find that SMT outperforms BPTT when pretraining various RNN architectures on tasks like language modeling and pixel sequence modeling. SMT enables nonlinear RNNs to better capture long-range dependencies and train in parallel, potentially unlocking the scaling of models that build temporal abstractions of past experience.

### [344] [Regret Minimization with Adaptive Opponents in Repeated Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06486)
*Mingyang Liu,Asuman Ozdaglar,Tiancheng Yu,Kaiqing Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对重复博弈中对手的适应性问题，提出了“重复策略遗憾”（RP-Regret）指标。通过设计三种优化算法，该框架能够在非凸场景下有效学习，并帮助智能体在重复博弈中收敛到更高收益的子博弈完美均衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的在线学习指标（如外部遗憾）无法有效捕捉重复博弈中对手根据历史行为进行适应性反馈的特征，导致其难以在对抗性或合作性重复博弈中实现最优策略学习。因此，需要引入能够反映参与者反事实推理能力的新遗憾指标。

Method: 1. 引入“重复策略遗憾”（RP-Regret）作为衡量标准，考虑了对手对历史行为的适应性。
2. 分析了实现该遗憾次线性增长的必要条件（针对策略变化、记忆长度等）。
3. 设计了三种算法来解决非凸优化问题：基于优化预言机（Oracle）的算法、基于线性化替代目标的算法，以及针对慢变对手的直接最小化算法。

Result: 理论上证明了RP-Regret在特定条件下可实现次线性增长；提出的算法能够有效处理非凸优化挑战；实验表明，在如“猎鹿博弈”（Stag-Hunt）等经典博弈中，最小化RP-Regret能够引导智能体达成更具合作性且效用更高的均衡解。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的重复策略遗憾（RP-Regret）为重复博弈中的学习提供了一个更具博弈论基础的评估指标。通过最小化该遗憾，智能体不仅能适应对手，还能共同收敛到重复博弈的子博弈完美均衡（SPE），在合作博弈中表现出比传统外部遗憾最小化算法更好的效果。

Abstract: In this paper, we study regret minimization in repeated games with \emph{adaptive} opponents who can respond based on histories of play. The standard metric of \emph{external regret} in online learning is known to fail to capture such adaptivity. To account for players' counterfactual reasoning, we introduce {\tt Repeated Policy Regret (RP-Regret)}, a game-theoretic metric that measures the difference between the \emph{realized} and the \emph{best-in-hindsight} accumulated utility when all players can \emph{respond} to the history of play. Compared to existing regret notions in this setting, ours is native to repeated game playing, enabling stronger comparators and opponents with fewer constraints, while maintaining the possibility of finding better equilibria when all players minimize it. We first identify necessary conditions for obtaining {\tt RP-Regret} sublinear in time, on the variation of the player's comparator strategies in the regret definition and on the memories of both the comparator and opponents' strategies. We then study additional conditions and provable algorithms to minimize {\tt RP-Regret}, which is by definition \emph{non-convex} in the strategy space. To address this challenge, we propose three algorithms: (i) one based on an optimization oracle, as assumed in some prior work in online non-convex learning; (ii) one that minimizes a convex and \emph{linearized} surrogate of {\tt RP-Regret} at each iteration; (iii) one that directly minimizes {\tt RP-Regret} when opponents change strategies slowly. Furthermore, when all players can run algorithms to minimize the {\tt RP-Regret} (or its linearized variant), certain subgame perfect equilibria of the repeated game can be learned. We also provide experiments showing that minimizing our regret notions can lead to more cooperative solutions with higher utility in games such as Stag-Hunt.

</details>


### [345] [TailLoR: Protecting Principal Components in Parameter-Efficient Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06494)
*Marius Dragoi,Ioana Pintilie,Alexandra Dragomir,Antonio Barbalau,Florin Brad*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TailLoR 是一种持续学习的新方法，通过固定预训练权重的奇异向量并仅对长尾奇异值进行低秩更新，配合软谱惩罚机制，有效减轻了任务间的干扰，提升了微调效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在持续学习中，现有的参数高效微调方法往往会因干扰而导致灾难性遗忘，而现有的基于谱分解的方法未能充分利用预训练权重的结构信息来引导高效的适应。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TailLoR 的方法，利用预训练权重中固定的奇异向量矩阵 U 和 V 作为参考框架，仅对奇异值矩阵进行低秩更新；同时引入一种软谱惩罚机制，抑制对主导奇异方向的更新，从而减少任务间的干扰。

Result: 实验表明，TailLoR 通过将微调引导至具有高灵活性的长尾谱坐标，显著降低了任务间的干涉，并在持续学习任务中表现出优异的性能。

Conclusion: TailLoR 通过利用预训练权重的奇异值分解（SVD）固定基底并专注于微调长尾奇异值，为持续学习提供了一种高效且抗干扰的参数高效微调框架。

Abstract: Parameter-efficient finetuning methods based on spectral decomposition have enabled progress in Continual Learning. In this paper we introduce TailLoR, which utilizes the singular bases U and V of the pre-trained weights as a fixed reference frame to learn a low-rank update applied to the singular value matrix. A soft spectral penalty discourages updates aligned with dominant singular directions, reducing interference while routing fine-grained adaptation into the highly flexible, long-tail spectral coordinates.

</details>
